aman ur ufin ara ansa ara εeddin; kkrent tḥemmalin, ččuren izenqan, kkren iberdan mačči d ayen ara yejmeε wasif. Aman kecmen s ixxamen. Lɣaci mačči akken ṭṭsen i d‑ukin. Akken kan yezgen yiḍ imezdaɣ faqen‑d d twaɣit yeḍran yid‑sen, ffɣen‑d qeccuc meccuc ar izenqan, bdan berzen tiregwa akken ad d‑ɛeddin waman; ageffur yettcercur fell‑asen, iḍ kamel nutni d imenɣi d waman, aman ḥebsen ur teddun, simmal yettali uswir‑nsen.

Mi yuli wass, yeḥbes ugeffur, imezdaɣ, walan tawaɣit i asen‑yeḍran; taddart ibeddel udem, aluḍ yessa am usalu n udfel, iqerman d tseḍwa ččuren izenqan, kra n yixxamen ɣlin. Tulawin bdan ad jebdent aman yeqqimen sdaxel n yixxam. Dindin irgazen nnejmaεen, maca iɛedda uzger deg uẓeṭṭa, fehmen belli ɣelḍen aṭas imi ur rrin ara i teɣri d‑ggren yimɣaren n taddart aggur yezrin. Gzan tamsirt, dindin kkren ar lxedma n taddart uqbel ad d‑yuɣal ugeffur. Dduklen argaz, tameṭṭut d yilmeẓyen am yiwen, am wakken xedmen lejdud‑nsen zik.

# Taferdedduct

Asmi i tella yakan d taferddedect di tεebbuḍt n yemma‑s, teḥrec. Teḥrec tugar akk tiferdeddac nniḍen, asmi yuzzlent deg uzabuq yettawin ar waskiwen n yemma‑s, akken ad d‑taf abrid‑is ar dduḥ n tudert, ara d‑yeslalen rruḥ di tmellalt, ara yegmun di tculliḍt d‑ḥudden tecriḥin n uksum di laman yeččuren d aman yeḥman.

Zrin wagguren, tsell akk i uskerwec n ddunit. Sṣut n yemma‑s d baba‑s imi i as‑d‑ttḥewwisen isem. Tecfa ɣef ṣṣut‑nsen. Nettat tetturar di tagut n temḍellas n yal ass, tenwa ddunit akk d ayla‑s. Tettεummu deg waman yeḥman, imellḥen i tejmeε tculliḍt‑nni n tadist n yemma‑s. Tsell i wul n yemma‑s imi iḥebbek, iḥebbek wul‑ines ula d nettat yid‑s. Tettaḍsa waḥd‑es, tefreḥ, tennecreḥ.

Xas ma tsell‑asen, ur tezmir ara ad ttwali tafat n berra. Xas akken tedyeq tculliḍt‑nni urǧin txaq. Xas akken d ṭṭlam urǧin tuggad, allen‑is medlent, am wakken mmundlen. Tettneqlab, tekkat s yiḍarren‑is akked yifassen‑is, tḥar ad d‑teffeɣ si tculliḍt‑nni ar ddunit akken ad ttwali tafat, ad tejbed uzwu i turin‑ines.

Tettumɣur, tettuzur, mačči am wussan n yimenza, asmi tella annect n uεeqqa n yired, tura tuɣal annect n tfeqlujt, tedyeq fell‑as; iḍarren‑is d yifassen‑is ur tezmir ara ad tent‑sembiwel akken tebɣa. Tettnadi tawwurt ad d‑teffeɣ. Tettneqlab, tettnejbad alarmi yiwwas kan! teɣli‑d ar yirebbi n ddunit, tettru.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Qqaren wat zik, llan tikelt sin watmaten; yiwen isem‑is Meğğkan, wayeḍ isem‑is Mawidkan. Meğğkan d nneyya, ixeddem үef twacult meṛṛa. Ma d Mawidkan d bu tḥila, ittxemmim kan ɣef ttrika. Asmi yemmut babat‑sen, yeğğa‑d si yal lxir atmunen.

Meğğkan үur‑s tikti, yenna i gma‑s ahwawi: “ad yerḥem Ṛebbi babat‑neү lεali, ay aү‑d‑yeğğan akk aya‑gi. Deg‑neү tajmilt yuksan‑itt, ad as‑tt‑nerr ma tadrimt‑is nessefti‑tt”.

Ineggez Mawidkan s werrif yini i bu nnif: “Jmaεliman afus‑ik ur ten‑yesṛif. Wa d baba‑inu, ayla‑s inu, kečč ur telliḍ d gma‑inu”.

Meğğkan ibat seg wayen la isell, yugad idim ad yazzel, yeṭṭef abrid‑is iүawel, үer at Ṛebbi issuүel, ad as‑d‑ciren үef win ay as‑isswen aүbel. Deg ubrid‑is yemlal‑d win үer‑s Ṛebbi yuzen‑d. Iseqsa‑t d yimeṭṭi itturug‑d: “A kečč umi zeddig wudem am lmelk, talwit melmi ara yi‑d‑tettunefk? Ma mazal gma ad idder, tuүalin ur tt‑id‑bedder”.

Inṭeq umexluq yini‑as: “tlatin iseggasen ay d‑mazal‑as”. Tүad‑it twacult‑is n‑yeğğa i udeүli. Immuqel Meğğkan үer yigenni, yini: “Wekkleү‑ak a gma Ṛebbi”. Sakin үer uxxam yebda‑d tikli. Үer tewwurt temmuger‑it‑id tmeṭṭut‑is, seg’meṭṭi yejreḥ yeẓri‑s. “Melmi akk‑a ara ɣ‑ifak Ṛebbi si ẓẓur?” Ay t‑id‑tqubel s wudem ur inuṛ. “Sbeṛ kan, d aya ay aү‑d‑isaḥen d‑amur, tlatin iseggasen werεad bdin”.

S igenni terfed tmeṭṭut iẓri‑s ineggin: “Wekkleү‑ak Ṛebbi a win yeččan gma‑s d amuddir, nekkni neshel‑ak, Ṛebbi d uwεir”. Sakin үer tүerүert temmuger‑it‑id yelli‑s, umi tettel tyersi di tgerjumt‑is: “A baba, melmi ara fell‑aү d‑teflali?” Sbeṛ kan, a taεzizt‑iw a yell‑i, akk‑a tlatin iseggasen ur d‑icerreq ur tt‑nettwali”.

Үer yigenni terfed teqcict iẓri‑s ismeqqin: “Wekkleү‑ak Ṛebbi a εemmi ur yellin d aḥnin!”

Azekka‑nni kan isselqef Mawidkan. Tbat twacult n Meğğkan. “A εni skiddiben at Ṛebbi?” Ay yenna Meǧǧkan s ubati. Iṭṭef abrid үur‑sen akken ad ten‑isseqsi. Di ttnaṣfa n ubrid, yemmuger‑it‑id lmelk‑nni. “A mazal‑ik themmled ula d ass‑a? Yax kfan fell‑ak iүeblan tura!” Ay as‑yenna. “Usiү‑d akken ad iyi‑d‑tessefruḍ adrug‑ik. Yax tenniḍ tlatin iseggasen ay d‑yeggran, akken ad faken fell‑i yinẓman” Ay as‑yenna Meǧǧkan.

“Smuzget ihi mliḥ akken ad tfehmeḍ. Aql‑aken di twacult‑ik di tlata, yal ma yiwen deg‑wen iwekkel Ṛebbi i winna, nekẓen‑d εecra iseggasen dinna. Ṛebbi ur ittettu ara, win deg‑s issutren kra”, ay as‑tt‑id‑yessefra lmelk bu tussna.

Missaɛudi Ǧaɛfer

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Mi ara teffɣeḍ i taddart n yiflisen metwal agafa asamer, ad ak‑id‑tqabel taddart n Teqsebt am ufrag zdat n ugrakal. Iberdan ideg ara telḥuḍ meqqren, hrawen. Iberdan‑agi diɣ ideg ara tedduḍ mxalafen; llan kraḍ seg‑sen: Amezwaru i d‑yezgan di lǧiha n ufella, yettawi ɣar Texxamt n leɛlam; wis sin; ɣar Tizi n Temlelt ma d abrid wis kraḍ i d yezgan si tama n wadda, yessuffuɣ ɣar Taddart n At Yusef.

Taddart n Teqsebt tettwassen aṭas ladɣa s ṭrad i iɛeddan fell‑as. Asmi i tt‑kecmen Yifrensisen; xedmen aṭas n ttawilat dinna, am yibasanen n waman, bnan ixxamen, bɣan ad idir deg‑s acku tesɛa aṭas n tɣawsiwin yelhant: akal‑is, amkan ideg i d‑tezga, yerna twaɛa akk tudrin, yerna‑as yilel agrakal ccbaḥa.

Ɣar lǧiha n wadda n taddart, metwal asamer anẓul, tella yiwet tewrirt n udrar teččur d isekla ad as‑tiniḍ d tiẓgi, di tama n udrar‑agi ttidirent aṭas n twaculin, gar‑asent tella yiwet iwumi qqaren tawacult n Ɛemmi Meẓyan I yeǧǧan mmi‑s d tmeṭṭut‑is wḥed‑sen.

Tameṭṭut‑is qqaren‑as Cabḥa, ma d mmi‑s: Amnay, d aqcic n ccuq, d netta i d asirem, d netta id azekka n udrum, yis ara yidir yisem‑is, d netta i d amekkasu‑ines.

Amnay yesɛa semmus n yiseggasen di leɛmer‑is, tettban tafat ɣef wudem‑is, yettidir netta d yemma‑s ɣef wayen zerɛen deg iḥerqan d tmizar. Yesɛa tajlibt n wulli yesuffuɣ‑itt mkul taṣebḥit ɣar yiwen n umadaɣ iwumi qqaren amadaɣ n Farɛun.

Amnay mmi‑s n dda Meẓyan d aqcic uḥdiq yessen amek ara yehder ad as –tiniḍ d aḥeddad n wawal. Acebbub‑is d aberkan, lqed d alemmas d azuran, tiṭṭucin‑is d tiberkanin ad as‑tiniḍ d aɛeqqa n uzemmur, ṭurcent, ḥercent. Yesɛedday ussan‑is d wulli‑ines; si lexla ɣar uxxam, seg uxxam ɣar lexla. Yesɛa yiwet n teqjunt d taberkant am yiɣden d taweɛrant am times, isemma‑as FINETTE. Tezga tesqabaḥ, ur tettaǧa ara win ara d‑yezzin ɣar Umnay neɣ ɣar wulli‑ines.

Ma d yemma‑s Cabḥa tezga di tmazirt, tneqqec, tzerreɛ ama d aẓalim ama d ayen niḍen ara yiḥwiǧen. Akka i tettidir twacult n dda Meẓyan, xas akken ixuṣ netta, yeǧǧa‑d argaz deg umkan‑is.

Armi d Yiwen n wass Amnay yeffeɣ netta d wulli‑ines ɣar umadaɣ n Ferɛun iččuren d isekla d yimɣan imcubbaken wa deg wa, isekla‑nni myuṭṭafen wa ɣar wa amzun d imdanen mi ara myuṭṭafen deg yifassen.

Myekcamen wa deg wa, myurzen s yisuraz n tejgagalin d yigeḍman n yinijel: d tizantin, d azzu, yal aseklu ad t‑tafeḍ din. Segmi ara tkecmeḍ alama teffɣeḍ, ad tettedduḍ di tili, aḍu asemmaḍ ad yeslufu i wudem‑ik. Yuli s ufella n teblaḍt yeẓẓiẓin i yiṭij, icennu, ma d taqejjunt taweɛrant i izemren ad tekkes iẓerman n wumdan, tettawi kan aratu.

Amnay yeksa armi d tameddit, dɣa yebda usigna am waken yufrar‑d, aneznaz‑nni id‑yesmiqqiyen ad as‑tiniḍ iruḥ yewwi. Cwiṭ n tafukt la d‑tettali.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Cwiṭ kan akka bedden‑d ɣur‑s kra n yimdanen s yibidiyen, dɣa yuẓa‑d Yiwen seg‑sen ɣur‑s yenna‑as: Acḥal ara tsenzeḍ ikerri‑a inek?

‑ Xemsa dduru!

‑Ala ay aterras ɣlay, ha‑t‑an siwa iɣsan i yellan deg‑s ilaq as aɣ‑d‑teǧǧeḍ ciṭuḥ di ssuma‑s.

Amnay imuqel imdanen‑nni dɣa yeẓra belli s tḥerci i as‑id‑ruḥen mačči d lbiɛ i bɣan ad aɣen dɣa yerra‑asen: Arǧu ar d‑yuɣal baba ad ak‑id‑yini acḥal ara ak‑t‑yessenz.

‑D tikti yelhan maḍi! ad qqimeɣ dagi alama yuɣal‑d baba‑k.

‑Arǧu ma tebɣiḍ, yerna baba ad iɛeṭṭel aṭas.

Amnafeq imuqel imeddukal‑is, yettaḍṣa, yeẓra belli Amnay ur yesɛi ara baba‑s, netta d yemma‑s Cabḥa kan i yettidir. Imnufaq‑agi gemnen‑d i takerḍa n wulli‑agi n Umnay, ẓran ur yezmir d acu ara yexdem weḥd‑s.

‑Ah, ay amecṭṭuḥ ur iyi‑d‑tenniḍ ara isem‑ik? Tettbaneḍ d aqcic uḥric, yettban baba‑k iḥemmel‑ik aṭas.

‑Anda teẓriḍ kečč belli baba iḥemmel‑iyi?

‑Aha, ur iyi‑sefqaɛ ara tura ini‑yi‑d isem‑ik?

‑Amnay.

‑I baba‑k isem‑is? Anida yezdeɣ? ur t‑ssineɣ ara.

‑Ayɣer iyi‑d‑testeqsayeḍ, mi d‑yuɣal ad t‑twaliḍ. Yerna ɣas ur ttraǧu ara, acku ad iɛeṭṭel!

‑Ah ya lkareɛ, cukkeɣ limer ad ak‑fkeɣ kra n zzhuṭ ad teẓreḍ amek tleɛbeḍ yis‑naɣ.

Yekker‑d yiwen seg‑sen yeṭṭef‑it‑id seg umeẓẓuɣ dɣa yenna‑as:

‑Tleɛbeḍ kečč yis‑naɣ? tɣileḍ tḥerceḍ?

‑Ayɣer? d acu i xedmeɣ? d tidet id‑niɣ.

‑Waqila mazal ur aɣ‑tessineḍ ara, mazal teqqur tqerruyt‑ik, lɛeb kkan mliḥ ad d‑lhiɣ yid‑k.

Imettukar rran abrid n wadda ma d Amnay teṭṭef‑it tergagayt, iɣawel yekker fell‑as yejmeɛ ulli ad iruḥ s axxam. Iteddu armi yewweḍ ɣar tlemmast n teẓgi, netta yella yuggad mačči d izli, la ihedder d yiman‑is; “lukan ad d‑uɣalen ɣur‑i d acu ara xedmaɣ? Amek ara rewlaɣ? neɣ yezmar lḥal ad ikksen ulli‑inu? s wayes ara ten‑qablaɣ?”

Iteddu, iteddu armi i as‑id‑ffɣen kan deg yiwen n udernu dɣa nnan‑as: “Waqila tferḥeḍ, tɣileḍ ad tsensreḍ seg yifassen‑nneɣ?”

Amnay ibedd, iqqur seg llxuf mi as‑id‑ffɣen, ffɣen‑t yidamen, yuɣal d awraɣ yeɛweq sani ara yerr.

‑Teẓriḍ ma teddiḍ di rray‑iw ɣas muddaɣ‑d ulli‑agi inek mebla awal.

‑D lmuḥal, acku ma yeẓra baba terwi.

‑Ah ya ibekki mazal tettɛawadeḍ‑d i wawal‑agi, ẓriɣ belli ur tesɛiḍ ara baba‑k>

Yekker umakar‑nni, yeṭṭef‑it‑id seg yifassen netta la yettru, la yettiẓẓif:

‑Serreḥ‑iyi! serreḥ‑iyi.

‑Nniɣ‑ak susem acku ma teddiḍ s usuɣu‑agi inek ad tedduḍ ula d keččinni.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Amnay mazal‑it yettsuɣu, ijebbed, ma d ssin‑nni niḍen n yimakaren zzin‑asen i wulli‑nni, jemɛen‑tent d taremmuɛt, nehren‑tent ɣar ubrid n wadda, syin ara tent‑sɛeddin. Ma d Amnay wwin‑t yid‑sen, acku ẓran ma ǧǧan‑t, ad iruḥ ɣar wat n Taddart ad as asen‑yini, yerna tura yessen‑iten mliḥ amek gan. Amakar yezwar‑it zzdat‑s ma d Amnay yeɛweq, yuggad ma yella d acu ara as‑xedmen ula d netta.

Imakaren‑nni wwin Amnay d wulli ines, gezmen yiwen n ubrid d udyiq di tlemmast n teẓgi, iččuren d iblaḍen, d asawen, ineḍ, igzem‑it iɣzer. Mi telḥiḍ azal n kradet n timar ad tefɣeḍ akkin i ubrid‑agi, ad tafeḍ yiwen n utmu d aqdim yettwabna s iqcuḍun d yiḥelyiwen mkul wa yesned ɣar wa. Isekla d yimɣan mcubbaken wa deg wa ulac d acu ara t‑waliḍ iɣum akk ur d‑yettban ara maḍi. Rran Amnay ɣar daxel ṣekkren tawwurt ɣar berra, netta mazal yettiẓẓif maca ulac win ara as‑id yeslen.

Yeqqim yiwen seg‑sen di berra iɛus‑it ma d ulli‑nni fkan‑tent i yiwen n umeksa ad tent‑yeks. Nna Cabḥa terǧa, terǧa twala Amnay iɛeṭtel aṭas mačči d leɛwayed‑is ad iɛeṭṭel amek akken iɛeṭṭel ass‑nni dɣa tenna deg wul‑is: “Awwah! yettban yella d acu yeḍran yid‑s! Ahat ukren‑t neɣ yeɣli deg ubrid maḍi !”

Nna Cabḥa terǧa, terǧa ulac teɛweq amek ara texdem dɣa tessawel i yiwen n lǧiran‑is tules‑as tadyant dɣa wina ijemmeɛ‑d at Taddart ruḥen ad d‑nadin ɣef Umnay d wulli‑ines. Ma di Taddart tekker tin imawlan ɣef uqcic amek ur d‑yuɣal ara s axxam am wussan iɛeddan. Ma d Nna Cabḥa tewwet‑itt tmaggart teqqur ur tezmir d acu ara texdem, tdeɛɛu kkan ɣar sidi Rebbi iwakken ulac d acu ara yaɣen mmi‑s.

At Taddart rran srid ɣar teẓgi dɣa bdan la ttwalin sani yerra, iluɛa‑ten‑id yiwen seg‑sen yenna‑asen‑id: “Lukan mkul tarbaɛt ad tetbeɛ yiwen n ubrid ahat ad d‑naf later‑is, yerna tiẓgi tmeqqer, tuɣ aṭas, ilaq ad nɣiwel cwiṭ acku qrib ad d‑yeɣli ṭṭlam, ur nettezmir ara ad nekkmel anadi fell‑as.”

Xedmen yirgazen akken i asen‑id‑yenna wina, mkul tarbaɛt teḍfer yiwen n ubrid, ma d tarbaɛt‑nni yuɣen abrid‑nni i yewwin yimakaren n Umnay, teddun, teddun armi slan i yiwen lḥes, qarben xmaṭ xmaṭ dɣa walan yiwen n urgaz zdat tewwurt n yiwen n utmu la yettawi yettara, am akken yella d acu i as‑iruḥen, yetqelleq.

Yenṭeq‑d yiwen gar‑asen: “Awwah amexluq‑agi ibedden dagi iɛusen atmu‑agi yettban yella d acu yellan, walim! yegguma ad yeṭṭef iman‑is.”

Yerra‑as‑id wayeḍ: “Tesɛiḍ elḥaq ayameddakel.”

Urɛad yekfa awal armi d‑yewweḍ kan wayeḍ ɣer‑s yettazal‑d yettiẓif:

- ‑Azel, azel a ɣiles d twaɣit teẓriḍ.
- ‑Dacu i k‑yuɣen, d acu yeḍran akka, hḍer.
- ‑Ɣiwel ad nawi lkareɛin‑a amecṭuḥ atan ttḥewissen fell‑as, atan tiẓgi tedwer‑as‑id yiwet n tarbaɛt. Akken kan slan i wayen i d‑yules umakar‑nni ɣiwlen ẓedmen fell‑asen dewren‑d akk i utmu, ṭṭfen‑ten, cudden‑asen iffassen‑nsen ɣar deffir. Amnay yettiẓif‑d s daxel, sufɣen‑t‑id ččuren‑t‑d wallen‑is d imeṭṭawen, yebda la yettru yegumma ad ifak nhiq, wwin‑t‑id ruḥen‑d s axxam.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Akken kan i t‑wala yemma‑s, tneggez, yeffeɣ‑itt waṭṭan imi twala mmi‑s yuɣal‑d ɣur‑s.

‑Tuɣaleḍ‑d a mmi ɛzizen sani terriḍ akka, ayɣer tɛeṭṭleḍ akka, yella win ik‑yukren ɛenni?

‑Ala a yemma ulac d acu iyi‑yuɣun lameɛna ulli‑nni inu ruḥent, ukren‑tent, suref‑iyi di leɛnayam a yemma.

Ineṭṭeq‑d yiwen gar yirgazen‑nni yenna‑as‑id:

‑Ulli inek ad d‑uɣalent ɣur‑k ayuḥric, nekkni aqlaɣ da, ur ttxemmim ara.

‑Lḥemdulleh a Rebbi imi ulac d acu ikyuɣen, qqiment wulli‑nni mačči d aɣbel.

Aqcic yuɣal‑d ɣar yemma‑s s lemɛiwna d tirugza n yergazen yesɛan nnif d tebɣest. Amnay d yemmas‑s farḥen aṭas imi taddart tebna ɣef nnif d trugza n yimdanen‑is.

Akka dɣa i ass‑yenna ferhat imaziɣen imula:

# Taddart n leqbayel¹

# D afzim ɣef twenza n udrar

# Trennu‑yas di leɛnaya

tessaweḍ alammi i as‑d‑tezzi s umrar terfed‑it am yirin n tuga tezger‑d leqrun adfel d uɣurar teṭṭef zdat waṭṭan d lgirra xas akked d laẓ tennum tetturar

taddart n leqbayel yiwen ur tt‑yecba tebna ɣef lsas n tlelli yal taddart weḥd‑s d tagduda akka i tt‑id‑nufa iḍelli I aɣ‑tt‑ǧǧan imezwura

tezḍa tagmat tzeṭṭ tadukli ger warraw‑is leqdar d lḥerma nettat I ten‑yesɛan ur tɣelli s tejmeɛt i ferrun tilufa s tejmeɛt i ferrun tilufa

BOUALIT Assiya

1 Ferhat Imaziɣen Imula: Taddart N Leqbayel.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Kuruna

Tiẓimḍelt‑a n kuruna, teǧǧa‑d arjujen deg yimezdaɣ n umaḍal. Anfafad‑a, ur t‑iẓerr yiwen s tiṭ‑anagar ma iwala‑t umejjay s umikruskup, ixdem ur yexdim umger deg yiger, yenɣa ur yenɣi Rrus d Tṭurk deg Yikurdiyen deg Surya. Win ur t‑tḥuza ara di tfekka, tḥuza allaɣ‑is. Uɣalen medden ttweswisen, yal wa, tal ta, tettcakkat deg yiman‑is tuden. Ur tferren, ut tsemgirrid gar yimdanen, d aserti, d anesbaɣur, d amejjay… win i tmugger deg ubrid‑is, tuwi‑t. Tugar aqjun amessuḍ, tugar izem yuggsen, tugar aneḍlib ameslub iddeɣlen, iẓẓaren medden akk d icenga, ira ad d‑yerr ttar deg‑sen. Ɣef waya i d‑ssawalen yimassanen n tezmert akken ad as‑neddari, s ukman deg uxxam ar ttɛeddi. Amzun akken, send ad yerzu ɣer kra n tmurt, yeɣra‑tt mliḥ, iga‑d aɣawas ara yeḍfer. Yeḥsa belli anagar imejjayen ara t‑id‑iqarɛen dɣa yezwar seg‑sen, yekkes‑iten. maca … Akken i as‑yenna Maɛtub: «Ɣas neqqḍen acḥal d itri, igenni, ur inegger ara . »

Ɣas akka, kurunaḥ‑agi lɛar, isken‑d leɛyub n yimdanen d yiwanaken. Ass‑a imdanen akk ssiriden akken iwata, ssizdigen ixxamen‑nsen, tiɣawsiwin‑nsen, izerwan‑nsen … Ziɣen tezdeg tla azal, macči d awal kan maca ilaq usnas ines deg tudert‑nneɣ n yal ass. Aswir n tujja yuder nezzeh deg waṭas n tmura, gar‑asent tamurt‑nneɣ, ur tesɛi sbitarat, ur tesɛi ttawilat swayes ara tqabel tagnit‑a n lḥers.

Leɛyub n tmurt‑nneɣ mačči kan deg taɣult‑a n tujjya d tdawsa, s umata, maca ttbinen‑d deg yal aḥric, deg tsertit‑is taserdasant. Deg lawan anda tiliẓriwin n umaḍal ɛerrḍent‑d imejjayen ad d‑segzun aṭṭan‑a, ad wellhen imezdaɣ, ad d‑rren asirem i yimdanen tezdeɣ tegdi; ttawin‑d iɣellaten d yikataren n temhaddit (les militaires)! Ɣilen Kuruna‑agi, d igen n yiremmaqen (terroristes) ad t‑ḥarben s umrig d yiserdasen‑nsen! Ma akka i t‑ttwalin, ad ffɣen ihi ad as‑gen aḥaqaf neɣ tiseɣliyin (barrages) ad t‑id‑ṭṭfen. Ur yelli d ccɣel‑nsen. Di lawan, imdanen ɣellin am yizan, nutni ttgen adellel s uneqneq i yisufar n wucci i d‑tefka twacult n Gaid Saleh, d tawsa …

Ɣas ɣunzaɣ‑tt, tger assaɣen n tensetla d twizi lid gar tmura, lid gar yimdanen, xersum s wawal kan i usebɣes. Kurunaḥ, tbeddel anamek n kra n tenfaliyin d tmiḍranin am: asaḍuf n unezmar (win iǧehden) «…iselman: ameqqran yečča amecḥuḥ», sin rnan (ɣelben) yiwen. »

« Asaḍuf n tigti d tdersi » … Aql‑aɣ nwala abirus d ameẓẓyan maḍi maḍi, ur t‑nẓerr anagar s umkriskup, yezmer ad isenger ṭṭayfa, ur ken‑ɛniɣ!

Ad beddlent tnummiwin d tmuɣliwin n yimdanen. Argaz, mebla ccekk, iḥulfa s wayen yettaɣen tameṭṭut ihejben deg uxxam; d lawan ad as‑yerr tilelli‑ines. Yessefk ad tili tagda gar urgaz d tmetṭut, ulac win ara d‑yekken nnig tayeḍ. Sya d afella, ilaq ad nettarra akk aɛjar. Ziɣen lhiǧab yelha, lid i tmeṭṭut, lid i urgaz, yettarra anfafad ur yettaweḍ ara ɣer yimi d wanzaren, syin ɣer taɣect d turin. Mačči d aqerruy i d‑yuwi ad ihjeb yiwen, lḥiǧab‑nni i ttarrant tlawin ɣef yicebbuben‑nsent, ur yuwi, ur yerri.

D tamentilt i ufares deg taɣulin yemgaraden. Aṭas n usmax ay yuzzlen, ara yazzlen. Ineɣmisen, ineggalen, imassanen, uran u mazal ad aun fell‑as; imedyazen ssefran u mazal ad ssefrun fell‑as, icennayen, inaẓuren n teklut d umezgun akked sinima … ad yili d asentel ɣef ara gen ifuras‑nsen deg wussan i d‑iteddun … Ula d nekki seg lbeɛǧ i yi‑d‑yeffɣen seg ubrak‑

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
agi deg uxxam , uɣaleɣ shetrifeɣ , sxerwiḍeɣ , sfelsifeɣ … Ah ! Iḥeqqa win yesfelsifen qqaren‑as afiluẓuf . Ay a yemma , ziɣen nekk d afiluẓuf , ur faqeɣ !

Inaɛ ddin n tfamilt‑im a Kuruna i yi‑irran d afiluẓuf . Terwi‑yi allaɣ‑iw , ur yi‑teǧǧi acemma ; kan akka i ttawiɣ tamettant gar wallen‑iw am yihiqel . D tikkelt tamezwarut i fkiɣ azal i tfekka‑w . Dduqquseɣ , ttiliheɣ , ttḥulfuɣ s kra yemwawlen deg‑i , sdaxel neɣ sufell ; ula d anẓad deg ucekkuḥ‑iw , ma iḥerrek , ad ṭṭucneɣ , ad as‑iniɣ waqila d winna i d‑yersen fell‑i . Yal ass , ad ssucfeɣ , ad seṭṭleɣ tamart . Zriɣ win yemmuten s waṭtan‑a, ur t‑ssiriden ara , meqqar ma mmuteɣ ad ruheɣ d azedgan , d amezdudgan .

Teḍra‑yi am win yesɛeddan tanafa , gneɣ urgaɣ am wakken lliɣ zik d argaz bu‑tissas , ttmeslayeɣ d yiman‑iw , nniɣ‑as :  «  Amek  akka  tura  ,  yiwen  urgaz  am  nekki  ad  heddren medden fell‑i , ad as‑qqaren « Yettaggad amikrub ?» Giɣ‑d ciṭuh n tebɣest . Friɣ‑tt d rray‑iw : « lmut , tettalas‑aɣ yiwen wass ;d acu kan , jmaliman ur mmuteɣ s kuruna » Ihi ,ɛezleɣ iman‑iw deg yiwet n texxamt , ur tteffɣeɣ , ur tetteɣ , ur ttesseɣ .

Deg  uxxam  ,  ttqelqen  fell‑i , sṭebtuben‑d deg tewwurt , ugiɣ asen‑tt‑ldiɣ ; Tameṭṭut‑iw , tesrusuy‑yi‑d tagella ɣef umnar , maca ɛedleɣ nnif , ugiɣ ad ččeɣ .

Nekk yellan d afiluẓuf yerna ɣriɣ amezruy, rzant‑d ɣer wallaɣ‑iw snat n tedyanin i yi‑d‑yefkan tabɣest . Tamezwarut , d Yugurten i gren Rruman ɣer usekraf , yeqqim din alarmi yemmut s laẓ ; tis snat , d aɣyul‑nni i ifelsfen akken , yemmut . Nniɣ‑as : Yugurten meqqar ma yemmut s laẓ , yemmut d asaḍ ɣef tmurt‑is ; i ma mmuteɣ am uɣyul‑a yeǧǧan iman‑is i laẓ , acu n yiseɣ ara sɛuɣ ?

Ad ruḥeɣ ad d‑nndekwaleɣ , ad d‑ffɣeɣ seg yir targit‑nni , ad d‑afeɣ iman‑iw zedreɣ deg tayeḍ . Rwiɣ ajafejef ! Am wakken d Ṭaher Ǧawut i d‑ibedden zdat‑i , yenna‑yi‑d : « Ma tkemneḍ , ad temmteḍ ; ma teffɣeḍ , ad temmteḍ ; ihi , ffeɣ , ma teddreḍ d lɛali , ma temmuteḍ , mačči d kečč i d amezwaru neɣ i d aneggaru , tamettant ɣef medden irkelli ! »

Yenna‑yi‑d kan akka , yennerfaɛ , ur d‑iban ara ; ha‑t‑a yusa‑d Kuruna s timmad‑is , ur t‑friẓeɣ d awtem neɣ d tawtemt , yettmeslay‑yi‑d s tcinwat , gziɣ d acu i yi‑d‑yeqqar , yenna : « Ayɣer i theddreḍ fell‑i ?

Rriɣ‑as : Amek ur ihedder ara yiwen fell‑ak, kečči txedmeḍ ahdum deg talsa !

Yenna‑yi‑d  :  Tura  mi  d‑rziɣ nekki i tessnem talsa ! Acuɣer ur asen‑tettrum  ara  anezgum  i yimdanen i ken‑icuban , yettmettaten akken d igiman si laẓ , yal ass ?

Rriɣ‑as : Aql‑aɣ ula d nekni d igellilen ! Ɣas akken , ur neǧǧi ara win yelluẓen deg taddart , win i aɣ‑d‑yessutren kra nefka‑as‑t .

Yenna‑yi‑d : Ur ttmeslay ara s usget , mmeslay‑d ɣef leɛmer‑ik .

Rriɣ‑as : Amek i tebɣiḍ ad awseɣ yiwen , nekk anagar i ttaɣeɣ 4 duru , ur d‑ittezzi ara wayyur , dayen fukken ; ma ur d‑rḍileɣ ara , ur ttidireɣ ara !

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Yenna‑yi‑d: I widak‑nni i d‑yesnulfuyen lgirrat neqqen imdanen i ken‑yecban, d acu i txedmem i wakken ad kfun ccwalat, ad tekfu tazzla n yidammen deg‑wen?

Rriɣ‑as: Ur neɛdil ara, widak d imdanen n udabu, sɛan tazmert n tmenɣiwt am kečč. neqqen wid i asen‑yehwan, mi asen‑yehwa! Newwet‑d seg‑sen, maca ugin ad aɣ‑d‑slen. Nekni d imdanen iḥerfiyen, nra ad yili usrad deg umaḍal iwakken ad tidir talsa di talwit.

Yenna‑yi‑d: Tessawḍeḍ almi i yi‑d‑tregmeḍ; xuḍi kečči, ur telliḍ ara deg leḥsab n widak ara kkseɣ si ddunit!

Uggadeɣ ad yendem, ad iyi‑yernu ɣer wumuɣ‑nni, rriɣ‑as‑d s usqewqew: « Ma tuwiḍ akk widak ssneɣ d wid ḥemmleɣ, ma ggriɣ‑d weḥd‑i, i wumi‑yi? »

Mi lliɣ ttmeslayeɣ yid‑s, yuwi‑yi‑d Rebbi ssut n Maɛtub, icennu:

« Si ddunit akk ad neffeɣ, D acu ara nawi yid‑neɣ? Siwa tardast n lekfen Markan deg‑s lefɛayel‑nneɣ! »

Kemneɣ, kemneɣ, ur yi‑yuwi ara ukmin; ḍaqeɣ! Taswiɛt kan, tesduqes‑iyi‑d tuddna n ccix, sliɣ i rrhi deg berra; slafayeɣ i wudem‑iw ad ẓreɣ ma deg ddunit i lliɣ neɣ mmuteɣ! Ziɣen rrhi‑nni, d amɣafer i ttemɣafaren medden; d lɛid ameẓẓyan.

Kkreɣ‑d, ssardeɣ, lsiɣ talaba‑inu tamaynutt, ruḥeɣ srid ɣer uletma ad tt‑id‑ɣafreɣ, kraḍ n wayyuren‑aya ur tt‑ẓriɣ. Dayen tekfa ccedda, yuɣal‑d uzmummeg ɣer wudmawen... Tudert tettkemmil

Madani Afia.

Tagi, d tukkist seg udris i d‑uriɣ tura kan ɣef waṭṭan‑a n kuruna

Tiẓimḍelt: pandémie

Rrhi: llḥess, ssut n lɣaci

Acekkuḥ: acebbub

Meqqar: alors, donc

Ad awseɣ: ad ɛiwneɣ

Yemwawel: yembawel

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Tuɣalin

Yeṭṭef‑iyi lehlak n lberd di Fransa, idmaren‑iw sewwen akk ɣer daxel, zgiɣ d asguḥu, tudert‑iw tcud ɣer tɛeqqacin‑nni n ddwa yi‑d‑yettak ṭbib. Yerna‑d waṭṭan n rrumatiz, iḍarren‑iw zgan ttqeddiren, uɣalen ur zmiren ara i tfekka‑w. Akka, aṭas i lḥan, tura ula d nutni ɛyan, ur zmireɣ ara ad beddeɣ aṭas amer ad ɣliɣ. Xas ini tazmert‑iw akk la tesgermud, truz sseḥḥa‑w, dayen teǧǧa‑yaɣ tezmer.

yerna‑yi leḥbis di txxamt. Ttɣimaɣ aṭas ur ttefɣeɣ ara. Ur ufiɣ yiwen d tama‑w, ad yi‑d‑yefk xas d afenǧal n tizana. Ur as‑ḥebbreɣ i tewser mm leɛyub, teɣli‑d s lemxatla, akken i d‑yeɣli yiḍ ɣef wass. Imezwura‑nneɣ mi i d‑ttaǧǧan lemtul, qqaren txeddm temẓi ɣef temɣer; yal wa yemmuger‑it‑id mmi‑s nneɣ yelli‑s, ad t‑yaf ɣer leɛquba‑s ad t‑yerfed.

Nekk deg wasmi i d‑kkreɣ rriɣ‑tt i jjiḥ, fkiɣ rray i tqerruyt, iɣileɣ ad yi‑tdum temẓi d sseḥḥa. Tura mi i d‑tesṭebṭeb tweser, la ttxelliṣeɣ, tufa‑d ifadden kkawen. kra d Rebbi kra d rray‑iw, ass‑a ggriɣ‑d am yitbir‑nni amerẓu ɣef i guǧen yimawlan. Ulac win ara d‑yerzun fell‑i, la aḥbib la wali, ḥala kečč a Sidi Rebbi.

Di txxamt n lɣerba weḥd‑i. Lukan ad d‑tas mm lḥeqq ad aɣ‑tawi, ur ttfaqen yis‑i alama tekfa‑yi tweka. Ad d‑iniɣ sseḥ, yettḍiqi lxater‑iw, yettfuḥ yimi‑w. Ttewḥid di Sidi Rebbi, d wamek iyi‑tkkelx yis‑s ddunit.

Yella yiwen n uqcic d atunsi, yezdeɣ nnig‑i. Isem‑is Yazid ttɣaḍeɣ‑t meskin. Mi qqimeɣ aṭas ur ffiɣeɣ ara, ad d‑yerzu felli. Maca meskin ur yettstaf ara ixeddem deg yiḍ deg uzal iggan. Nekk tineggura‑ya, xas ini inɛed ur tteffɣeɣ ara; ccetwa kamel sɛeddayeɣ‑tt deg wusu.

Aql‑i ɛeddaɣ‑d 70, qrib ad leḥqeɣ 80. Aggad ixedmen leqrar i yiman‑nsen, diminajin, uɣalen akk ɣer tmurt, ufan tameṭṭut tqubel‑iten‑id d dderya‑nsen meqqrit. Ḥala nekk i d‑yeqqimen tura d awḥid, ur giɣ leqrar, ad mmteɣ d aɣrib aḥlili. Ula d aẓekka ur t‑kettbeɣ di tmeqbert n taddart‑iw, gar yimawlan.

Yebda yetteffeɣ lḥal deg waggur n maggu, ara d‑yuɣalen di lxir, nniɣ‑as ass‑agi, ay ɛziz a Sidi Rebbi, ad kkreɣ ad lḥuɣ cwiṭ, ad kkseɣ ɣef wul yemɣumbasen, acḥal aya yuli‑t lɣim. Ad yefsi wadif isebken deg yiɣsan, ad waliɣ xas s wallen‑iw, ad d‑yekkes cwiṭ n lxiq.

Kkreɣ lsiɣ amunṭu‑yinu aberkan, rriɣ akacyal ɣef umgerḍ‑iw, ɣumeɣ iman‑iw ɣef usemmiḍ, caddeɣ isebbaḍen‑iw, kkreɣ meckukleɣ acemma ɣer berra. Leḥḥuɣ s dderdifeɣ. Ɛeddaɣ‑d deg ubrid‑iw ɣef kra n yimukan, asmi lliɣ meẓẓiyeɣ ttawiɣ abrid s leḥmeq; tura imi tagecrirt teḥfa, afud‑iw yeɛya, yal mi lḥiɣ aqeddim ad steɛfuɣ.

Ru ay ixef‑iw ma ad truḍ ɣef seḥḥa taɛzizt i aɣ‑yeǧǧan! Uliɣ ɣef tqenṭert n Lasan di temdint n paris, ifassen‑iw ṭṭfen deg yicebbaken, ttmuquleɣ ɣer wasif n Lasan, aman ttazzalen, meɛna tignawt ur teṣfi ara mliḥ, mazal semmeḍ lḥal. Uggadeɣ asemmiḍ, nniɣ‑as ad uɣaleɣ alama d taxxamt. Maca mekteɣt ṭṭiq‑nni aberkan texxamt. Mi kkreɣ ad ruḥeɣ, iɛjeb‑iyi lḥal, nniɣ‑as ad rnuɣ cwiṭ, taxxamt ur tfat ara.

Ɣer din ukiɣ‑d, ufiɣ‑d iman‑iw sufella n umeṭreḥ di sbiṭar, lexyuḍ deg wanzaren‑iw, wayeḍ deg ufus azelmaḍ. Taqerɛet n sirum tɛelleq ar yidis‑iw, tamacint la tẓenẓun nnig uqerruy‑iw la tḥesseb deqqat n wul‑iw. Tettlaɛi‑yi‑d tefremlit. Ziɣen ɣliɣ deg ubrid, nekk ur faqeɣ, iwin‑iyi ɣer sbiṭar ur ẓriɣ, qqimeɣ ass kamel ur d‑ukiɣ almi d tameddit i d‑dkewleɣ.

Yenna‑yi ṭṭbib:

Yeṭṭef‑ik teqlaq d lungwaṣ, yelha‑yak mliḥ lukan ad tuɣaleḍ ar tmurt‑ik, d lɛali‑t ubeḥri n tmurt i sseḥḥa n bnadem...

Nniɣ‑as deg wul‑iw ahat d abeḥri n tmurt i yi‑d‑isawlen tikkelt‑a, waqila ad uɣaleɣ, xas ad gnneɣ di lǧameɛ, ad ddariɣ tujwirt, win tufiḍ ad yi‑yefk tin n Rebbi am ubungif‑nni n taddart n wasmi meẓẓiyeɣ...

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Qqimeɣ kra n wussan di sbiṭar, la aḥbib la wali, ḥala kečč a Sidi Rebbi. Ad beddeɣ ɣer ṭṭaq, ad waliɣ lɣaci leḥḥun, zehhun, ttaḍṣan, nekk ar daxel qebreɣ. Iruḥ‑n yiwen n wass Yazid, iɛedda ɣer ṭṭbib, isteqsa‑t melmi ara ffɣeɣ, yufa akken ar wass n ttlata, ay aɛziz a Rebbi.

Ass‑nni n ttlata iseḥḥebs‑d aṭaksi deg tewwurt n sbiṭer. Ffɣeɣ‑d, uɣaleɣ‑d ɣer texxamt, am yal ass. Yenna‑yi‑d ayen teḥwajeḍ, a baba, ini‑yi‑d. Aql‑i da...Yekker iruḥ, nekk qqimeɣ ttxemmimeɣ gar‑i d yiman‑iw i lehdur‑nni n ṭṭbib. Lukan ad uɣaleɣ ɣer tmurt, wissen amek ara afeɣ taswiɛt, tizɣwa n baba tura ahat ɣlint. Meɛna axir‑iyi ad ddariɣ tujwirt n taddart‑nneɣ, wala tin n Fransa. Yazid yal tameddit uqbel ad iruḥ ɣer lxedma, ad d‑yerzu fell‑i, ma ulac acu i yi‑ixussen. Ad t‑iḥrez Rebbi ! Ula d netta meskin ur yesɛi ara baba‑s. Ḥala yemma‑s d yiwet n uletma‑s i yesɛa, d netta i ixeddmen ɣef uxxam‑nsen. Yettwali‑yi deg umur n baba‑s, ad t‑yerḥem Rebbi, terẓeq‑as lǧennet u rreḥman ! Ɛeddan kra n wussan, nniɣ‑as ; a Yazid a mmi, ar melmi ara qqimeɣ akka ? Ṭṭef‑iyi lbeyyi ad diminajiɣ, ad uɣaleɣ ar tmurt n yimawlan. Ẓriɣ at taddart‑iw ur yi‑ttaǧǧan ara.

Yal ass d tazzla, yeṭṭef‑iyi‑d lbeyyi i wass n lexmis, ay aɛziz a Rebbi, ɣef 11:30 n ṣṣbeḥ , ar wass‑nni n lexmis ṣṣbeḥ, refdeɣ‑d tabalizt‑iw, lsiɣ lqecc‑iw, ffɣeɣ di texxamt‑nni taberkan n lɣerba, nniɣ‑as : “Bqa ɛla xir a lɣerba mm leɣrur. Ufan ttemɣer i d‑izegren ɣef temẓi , yili mačči akka ad teḍru yid‑i.”

Rekbeɣ aṭaksi, ɣef 11:00 lliɣ di Orly. Nedhen‑d i wid ara irekben i rruplan n 11:30 ar lezzayer, ad d‑heggin iman‑nsen. Ṭṭfeɣ amkan‑iw tabankiḍt tis tlata ɣer ljiha tazelmaḍt d tama n ṭṭaq, tesrafeg yis‑i ɣer tamurt‑iw ɛzizen, tin ǧǧiɣ acḥal d aseggas.

Aql‑i rseɣ di layrupur, tablizt gar yifassen‑iw. Ṭṭfeɣ aṭaksi ɣer taddart‑iw ǧǧiɣ qrib 50 d aseggas. Ffɣeɣ‑tt d amecṭuḥ urɛad lḥiqeɣ 20, uɣaleɣ‑d d amɣar ɛeddaɣ 70, qrib 80. Kra yekka ubrid, nekk ḥekkuɣ‑as‑d tajrirt‑iw i ucifur‑nni. Nniɣ‑as amnedra amek ara afeɣ taswiɛt ! wissen ma yella wanda ara nseɣ tameddit‑a, nneɣ akken yeqqar lemtel‑nni n taɛrabt “ ṭaḥ llil win nbatu”. Yeggul deg‑i ad dduɣ s axxam‑is ad nseɣ. Yenna‑yi ḥala nekk d temɣart n yemma i ttɛiciɣ, ad tedduḍ ad tenseḍ, azekka ṣṣbeḥ Rebbi yefteḥ, d nekk ara k‑yessiwḍen ɣer taddart‑ik, ur ttaggad ara. Nleḥq‑d sɣur lmeɣreb, nerra s axxam‑is. Ččiɣ imensi, swiɣ, yessa‑yi‑d nsiɣ.

Azekka‑nni tanzayt, yessaweḍ‑iyi‑d ɣer taddart. Leḥqeɣ‑d lewhi n ṭṭhur, rseɣ‑d berra n taddart. Nekkni nezdeɣ di leɛzib, weḥed‑nneɣ, ɣer nnig‑nneɣ d taddart. Ttedduɣ txemmimeɣ, ttmeslayeɣ gar‑i d yiman‑iw amek ara afaɣ tagnit. Kemmleɣ abrid almi d lḥara‑nneɣ, ufiɣ‑tt yul‑itt unajjel, yemɣi deg‑s yidmim. Zik teḥjeb s yiɣulad d yireccaqen, tura yal lec yeɣli. Teqqim akk tudert tebǧeḥ, ḥala yiwet n tzeqqa i yi‑iḍehren tselk acemma. Amek ara xedmeɣ ? Anda lembat‑iw? Ufiɣ tamazirt n baba, zik d tawesɛant, s ṭṭelq n wallen, tura yebḍa‑tt Urumi ɣef sin, yesɛedda deg‑s abrid n ukeṛṛus ; lǧiha nnig ubrid, tayeḍ ddaw ubrid. Tizemmrin ulac win i ten‑ixedmen ; ta terɣa, ta teqqur, ta teɣli. Qqimeɣ ɣef tecruft, ruḥen‑iyi‑d yimeṭṭawen. Ɣer din sliɣ i ddkeṛ n unerḥum, yella win yemmuten, babben‑t‑id deg usenduq ɣer tmeqbart. Ad ɛeddin sya, deg ubrid‑a, rrif n tmazirt.

Qqareɣ‑as deg wul‑iw wissen wi akka yemmuten. Si mebɛid a d‑yettali ṣṣut, simmal yettzad. Ɛeddan, uwwin‑t, ruḥen. Yiwen ur yi‑d‑imuqel, nekk yiwen ur t‑ɛqileɣ. Yeggra‑d akken yiwen n uqcic d alemmas, ad yesɛu 15 n yiseggasen. Steqsaɣ‑t anwa akka yemmuten ɛni.

__ D yiwet n temɣart n taddart.

__ Amek i as‑qqaren ?

__ Taseɛdit n uxxan n Ureẓqi u Muḥ, tamɣart n Muḥend‑Akli.

— Ad tt‑yerḥem Rebbi ! I umɣar‑is, Muḥend‑Akli, mazal‑it

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
— Ah, mazal-it. Maca ula d netta d amuḍin. Tineggura-ya yeṭṭef-it leḥbis, deg uxxam kan.

Suffuɣen-t-id warraw n mmi-s tikwal ɣer lǧameɛ.

— Akka. Saḥḥit a mmi.

— Ulac deg-s. I kečč a baba d aberrani aɛni? Taddart-agi qqaren-as Taddart Ufella; ma yella wacu teḥwajeḍ nneɣ tebɣiḍ, ini-yi-d, ad ak-t-id-xedmeɣ.

— Ala a mmi, ur ḥwaǧeɣ acemma; s teɣzi n leɛmer-ik! Ad ak-imel Rebbi iberdan n lxir ncalleh!

— Saḥḥit a baba! Ihi akka, nekk ad ruḥeɣ ad leḥqeɣ arbaɛ-ina ɣer temqbert, a-t-an ǧǧan-iyi. Ikemmel abrid-is. Ass-a yekfa leɛtab n ddunit ɣef Taseɛdit. Aṭas i twala temcumt, d adrar n ṣṣber, tɛebba ɣef tuyat-is taɛkemt ẓẓayen. Tajmlit-is tewweḍ ass-a. A Sidi Rebbi sixfef fell-as taɛkemt n laxert! tgeḍ-as amkan di ṛṛeḥma, d reḥma!

Ɛeddan ruḥen, kemmlen abrid-nesen; nekk qqimeɣ seddaw n teslant, yeksa-yi laẓ. Kkseɣ-d cwiṭ n uɣrum, sexsiɣ-t yis-s, qqimeɣ ttxemmimeɣ. Tuɣal-iyi am wakken d leḥya ad waliɣ at taddart. Yezher uzal, Medden akk nnejmaɛen deg yixxamen-nsen, ḥala zḍec i yeɛmern iṛideḥ, ma nekk ur nesɛi ara axxam, aqeggel-iw ass-a seddaw n teslant. Mi i d-yekker ubeḥri-nni n uzizgu, yedden lwasɛ, nniɣ-as welleh ad ruḥeɣ ad ɛeddiɣ ɣer lǧameɛ, ad waliɣ ma yella win yellan. Ɛeddaɣ ɣer lǧameɛ-nni aqdim, ufiɣ-t irab. Taddart tbeddel mliḥ, zik kra n yixxamen, tura Llah ibarek teččur.

Ufiɣ kra n yixxamen ɣlin, kra guǧen. Iruḥ am wakken iɛreq-iyi lḥal. Ufiɣ yiwet n tmeṭṭut d talemmast, tetteddu ɣer tala ad d-tagem. Bɣiɣ ad tt-steqsiɣ, meɛna yeggugem yimi. Mi truḥ ad teffat, xziɣ cciṭan, luɛaɣ-tt: “Semḥ-iyi a yelli ad kem-steqsiɣ, ma ulac uɣilf!”

Tneqlab-d, terra-yi-d:

__ Ulac deg-s a baba, steqsi-yi-d ɣef yiman-ik.

__ Ttnadiɣ ɣef lǧameɛ n taddart. Zik yella sdat-agi,

__ Ala lǧameɛ a-t-an nnig taddart, ar Ugni.

— Saḥḥit a yelli! Ad am-imel Rebbi iberdan n lxir ncalleh! yerḥem ɣef lwadin-im!

— Ulac deg-s a baba. Ajmaɛin.

Tekker truḥ, tkemmel abrid-is ɣer tala; nekk uliɣ s Agni, ufiɣ kra n yilmeẓyen ttqessiren gar-asen, d yiwen n umɣar yeqqim weḥd-s, deg ufrag n lǧameɛ, yesrebreb aqelmun n ubernus ɣef wudem-is, taɛrurt-is tekna. Neṭqeɣ-d, luɛaɣ-t, “salam ɛlikum.”

Yerfed aqelmun-nni ɣef wudem-is, yetbeɛ anda i d-yettruḥ ṣṣut: “Weɛli-kum ssalam! yenqes yiẓri-w, ur ttwaliɣ ara mliḥ alama yiwen iqerb-d d tama-w ara tɛeqleɣ d anwa-t!”

Iruḥ am wakken ɛeqleɣ-t, maca ur tebbteɣ ara iman-iw.

— D Muḥend-Akli aya? Nekk d Saɛid n dadda-k Ɛmer u Meqqran.

Muḥend-Akli d arfiq, d aḥbib n temẓi. Ya ḥesra ɣef zik-nni!

__ Ur yi-d-qqar ara d Saɛid n dadda Ɛmer? Anwa i d as-yennan ass-agi ad k-ẓreɣ, a Saɛid a gma!

Iban-iyi-d am win yeɛyan di tudert, acemma ur d as-yehwi. Udem-is yuɣal d aberkan, yekmec am tkerciwt, umbeɛd d udem-nni acebḥan am lefner, yiwen n wuglan ur d yegri ɣef yineɣ. Acebbub-is d acebḥan, zik d aberkan am ssmex Wajbeɣ-t: “Ad ig Rebbi teǧǧa-d temɣart-ik...

__ Ad ak-iɛewweḍ Rebbi s lxir, a Saɛid a gma! Twalaḍ! ula d tamɣart teǧǧa-yi, ggriɣ-d weḥd-i.

Tewɛer tuǧǧla n tewser. Lukan xir d nekk i yemmuten...

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
— Ur qqar ara akka, a Muḥend‑Akli ! Wagi d lmektub n Sidi Rebbi.

__ I melmi akka i d‑tleḥqeḍ ihi a Saɛid ?

— Sgelli ɣef ṭṭhur‑nni. Deg ubrid i ken‑id‑ufiɣ mi tewwim tanerḥumt‑nni. Ad fell‑as yeɛfu Rebbi temcumt ! aṭas n lhem i teẓra di ddunit‑is!

__ Susem kan a Saɛid a gma ! Ayen iɛedden fell‑as d tifsax deg‑m a tudert. Nneɣ ɣef Uceɛban meskin. Ad t‑yerḥem Rebbi !

— Ur yi‑d‑qqar ara yemmut Uceɛban, meskin !

— Yemmut di lgirra tis snat, maca yeǧǧa‑d amur‑is yeɛmer.

— Yezweǧ meskin ?

— Tezwǧ‑as yemma‑s, ad ten‑yerḥem !

— Dɣa ḥemdulleh ! ad fell‑asen yeɛfu Rebbi !

— Kečč la xbar‑ik ! Ttceyyiɛeɣ‑ak‑in tibratin, ur yi‑d‑tettarraḍ ara, dɣa dayen.

— Welleh, a Muḥend‑Akli a gma, deg wass‑n mi sliɣ s lexber n lmut n yemma, dɣa d tin i d tabrat taneggarut ɣriɣ. Uɣaleɣ beddleɣ tansa, ur bɣiɣ win ara yi‑d‑isnedfen, ad d‑mmektiɣ tamurt, almi ɛeddan ugar n 50 d aseggas... I kečč a Muḥ, d acu tesɛiḍ d dderya ?

— D tullas, d bab n tullas.

— Llhiberk, lhant ula d tiḥdayin.

— Welleh ma ǧǧant‑iyi, msakit, nutenti d warraw n Uceɛban. Meɛna uggadeɣ teryel‑nni, tislit n dadda Lwennas, ad fell‑as yeɛfu Rebbi. Ẓriɣ tettraǧu kan ad kemmleɣ ad neqreɣ, ad ten‑tsufeɣ.

— Yennulfa‑d dadda‑k Lwennas, liqan iɣab.

__ Ah, yuɣal‑d. Ula d netta liqant tɣurr‑it lɣerba, maca yuɣal yerra‑d agerzim s axxam, yezweǧ, yesɛa tlata n warrac. Ad fell‑as yeɛfu Rebbi ! Yesɛa snat n teslatin, yiwet newwi‑tt‑id di xwali, d lmalaykat ; tayeḍ akin i udrar, maca tewɛer, d ǧahennama. A‑tt‑an tɛewwel ad tsufeɣ arraw n Uceɛban ɛinani, tettraǧu kan ad kemmleɣ ad neqreɣ. Ula d tamɣart‑is ur tt‑tettqadar ara.

Nettqessir nekk d Muḥend‑Akli. Neqqim almi yesrareḥ tuddna n lmeɣreb. Netta yesnefsusi‑d ɣef wuli‑s, yettu lhem‑is ; nekk augar. Yekker iẓull lmeɣeb. Yeggul deg‑i, ad dduɣ s axxam‑is. Qqimeɣ kra n wussan, nemwanas. Ilmeẓyen n taddart, ad  ten‑iḥrez Rebbi, nnejmaɛen‑d meṛṛa, rran tazeqqa‑nni n baba yeɣlin. Fersen akk lḥara‑nni, qelɛen anejjel‑nni...

Aql‑i ggriɣ‑d d awḥid, teɣlid fell‑i tmeddit, meɛna ɛṭi‑ten sseḥḥa wat taddart, ur yi‑iǧǧi ara. Sya u sya i d‑rezzun fell‑i, yal wa d acu ara yi‑d‑ixdem. Ur yi‑ixus wara. Mi d azizgu, ad ffɣeɣ ɣer berra, nekk d Muḥend‑Akli. Iḥekku‑yi tudert‑is am win yeldin taktabt, yal ass d tawerqet, d tidyanin yecban timucuḥa‑nni n tilawt ttawin yimɣaren n zzman. Ɛaceɣ ugar n 50 n ssna di Fransa, yiwen n wass ur ḥusseɣ s wayen ttḥussuɣ di taddart‑iw ; ul‑iw yuɣal‑d d aleqqaq, mačči d winna ibnedqen di lɣerba. Lukan d temẓẓi i d‑yezqqiren ɣef tewser yili d awezɣi ad ǧǧeɣ tamurt ; maca akken yeqqar urumi “ c’est trop tard ”. Ula i d xdem neddama n tagara. Nddekwaleɣ‑d tameddit n wass, tferfer‑iyi temẓi.

Zuhra LAƔA

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
D tnaṣfa n wass. Lḥal di berra yeqber; iṭṭij ineṣṣef igenni, tamdint n lzzayer texla, izi ur yḥerrik ara di berra. Seg wakken yeḥma lḥal, cucfeɣ rebɛa n tikkal neɣ kter, ɣas akken, ḥulfaɣ i ṣṣura‑w tekker deg‑s tmes; tidi tcercur ɣef leḥnak‑iw d wenyir‑iw amzun d isaffen. Aḥaruq unebdu, rniɣ ddiq n texxamt. Akka i d tixamin n Bgayet, ddiq, lḥamu arnu nnwa n lebḥer. Ad‑as‑tiniḍ d tuggi, ayen tsumaḍ ak‑id‑yesserɣ.

Tawwurt n ubalku tebrareḥ, ṭṭiqan cetḥen. D azal azylal! Cwiṭ n nnesma ulac‑it ad iyi‑d‑terr rruḥ. Ceɛleɣ tasebbuḥrut maɛna tidi mazal‑it tetcercuq. Syin akkin, bdiɣ ttawiɣ tarraɣ deg wexxam, txemmimeɣ ad ɛiwdeɣ ucaf, neɣ ad waliɣ tilizi...Dewreɣ almi ɛyiɣ, kecmeɣ ɣer texxamt nniɣ‑as ad aruɣ, ad kemleɣ taqsiṭ bdiɣ ahat ad tuɣ azɣal. Mazal‑iyi sin wussan kan ad t‑ceyɛeɣ ɣer weɣmis ''Aneɣmas'' «La dépêche de kabylé » i deg iyi‑d‑tṣaḥ teweriqt, yal ddurt, taruɣ deg‑s tullisin‑iw. Mara d iniɣ taruɣ, mačči d Fulknir neɣ d Gugul, maɛna seg asmi i yebdiɣ tira, iɛejeb‑iyi lḥal. Iɛjeb‑iyi wayen taruɣ.

Timdukal‑iw yetabaɛen tiqṣiḍin‑iw, qqaren‑iyi‑d akk « tezzewreḍ teǧǧiḍ izgaren » mara d cekreɣ tullisin uriɣ yakan, maɛna ur cliɛeɣ ara. Di tira, akken twaliɣ, ilaq uqbel kulci, ad ak‑yeɛjeb wayen tettaruḍ, ad tḥemleḍ i wakken ad tkemleḍ. Yal yiwen yettaru kan tudert‑is...s tira kan i zemreɣ ad begneɣ tudret‑iw, tḥulfuɣ iman‑iw d ilelli, yal mara inigeɣ ɣer tmurt n wawalen d tugniwin...Ayen ara k‑iɛejben ugar, d amek ara yezger wayen nettaru akud akken ad yidir d leqrun mbeɛed‑nneɣ, am akken yedder wawal neɣ kter...

Taẓuri tettili‑d yal mara icerreg yiman n unaẓur agu‑nni yesdergen ɣef medden akk lesrar n ugama d wayen akk is‑d‑yezzin, mara yessiweḍ ad isami s lejwareḥ‑is afwad n ugama, mara yers uḍar‑is ɣef webrid, uɣen akk medden iban‑asen‑d d timeḍell‑as, ger usurif d wayeḍ ad taɣ tafat alama yuɣ akk webrid...Maca, mačči yal win i yesnen kra seg ugama d lesrar‑is, akken yebɣu ibeggen‑it‑id di tẓur‑ines, yuklal ad s‑nsiwel "Anaẓur". Isem n unaẓur mačči aṭṭas i t‑yuklalen...

Tagida akken iteǧǧiɣ deg iḍelli, aɛemmur n iɣmisen di teɣmert, idlisen mbezrurɛent, ta tecteḥ, ta temdel, ta ɣef yiri qrib ad teɣli, d wayen din n tiwreqtin yekmumsen. Seg akken taruɣ tɛawadeɣ, yeččur ubidun n wafrasen almi yenfel. Afenǧal n lqahwa taberkant yenɣel, yeɣma ɣef kra n lkwaɣeḍ yersen sdat‑s... Lḥaṣul, acemma ur d‑yeḍtir di texxamt. Tuɣal d adaynin, akka i yetuɣal ma ulac tilawin deg wexxam, din kan i nessen lqima‑nsent!

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Qqimeɣ  ɣef  tseɣimt,  iḍarren  deg  idis,  ṭfeɣ  imru  deg  ufus‑iw,  wwiɣt  ɣer  yimi‑w, txemmimeɣ amek ara  s kemleɣ i teqṣit‑nni.  Akken bdiɣ tira, azal  n sin n ijariḍen,  ma aṭṭas, yeɣli‑d fell‑i nadam am ẓebra, ḥulfaɣ i wallen‑iw teqnent si tazayt, ma d allaɣ‑iw yeddawar seg akken i yeḥma lḥal. Kkreɣ ssardeɣ‑d udem‑iw ahat ad‑iyi‑kkes, ulac. Mi ḍfeɣ  imru  ad  qnent  wallen‑iw.  I  wakken  ur  gganeɣ  ara  ɣef  tagida,  ẓleɣ  acemma ɣef umeṭreḥ, ad sɛeddiɣ tanafa. Maɛna, seg wakken yerɣa wussu, tneqlabeɣ kan rennuɣ, d lmuḥal ad ḍseɣ deg anect‑nni n unaɣur...

Akken walaɣ lḥal yerreẓ‑d, tusa‑iyi‑d tikti, ad ṣubbeɣ ɣer cceṭ n lebḥer, deg‑s ad wɛuɣ abeḥri ad iyi‑d‑yessaki, yerna ad lḥuɣ cwiṭ, ad iyi‑ d‑asent, ahat, kra n tikti ad kemleɣ taqṣit. Akken yenna Kateb Yasin: « tikta tasent-d lawan n tikli ».

Kreɣ‑d  s  leɛgez,  nadam  mazal‑it  deg‑i,  zzuɣreɣ‑d  iman‑iw  almi  d  taxxamt  n  tarda,  ḍegreɣ aman ɣef udem‑iw, greɣ iḍarren‑iw deg icifaḍ, ɣelqeɣ tawwurt n ubalku, ma d asfaylu ǧǧiɣ‑t  yeldi  kra,  akken  ad  tebbuḥru  texxamt  mi  ara  d‑uɣaleɣ  ɣer  lewhi  n uzuzwu. Ma d lebɣi‑w yeqsed lebḥer. Sdat n lbaṭima mlaleɣ‑d Nna karima, teseqsa‑yi‑d ɣef imawlan‑iw, amek ittilin, ma qrib ad uɣalen si tmurt neɣ ala. Axaṭer ɣef akken id d‑tenna  tecdha  yemma,  alla  yid‑s  i  la  t‑ttqeṣir,  i  la  t‑tekkes  lxiq  n  temɛict  di  temdint.

Tettwali di yemma rriḥa n tmurt, ɣur‑s tamɛict di temdint d inig ameqran. Dɣa tekcem s axxam‑is nek kemleɣ abrid‑iw, Ur zriɣ amek itt‑id‑mlaleɣ, d wamek it‑ruḥ...

Qqimeɣ kra n lweqt akken ttmuquleɣ deg warrac, tturaren ddabax uḍar zdat n lbaṭima. Syin  akin,  kemleɣ  abrid  ɣer  yiri  n  lebḥar,  din  meqqar  ulac  lɣaci,  dɣa  dayen  id‑iyi‑swehmen, annect‑nni n wezɣal isem n wemdan ur yexliq ara di lebḥer; ala nek d ṣṣut n lmwaji id d‑yettuɣalen si lebɛid staɛfayent ɣef yiri. twaliɣ amek rmel i yettsummu deg‑sent, ttaǧant‑d ala ikuftan icebḥanen. Nek deg‑sent zehhuɣ: amek id d‑ttruḥunt si lebɛid d wamek  itt‑ruẓent ɣef tacciwin,  d  ṣṣut id‑segrayent bḥal acewwiq seg akken  yewzen.

Abeḥri  yebda  yettara‑d  deg‑i  tarwiḥt,  yeslufuy  i  wudem‑iw,  ḥulfaɣ  yedhen  turin‑iw,  yeḥya‑d  tafekka‑w  yesseknef  uzal  n  Bgayet.  Kseɣ  icifaḍ‑iw,  ɛelqaɣ‑ten  ɣef  tayet‑iw tayeffust, tedduɣ, sakin am uderwic, i leḥfa, ɣef rmel yeskikiḍen tileqwaɛi n iḍarren‑iw seg  wakken  mazal  deg‑s  lḥamu.  Ssaliɣ  aserwal‑iw,  ttleɣ  rjul‑is  almi  d  tigecrar,  dɣa  skecmeɣ  iḍarren‑iw  deg  waman.  Akken  kan  iyi‑d‑suman,  ḥulfaɣ  i ṣṣura‑w  teccatew, yebda iɛeǧǧeb‑iyi lḥal, qqimeɣ turareɣ s waman...

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Akud yettazal kan mara t‑neḥwij, yettafeg am aḍu mara nebɣu ad yiɣzif... Iṭṭij yebda azrureg, amzun yeseblaɛ‑it lebḥer, tezzi‑yas‑d laḥmuregga. Tafat‑nni taneggarut id d‑yeǧǧa, yeḍla‑tt i lebḥer, yuɣalen yettfeǧǧiǧ si tezweɣ, ma d igenni ireqq am lemri. Nechameɣ sdat n tfelwit‑nni, amezzun d tazerbit n rqem yeḍbeɛ ufus n unaẓur. Dinna i teḥbes tiɛubja ...Qqimeɣ ttfarriǧeɣ deg‑s almi ttuɣ iman‑iw ...

Din din, yemɣenbas‑d igenni, tulit‑id tebrek deg yiwet n tikkelt, lebḥer yemcewwal, amzun akken yella win iten‑yesserfan. Akken walaɣ yebda iɣelli‑d ṭlam, yesberber acḍaḍ‑is i tɣaltin, yebda wul‑iw yettmergigid. Kreɣ, zwiɣ rmel ineṭḍen deg usarwal‑iw, lsiɣ icifaḍ‑iw, uliɣ‑d. Werɛad ineṣfeɣ abrid, sliɣ i tiẓẓift. Si tama taẓelmaṭ i d‑tekka.

Rǧiɣ cwiṭ deg wemkan‑iw, muqleɣ akka d wakka, ulac. Nniɣ‑as ahat d imeẓẓuɣ‑n‑iw kan id d‑yettarran ṣṣut. Akken ruḥeɣ ad‑kemleɣ abrid, sliɣ daɣen i tiẓẓift‑nni. Tikelt‑agi tugi ad teḥbes, d ṣṣut n teqcict! Iyi‑d icebba Rebbi. Tebɛeɣ asuɣu ansi i d‑yekka, iḍher‑iyi yiwen wecwaw yufrar‑d ɣef waman, ma d isuɣan‑nni, am akken kkufren; tikwal ad‑sen‑sleɣ tikwal ala. tazaleɣ ɣef cceṭ am win yeffeɣ leɛqel, tmuquleɣ ɣer tama n wecwaw‑nni, dɣa tban‑iyi‑d tfekka n lɛebd tettemɛebbar d lemwaji, ala ifassen‑is id d‑ibanen, ma d aqerru‑s mi id d‑yuli ad‑t‑ ɣummen waman amzun yella kra it‑ijebden ɣer lqaɛ....d taqcict! D taqcict! Tura tḥeqqeɣ...

Akken walaɣ d lɛebd iffeɣ‑iyi leɛqel ugar. Ur Ẓriɣ d acu ara xedmeɣ, dɣa bdiɣ a tuɣuɣ ula d nek « Ahanu‑t! ahanu‑t!.. » ulac! Ẓriɣ ulac yiwen ur yelli ara d‑yeslen. Si tama txemmimeɣ ad ruḥeɣ ad‑ssiwleɣ i walbɛeḍ neɣ i yiɣallen n usemneɛ ad t‑id‑smenɛen, maɛna ugadeɣ ad iruḥ fell‑as lḥal ad teɣreq. Si tama nniḍen, kukraɣ lebḥer yerfan deg yiwen n tikkelt d waman isemmaḍen arnu ɣer‑s ṭlam id d‑yeɣlin, ma yečča‑t lebḥer ad‑iyi‑seddu. Uɣaleɣ sakin am win iḥeṣlen ger lḥafer d tṣemmart. Mi id d‑mektaɣ taqcict ad tan ger tudert d lmut, gezmeɣ‑t, din din, di rray, ɣas akken ugadeɣ ad teglu yis‑i tɛeǧǧaǧt‑nni...

Kseɣ icifaḍ‑iw, negzeɣ s aman, kkateɣ s ifassen s iḍarren almi i yewwḍeɣ ɣur‑s. Nettat, si tufɣa n leɛqel, txebbeḍ deg waman, tuɣ‑it lḥala, tetsuɣu ɣer Rebbi it‑id‑ixelqen, yerna mi teldi imi‑s ad s‑kecmen waman ad t‑selqef. Dayen tuyes tudert, tebda la tberru i yiman‑is. Akken leḥqeɣ, ṭfeɣ‑t‑id seg ufus, maɛni si taẓayt‑nni qrib tegla yis‑i. Tuyat‑iw gezment si ɛeggu, temɛebbareɣ d lemwaji, nitenti jebdent nek jebdeɣ, lebḥer yeldi‑d imi‑s ad‑aɣ‑yessebleɛ di sin… Dɣa imi d tfaq acemma d yiman‑is, tneggez‑d fell‑i am

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
tin id d‑yuɣalen si lmut, teṭṭef‑iyi si lexneq almi id d‑grent wallen‑iw, ur d‑kkiseɣ ara tamgart‑iw ger ifassen‑is almi it‑cerweɣ merriɣet. Sakin rriɣ‑t‑id ɣer leɛqel‑is, tethedden, zuɣreɣ‑tt‑id, nɛum‑d almi d cceṭ. Azal n xemsa ddqayeq d nek d imenɣi d lebḥer, xemsa dqayeq amzun d aseggas, almi nwiɣ ad neǧǧeɣ tarwiḥt‑iw...

Mi d‑newweḍ ɣer cceṭ, nettat teqqim ɣef tgecrar, terra‑d kra teswa, nek negfeɣ, ḥulfaɣ i ṣṣura‑w temmar, tettergigi si ɛeggu ad as‑tiniḍ d win yewwet mirqes. Mi d‑ terra ayen teswa, tefser iman‑is am uceṭṭiḍ ɣef rmel, tneggef ula d nettat seg akken tefcel. Nesteɛfa kra, dɣa zziɣ‑d ɣur‑s steqsaɣ‑t d acu i txeddem tlemẓit am nettat lawan‑agi di lebḥer?!

Akken iyi‑d‑twala, tenekmumec ɣef yiman‑is, akken ur t‑twaliɣ ara ayen tekseb, imi iceṭṭiḍen telsa ḍebɛen‑d ɣef tfekka‑s yeččuren kra, ad as‑tiniḍ nitni d teksumt‑is yiwen, seg akken bezgen, yerna xfifi‑t. Acebbub‑is yebzeg, yenṭeḍ ɣef udem‑is d tuyat‑is; yeddel‑as‑tent kra. Tudmet‑is d taxemrit d tamecṭuḥt, tiḥnakin‑is d tizeggaɣin, tetban meẓẓiyet, azal n ɛecrin iseggasen kan ara s‑fkeɣ.

Mi qerbeɣ ɣur‑s, twexxer ɣer deffir, tebda tettergigi am yifer si tawla n usemmiḍ neɣ ahat si tegdi ur ẓriɣ ara? Steqsaɣ‑t isem‑is, d acu itxeddem dinna, nniɣ‑as: « isem‑iw Lina » ahat ad iyi‑tfek laman, ulac acemma! Ad as‑tiniḍ teggugem, tessusem kan, tečča‑yi‑d s tmuɣli. Nnefs ur t‑id‑yuli ara. Ahat iẓra‑nni ad neṭqen! Ulac ula d tanmirt imi t‑id‑snesreɣ ger ifassen n lmut. Bɣiɣ ad tẓer belli ur ilaq ad‑iyi‑tagad, ḥawteɣ‑t ad‑tini anda tezdeɣ akken ad t‑awiɣ ulac lmenṭeq. Ur ẓriɣ ara ansi iyi‑d‑tekka tmexluqt‑nni neɣ sani ara t‑rreɣ....

Mi iseḥsabeɣ akk i tigi, sliɣ i lheffat, walaɣ taftilt mebɛid d lxyal ur t‑frizeɣ ara si tallest. Simmal ad d‑taẓent lheffat‑nni, taftilt‑nni tetimɣur, lxyalat‑nni ad tbanen, ḍehren‑iyi tlata yergazen, ad d‑teddun qbala ɣer‑neɣ, ad ssawalen, s taɛrabt, qqaren: « wakka yellan ? Err‑d awal ». Seg akken i yugadeɣ ad ilin d iceffaren, ssusmeɣ ur d‑rriɣ ara awal. Yuɣ lḥal ugadeɣ ɣef tmexluqt‑nni, ma d nek zemreɣ i yiman‑iw. Nitni taẓen‑d nekni nettergigi, dɣa temmeɣ‑d, tḥennec‑d ɣur‑i, nek tṣebbireɣ‑t, ɣas akken ur ẓriɣ ara iɣ‑yetraǧǧun...

Linda Makur.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Asirem n taǧǧalt

Tudert, abrid‑is yessawen, yiwen tefka‑as yezha, yufa ayen yessaram, wayeḍ tekkes‑as, yeṛwa tigad yuran fell‑as; maca d tagi i d tudert. Ayen tettidir tmetti macci d ayen ara d‑yales yimi s yiḥulfan war tilas, amek tettidir tmetti taqbaylit d twaculin s umata.

Tagi d yiwet n twacult, d tawacult n Nna Ferruǧa; yettidiren di lḥif d wurrif, imi ur yeshil ara ɣef tmeṭṭut ad teǧǧel di leεmer‑is akken meẓẓiyet, tegrra‑d d taǧǧalt; argaz‑is yemmut yeǧǧa‑d tarwa‑s d imeẓẓyanen, d igujilen. Tqubel ddunit akken i d‑tusa, imi tameṭṭut taqbaylit tettwassen si zzman aqdim s nnif‑is d lḥerma‑s i as‑yefka Rebbi. Xas akken d iberdan yessawnen i d‑temlal maca akken i d‑usan tusa‑asen; tṛebba tarwa‑s, texdem axxam‑is, terna lexla (temger lɣella, tḥuc tuga, tezdem isɣaren, telqeḍ azemmur,...) win i wumi yewεer ccɣel ad as‑yessiwel, ad texdem ɣur‑s d ayen isehlen. Akka i tqubel laẓ‑is.

Tudert n Nna ferruǧa akka akk i truḥ ɣef wudem n warraw‑is akken ad d‑kkren, ad izmiren i yiman‑nsen, teswa fell‑asen timerẓuga awi‑d kan ad twali tarwa‑s ferḥen xas ulamma lexṣas yella, maca tewweḍ ɣer lebɣi‑s seg wasmi i d‑lulen warraw‑is d imecṭaḥ tezga teqqar‑asen: "Ad timɣurem, ad teɣrem, ad tizmirem i yiman‑nwen imi leqraya d tafat. S usirem i tebna tudert n warraw‑is".

Nna Ferruǧa, tesεa sin warrac Meqqran akked Muḥend, d kraḍ n teqcicin Faḍma, Lǧuher, Ɣnima. Am wakken qqaren di lḥif i d‑yettban urgaz, s tidet lḥif yettṛebbi, yettawi amdan ad yeddu deg ubrid lεali, Meqqran d Muḥend d inelmaden deg tesdawit; d Meqqran i d amenzu n uxxam, fell‑as i ters teεkemt ẓẓayen, Muḥend d amaẓuẓ; d netta i d amecṭuḥ, xeddmen daɣen anda ufan i wakken ad d‑ḥellin ciṭuḥ n umeṣruf, akken ad awsen iman‑nsen, d twacult, tabaεen kan leḥlal. Nna Ferruǧa yal tikkelt tettweṣṣi‑ten ɣef temεict n leḥlal imi leḥlal am seksu n yirden, ad t‑reḍmeḍ ad ifetti, ma d leḥram am seksu n ubelluḍ ad t‑reḍmeḍ ad ifessi.

Akken daɣen tettweṣṣi‑ten ɣef tegmat deg way‑gar‑asen, Meqqran d Muḥend ṭṭfen deg wawal n yemma‑tsen, yenna Meqqran deg usefru‑a mi yuɣal meqqar:

A yemma εzizen a yemma

Akken akk i d‑nekker drus

Deg gma ur ttakeɣ afus

Di ṭṭiq ur t‑ttaǧǧaɣ ara

D mmi‑s n baba d yemma

Fell‑as ur ttakeɣ afus.

Kemmlen akken amennuɣ d ddunit, mi llan di tesdawit, sεan leqraya ad ɣren, akud i d‑yeggran xeddmen deg‑s, ur ttɣimin ara akk, ma yella deg uxxam i llan ttεawanen yemma‑tsen deg wayen yellan: tayessawt, azdam, anɣac, aleqqem, afras,... ur sεin ara timirt ad qqimen.

Meqqran d Muḥend ur ssinen tiɣimit di lqahwa, neɣ deg uzniq n taddart, s wakka nnuɣen d ddunit alarmi i d‑tban ciṭuḥ tafat fell‑asen, xedmen akk ayen yellan deg‑sen akken ad awḍen ɣer lebɣi n yemma‑tsen, d uḥdiqen, d umεinen, ttqadaren akk medden d amedya deg taddart win yekkren ad asen‑yini: "Ad yerḥem Rebbi taεebbuḍt i ken‑yurwen".

Nna Ferruǧa d tameṭṭut d wawal, timital‑is ur llint aṭas am nettat; d tin i d‑iṛebban sin yirgazen, d kraḍ n tlawin, teskker‑iten‑id, fazen, texdem‑asen akk ayen i ilaqen deg wulac, maca ul‑is yeččur d tumert. Asirem amezwaru, tewweḍ ɣur‑s; arraw‑is meqqer‑it, ɣran akk, wwin akk abrid igerrzen werǧin ssinen yir tikli ala tin yessufuɣen i ḍefren. Ma d asirem wis sin, akken teqqar deg wawal‑is a wer mmteɣ alamma ḥeḍreɣ i lferḥ n warraw n warraw‑iw. Nna Ferruǧa tenna deg usefru:

D abrid n baba d jeddi

Ammus ur t‑yuli ara

D abrid‑nsen i wwiɣ

Win yeṭṭfen di tjadit‑is

D lmuḥal nekk ad anfaɣ

Yeḥrez nnif‑is

Lewṣṣa‑yi id‑ǧǧan

Isem‑is ɣer medden yeswa.

Abernus fell‑as ḥurbeɣ

Sɣur: Samira Cekkal.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Tekcem yiwen n tmeṭṭut ɣer sbiṭar ad terbu, tameddit n wass. D lweqt ideg I d‑ilul uqcic tameṭṭut tewweḍ leɛfu n Rebbi. Yeɣli‑d leḥzen d aberkan ɣef uqerru n urgaz, isḥassef imi d‑tɣwer tmettant ɣef tmeṭṭtut‑is. Yemmeɣ urgaz yefka aqcic ameɣbun i xalt‑is, ad trebbi. Ɛeddan azal n sebɛa n wagguren n leḥzen, argaz ur yeṣbir ara yekker yawwi‑d tameṭṭut tis snat, yesɛa yid‑s aqcic d teqcict.

Zrin yiseggasen yuɣal urgaz yewwi‑d aqcic‑nni n temzwarut ad yidir ɣur‑s. Aqcic ameɣbun di rrif i d‑yufa iman‑is, acku yanbaba‑s tɛezel‑it ur teṭṭhella ara deg‑s meskin, tasa‑s tecweḍ kan ɣef warraw n tɛebuḍṭ‑is. Aqcic ameɣbun yerwa timerzuga, ula d učči i d‑yettawi baba‑s, d tisigar id‑lqut‑is, yerna weḥd‑s id as‑d‑ttak am ugdi.

Yiwen n was, usan‑d imawlan n tmeṭṭut ad ččen imensi, ikcem‑d uqcic ɣer tẓeqqa n yinebgawen, yedda‑d lqeḍ‑is seg wayen iwala n tgella ɣef ṭṭabla, yemmeɣ ad yeddem abruy n lmekla ad yečč, dɣa twala‑t yenbaba‑s, tuzzel‑d tezwi‑as tafettus, temmeɣ tefka‑as cwit rruz ɣer tqedduḥt tewwiḍ‑t ar ssiwan, tenna‑as: “Qqim da alemma ruḥen yinebgawen.” Yeqqim uqcic bu rebɛa iseggasen di berra itett i usemmid n tegrest igezzmen iɣsan, seg wakken yugad yenbaba‑s ad as‑ters ur yekcim ara mi yekfa učči.

Suhlen yinebgawen, tessared leḥwal, tejmmeɛ arraw‑is ɣer texxamt ad ṭsen. Mi d‑yewweḍ urgaz seg lxedma, tenna‑as: “ad ak‑d‑seqqiɣ ad teččeḍ?”. Yenna –as: “Ala, ččiɣ di berra.” Yesteqsa ɣef mmi‑s amenzu, tenna‑as ha‑t deg wussu yeṭṭes, tettu belli tḥebes‑it di berra. Yetthenna, iruḥ srid iɛedda ad yeṭṭes, maca aqellid ameqqran bab igewan ur yeṭṭis, ha‑tt‑a tbedd‑d ɣur‑s tmeṭṭut‑is tamenzut di targit tenna‑as: “Ḥader mmi‑tneɣ.”

Yeffafa‑d seg tgunit am win ara d‑wteḍ s ubeqqa, dɣa yezzi ɣer tmeṭṭut‑is yenna‑as: “Anda‑t mmi?” Nniɣ‑ak ha‑t‑an deg wussu yeṭṭes. Yuɣal urgaz ɣer tguni, ha‑tt‑a i tikelt nniḍen tmeṭṭut‑is terza‑d ɣur‑s tenna: “hader mmi‑tneɣ.” Yedduqqes‑d seg tnafa yemmeɣ yenna i tmeṭṭut‑is: “A tameṭṭut anida‑t mmi?” Uhhhh, icɣeb‑ik mmi‑k, ɛeddaɣ sgelli ɣur‑s, ufiɣ‑t yeṭṭes, ulac acu ara tagaded. Iɛawed yeṭṭes ha‑tt‑an itikelt nniḍen tuɣal‑d tmeṭṭut‑is yemmuten tenn‑as: “Dayen tura ifut lawan mmi‑tneɣ yerna‑d ɣur‑i.”

Yekker s lemɣawla, yettnadi, deg uxxam yessawal i mmi‑s, temsusam ddunit yetti‑d akk tixxamin, ulac ur d‑yewwit ara deg uqerru‑is belli ad t‑yaf deg ssiwan, srid yeldi tiwwura n ssiwan iwala mmi‑s yenneḍ ɣef yiman‑is aqerru‑is deg gar iḍerren‑is, ibeddel wudem‑is unuɣ, zegzaw uksum‑is, yemmeɣ fell‑as baba‑s ihucc‑it, ulac, smmeḍ dayen yewweḍ leɛfu n yakuc (Rebbi). Gar ifassen‑is taqedduḥt n rruz tzeggen, axater yesɛa ttiɛad d wid t‑iḥemmlen, yettagaden fell‑as, yesɛa ttiɛad akk d yemma‑s.

Yeqqar yinzi: “Argaz d asalas, tameṭṭut d ajeggu alemmas” ma yerreẓ ujeggu, terreẓ twacult, trab tmetti. Ihi a tiyemmatin, tiqbayliyin ḥadremt tarwa‑nkent, d agerruj‑nkent.

Tasuqilt: TAYEB LOUNES

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Yiwen n wass deg wussan n unebdu, yella Dda lḥusin yeqqim di tejmaƐt d yimdukkal‑is, ttqessiren sqerdacen timsal ɣef lexṣas n waman i yeččan ddunit, yenṭeq Dda lḥusin yenna‑asen: « nekk ala taɣuzi n lbir ara tt‑iselken yid‑i ». Armi d‑yelḥeq s axxam yekker yenna‑as i tmeṭṭut‑is a yelli‑s Muḥ Urezqi Lmesɛud: « qrib ad teɛyu ccedda fell‑aɣ, ad yekkes lḥif n waman ɣef yiqerra‑nneɣ » ad nestaɛfu si tagmin, ad yestaɛfu uɣyul‑iw meskin yerwan ttɛebga acḥal d aseggas.

Tamɣart terra‑as :« a lxir‑nneɣ ay amɣar, amek akka ? », yenna‑as : « jmaɛliman ar tikkelt‑a ad‑ɣzeɣ lbir » Dda lḥusin yessufeɣ awal di taddart, iwakken ad d‑asen iwaziwen ara t‑iƐiwnen, ha‑t‑an yewweḍ‑d wass anida bdan taɣuzi n wanu, Dda lḥusin yefreḥ mačči d kra imi ad yesƐu aman i lebda, am win iwumi tekkes tƐekkemt, ussan ttƐeddin lbir ittelqay irennu, ma d aman ula d tiqqit ur d‑tban, Dda lḥusin yebda‑t‑id unezgum d uɣbel.

Ha‑t‑an Ɛeddan sin n wagguren segmi bdan taɣuzi, lbir n Dda lḥusin yeqqur amzun yewwet deg‑s uɣurar. Dda lḥusin yerfa mačči d kra, imi taqsiḍt yeḍran yid‑s werğin teḍri di taddart, acku yal win yeɣzan lbir yufa aman, ala ɣef Dda lḥusin i tekkḥes teswiƐt, armi wwḍen ilmeẓyen n taddart qqaren‑as : « lbir n Dda lḥusin yelha kan i ujmeƐ n yirden ».

Dda lḥusin yeggul ur yeḥnit ur terni ula d yiwet n terdast di tɣuzi, ussan ttƐeddin tallit n unebdu teffeɣ, yekcem ḥertadem tebda‑d tissit tamezwarut, Dda lḥusin yella yeṭṭes ad tili ahat d azgen n yiḍ, ssakint‑tt‑id tmiqwa n ugeffur timezwura, mi ṭerdiqent ɣef lqermud n tzeqqa, yeddunfi‑d iruḥ d tazzla yewwi‑d iḥelyiwen, yeṭṭef abrid‑is ɣer lbir mi yelḥeq ɣur‑s yenna‑as :« akken iyi t‑ḥermeḍ seg wid lqaƐa, ad k‑ḥermeɣ seg wid igenni », yekker iɣumm‑it.

Zrin kra n wussan at taddart walan d acu yexdem Dda lḥusin, kkren usan‑d ɣur‑s nhan‑as akken ad yekkes aɣummu ɣef lbir. Dda lḥusin yenna‑asen : « a yat taddart lbir‑agi ur yesfillit ara i wayen yelhan, d acu xas akken gulleɣ ur ḥniteɣ, meƐna ur ttruẓuɣ ara leƐnaya‑nwen », lbir yettwakkes‑as uɣummu ccetwa teğhedd, aṭas n ugeffur i yewwten lbir yeččur armi yettenfal.

Ha‑t‑an telḥeq‑d tefsut ğuğğgen akk ijeğğigen d yimɣan, Dda lḥusin yeqqen aɣyul‑is am yal ass di tmazirt akken ad yeks, armi d tameddit iruḥ ad t‑id‑yejmeƐ, yufa ḥaca amrar deg umkan‑nni, imuqel akka n wakka ur t‑id‑yufi, iṣub ɣer tejmeƐt yessteqsa at taddart ma ulac win iwalan aɣyul‑is, kkren wat taddart ama meẓẓi ama meqqer, kkan akk taddart aɣyul ur d‑iban later‑is, yeɣli‑d ṭṭlam nnejmaƐen wat taddart s ixxamen‑nsen, ma d Dda lḥusin i teƐreḍ deg‑s tmeṭṭut‑is ad yečč imensi yugi, iɣaḍ‑it uɣyul‑is mačči d kra, ala aɣyul d tmeṭṭut‑is i yesƐa d amwanes di ddunit‑is, iḍes yefferfer seg wallen‑is, yeqqim yettxemmim ɣef wanida i yezmer ad yili uɣyul‑is, ciṭuḥ kan akka am win it‑id‑yewwten s ubeqqa yemmekti‑d lbir‑nni, yekker s tazzla ɣur‑s xas akken d ṭṭlam tafat n tziri twanes‑d tasusmi n yiḍ, mi yewweḍ ɣer lbir yufa aɣyul meskin yeẓẓel s daxxel, Dda lḥusin nnefṣ di ṣṣura‑s truḥ, yeğğa‑t uɣyul iɣef irebba tassa, werğin i t‑yeḥsib d aɣyul iḥseb‑it amzun d amdan neɣ d yiwen si twacult‑is amzun d amdakkel‑is, yid‑s i yecrek lbaḍna d lesrar‑is.

Yerğa armi d‑yuli wass yerza ɣer wat n taddart yules‑asen ayen yeḍran, ddan‑d yid‑s ur t‑ğğin ara weḥd‑s.

Mi d‑uwḍen heggan iman‑nsen ad kksen aɣyul si lbir, inṭeq Dda lḥusin yenna: « ur ttceqqit ara iman‑nwen aɣyul sdaxxel n lbir ara ittwamḍel dayen ad nermed lbir », yeɣli‑d leḥzen ameqqran ɣef Dda lḥusin imi mačči akken i tt‑yenwa i teffeɣ, yeḍmeƐ ad yekkes lḥif n waman ɣer taggara iruḥ rruḥ d asfel. At taddart gan‑d tiwizi wa gar‑asen, uɣen‑as‑d yiwen n uɣyul i Dda lḥusin.

Suhila ǦELLIL

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Lefraq d usirem …

Qasi, d yiwen n umsedrar leɛmer neffiɣ. D afellaḥ n tmurt werǧin nekcim ar uɣerbaz : ur yessin ad yaru ula d isem‑is. Taddart‑is, d Iɣil n Tsafin, yejguglen ɣef udrar ɛlayen, yeččuren d isekla n bu tcacit ( abelluḍ) akked uzemmur. Ɣef teɣzi n wass, netta di lexla d tayessawt, afras d nnqec. Yeḥrec mačči d izli, anda yerra afus‑is ad temɣi, ad d‑tefk ṣṣaba. Yettidir akked baba‑s deg uxxam aqdim, yuɣalen d asemmḍ segmi temmut yemma‑s asmi yesɛa 6 n yiseggasen di leɛmer‑is.

Nnan‑d wat zik : «Ma kkseɣ‑ak baba‑k, ur ak‑kkiseɣ ara; ma kkseɣ‑ak yemma‑k, ur ak‑ǧǧiɣ ara». Yewɛer wuzzu n tyemmat, mi ara tesriffegt d tamecṭuḥt ad d‑teǧǧ arraw‑is d ileqqaqen, ur zmiren ara i yiman‑nsen. Ɣas ulamma, ula ababat iḥemmel tarwa‑s, meɛna ulac win izemren ad yeṭṭef amḍiq n tyemmat neɣ ad yesɛu iḥulfan i tesɛa ɣur‑sen. Akka i teḍra d Qasi, yemdeggar d wussan iwakken ad d‑yimɣur ad yizmir i yiman‑is. Teqqed‑it dunnit am ufexxar almi yewweḍ 18 n yiseggasen di leɛmer‑is. Win ara t‑iwalin ur as‑tent‑yettakk ara, yettban‑d yugar akk tizya‑s di leɛmer, ad tɣileḍ iga axxam, yesɛa arraw‑is. D lḥif d tiggujelt, i yerran aqcic d argaz deg yir lawan. Si ḥertadem almi d taggara n tefsut, d ameksa, d azeddam…yegla akk yis‑sent, ma yella deg unebdu yettṣubbu ar uzaɣar iwakken ad d‑iḥelli cwiṭ n umeṣruf ar xwali‑s, imegger timẓin d yirden deg yiɛerqyab. Mi tekfa tsemhuyt, ad d‑igerrez ttɛebga i uɣyul, mkul lxir ad as‑t‑id‑fken iwakken ad iɛemmer ikufa i tegrest.

Baba‑s n Qasi, yebda iɛeyyu, tebda‑t tewser ɣef zik n lḥal si leɛtab n dunnit. Meɛna, yesɛa zzher imi t‑yesɛa, xas yiwen n lewḥid, yeɛmer‑as axxam, iɛawen‑it di mkul ha tamsalt. Xas iɛawed zzwaǧ ɣef yemma‑s, temeṭṭut i d‑yewwi am tweṭṭuft, teṭṭef axxam terna lexla, d taɛewwajt n tfettusin, yerna tḥemmel Qasi ad as‑tiniḍ d netta i t‑yurwen. Mi d‑tebder isem‑is, tečča, tewa.

Yiwen wass, mi tekfa tmegra, Qasi yuli‑d ar taddart ɣef wudem n ssbeḥ. Mi d‑yekcem tajmaɛt, yaf‑d yekker uhetwir si lɣaci yellan deg umraḥ n taddart. Yaḥbes, yessawel i yiwen n unarag‑is iwumi qqaren Maziɣ. Yenṭeq ɣur‑s:

- A Maziɣ ! A Maziɣ
- Anɛam a gma Qasi, Acu teḥwaǧeḍ?
- Ssarameɣ d lxir kan i yellan di taddart, ayen akka d‑ffɣen akk lɣaci lawan‑agi ?
- D lxir kan a gma, ɛni ur teẓriḍ ara d tameɣra n Wezna ass‑agi, la nettraǧu iqeffafen ad d‑asen ad tt‑awin.
- Wezna! Ad teddu d tislit! Awah xaṭi! Tɣelṭeḍ a Maziɣ…
- Ayɣer a Qasi !
- Dayen ulac, ulac…tanemmirt

Qasi, mremɣent‑d wallen‑is d imeṭṭawen, mi yesla belli tin iḥemmel, yessarem ad yeg yid‑s axxam, fkan‑tt yimawlan‑is s bessif i yiwen n umaṛkanti ara tt‑id‑yesɛun d yelli‑s. Yettuɣaḍ lḥal, imi yiwen ad‑iṛebbi tayri s yiḥulfan yeṣfan, syin ad d‑yas win yesɛan cci ad yefreq ulawen s useḍmeɛ s udrim yettfakkan. Akka i teḍra d umeɣbun, ul‑nni yebḍan ɣef yemma‑s mi t‑id‑teǧǧa d amecṭuḥ, iɛawed beṭṭu ɣef tin izedɣen ul‑is. Am wakken qqaren : «  Ma mačči d lmektub, d zzher amcum i yettbeddilen tirga ».

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Qasi, kkawen yifadden‑is, iruḥ leɛtab‑is, kra yexdem yeddem‑it waḍu. Ur as‑d‑yeqqim ɣef way‑deg ara iḥir di taddart‑is, ul‑nni yebdan yettilqiq yuɣal d lqaseḥ ɣef tikkelt. Yeqqim, ittemxemmam d yiman‑is, yaf‑d ḥala tuffɣa ara t‑iselken, ara as‑isettun tidyanin yeḍran yid‑s. Yuɣal, ihedder weḥd‑s yeqqar‑as: «Tuffɣa, leɛmer ffiɣeɣ si temnaḍt‑agi nneɣ, meɛna d tiyita‑agi n Wezna ara i iyi‑yawin ad ffɣeɣ tuffɣa n ubeṛṛiq.»

Baba‑s d tmeṭṭut‑is, faqen s ssebba n unezgum n yilemẓi, meɛna aḥlil fell‑asen, imi tamsalt i iceɣben Qasi d lɛib ad hedren fell‑as, acku di tmetti n leqbayel ur heddren ara medden ɣef tayri d yimawlan‑nsen. Maca, teddun‑as di lebɣi s wayen iwumi zemren iwakken ad as‑settun cwiṭ ayen i t‑yuɣen. Maɛna, ilemẓi yefra‑tt deg uqerru‑s.

Zrin kra n wussan, yejmeɛ‑d iceṭṭiḍen‑is, yeddem‑d idrimen yeffer di tecḥiḥt‑is, yeǧǧa sslam i wat uxxam, yeffeɣ taddart‑is s leḥzen, ur d‑idewwer ara ula ar deffir. Ur yuḥtam ara ugeswaḥ. Yesɛedda 3 n wussan deg ubrid‑is ar tmaneɣt n Lezzayer, tikkelt ad iwehhi ad as‑d‑sneɣsen amecwar, tikkelt‑niḍen ad tt‑yewwet ɣef uḍar. Mi yewweḍ ar dinna, yewhem deg wayen iwala, zzhir, aɛeyyed, aṣuni n tkeryas…yeɛweq sani ara yerr, acu ara yexdem? ur yessin ula d yiwen ad as‑imel ciṭ iberdan. Yettuḥeyyer!mi yettwali d igelfan n yimdanen heddren s teɛrabt, netta ur yegzi ur yerri deg wayen isell, ur yessin ara ad d‑yessenṭeq ula d yiwen wawal si tutlayt‑nsen.

Di tallit‑nni, yuɣ lḥal adabu yexdem lbaṭel di Leqbayel, iḥerrem‑iten di tutlayt n tyemmat‑nsen, win ara d‑ihedren s teqbaylit ad t‑wwten neɣ ad t‑awin s asekraf. Qasi, yesɛa zzher imi t‑id‑iwala yiwen n uqbayli, ifaq‑as belli ur yessin ara amek tetteddu tudert di tmaneɣt. Inṭeq‑d ɣur‑s :

- Azul fell‑ak a gma!
- Azul a Mass
- Walaɣ‑k‑id ɛerqent‑ak, tɣaḍeḍ‑iyi, ladɣa mi faqeɣ belli d mmi‑s n tmurt‑iw
- Wellah! leɣmer walaɣ annect‑a segmi d‑mɣiɣ ar dunnit‑agi
- Aha kan agma, tamurt igezren yiḍan, mačči ḥala aya ara twaliḍ
- ɣur‑k kan ddu‑d yid‑i ur ttxemmim ara, ad ak‑mleɣ iberdan akken ilaq
- Ad k‑iɛuzz Rebbi, yessefti a gma

Argaz, yewwi Qasi, ixelleṣ‑as‑d imensi deg Usekwar (Le Squar), syin yewwi‑t ar usensu anda yella, yeṭṭef‑as taxxamt. lḥaṣul iɛawen‑it di mkul ha tamsalt, yefka‑as‑t‑id Rebbi d amnir deg ubrid‑is. Azekka‑nni, ffɣen‑d ar lqahwa, qqimen  ttqessiren, awal ijebbed‑d wayeḍ. Yenna‑as urgaz‑nni i Qasi: «Twalaḍ asagen‑ina ay ameddakkel! Akka sin wussan ad d‑yekcem yiwen n lbabur n yiminigen si tmurt n Fransa. Mi ara yuɣal, ad dduɣ deg‑s ad ffɣeɣ si tmurt‑a i aɣ‑yugin»

- Amek ara xedmeɣ ma truḥeḍ, nekk ur yessinen ad hedreɣ ula d awal n teɛrabt dagi
- Ma tebɣiḍ ad tedduḍ, lbabur yewseɛ yerna di Fransa tella lxedma d tudert yelhan.
- Ihi acu i ilaqen iwakken ad dduɣ?
- Teḥwaǧeḍ nnekwa akked 1000 n yidinaren, yerna ma xuṣṣen‑k ad ak‑ten‑rnuɣ, acku yettuɣaḍ lḥal ad teqqimeḍ di temdin‑agi
- Tanemmirt a gma, lxir‑ik d ameqqran

Din din, zrin sin n wussan, lbabur ameqqran yewweḍ‑d asagen. Rekben, cerrgen leḥer agrakal di kra n tsaɛtin. Qasi, yefreḥ, ur yefriḥ. Imi si tama yebda itettu uzzu‑nni n tayri i t‑yezdin d Wezna. Si tama niḍen, yemmekta‑d baba‑s, yuggad ad yemmet ur t‑yettwali …

Werdi Lyazid

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Temẓi-iw yettwarehnen

Ḥulfaɣ i wussan‑nni, lliɣ am tjeǧǧigt‑nni i d‑yeṭṭillin, ad tẓer tafat, leɛyaḍ…, lhul‑nni i d‑yettnalen timeẓẓuɣin‑iw, seḥmayen‑d idammen‑iw ɣer tuffɣa. Abrid, yezga yeččur d igerdan n lǧiran yetturaren. Akken ara d‑ldint wallen‑iw, ad d‑afeɣ iman‑iw gar‑asen.

Ah! Ay ussan n temẓi‑iw! Mraw d yiwen n yiseggasen kan ara sɛuɣ, mi d‑yekcem jeddi d jida, yid‑sen tayemmust tacebḥant. Ur d‑uwiten ula di tewwurt, almi ten‑ufiɣ kan sdat‑i. «A wiza ! Ruḥ kan els‑d iselsa‑agi ». D tazzla, ay tt‑ṭṭfeɣ ɣer texxamt. Lferḥ‑iw mi ara iyi‑d‑yawi walbeɛḍ kra, ya lukan d taḥlawant. Icettiḍen dɣa, ad d‑kkeɣ akk yis‑n taddart, ad zuxxeɣ gar tezya‑w. Ula d iḍes, rrif nsen ay gganeɣ. Ldiɣ tayemmust‑nni, ufiɣ d taqendurt tacebḥant yeččuren d ijeǧǧigen d umendil azewwaɣ « Ay acḥal lewwaɣit ! ». Ur iyi‑tewwi tmurt si lferḥ, bdiɣ ttemɛebbareɣ yid‑sen, ur asen‑ufiɣ lewhi.

Cwiṭ akka, teḍfer‑iyi‑d jida, tḍal‑d si tewwurt, dɣa tendeh i yemma «A Lǧuher ! Rwaḥ kan zwir di yelli‑m, ha‑ten‑an qrib ad d‑awḍen ».

Tusa‑d yemma, tcebbeḥ‑iyi, teqqen‑iyi ula d abruc d uzrar n sxab. Ay acḥal ferḥeɣ ! Cwiṭ akka, tekcem‑d terbeɛt n tlawin d kra n yirgazen, tessers‑d yemma lqahwa, qqimen ttqessiren. Ma d nekk, si leḥya ffreɣ deffir tewwurt ṭilliɣ‑d. Ziɣ, asmi ɣran lfatiḥa, deg uzniq ay lliɣ tturareɣ ! Mi kkren ad ruḥen, tusa‑d yemma, tḥennec‑iyi‑d, tenna : « Ttḥadar iman‑im a yelli …!». Imeṭṭawen dlen iẓri‑is. Temmeɣ‑d yiwet si gar tid d‑yusan, teṭṭef‑iyi afus, tewwi‑iyi «Ad kem‑nawi ad am‑d‑naɣ kra, ad d‑nuɣal » iyi‑d‑tenna.

Kra n lweqt, nekcem axxam ur ssineɣ, wwin‑iyi ɣer texxamt, rran‑d fell‑i tawwurt, ǧǧan‑iyi‑d yelli‑tsen i yellan d tizya‑w, tetturar yid‑i s uzrar‑nni i icebbḥen taɛenqiqt‑iw. Mi d‑tewweḍ tmeddit, ha‑t‑an yekcem‑d urgaz s unyir ikersen, ad yili iɣleb baba di leɛmer. « Nekk d argaz‑im»Iyi‑d‑yenna. D aya kan i sliɣ, maca, ur fhimeɣ d acu i yebɣa ad iyi‑d‑yini, terkeb‑iyi tuggdi d tergagayt, uɣaleɣ cbiɣ kan itbir‑nni mellulen iwumi rẓan tiferrawin, sersen‑t rrif n wasif.

Ttɛeddin wussan d yiseggasen, nekk yal ass d imeṭṭi, tiɣimit‑iw metwal ṭṭaq. Ssawaleɣ i yemma, ad d‑tas ad iyi‑tawi « Mačči d kemm ara lummeɣ, ɣlayit yimeṭṭawen‑nni inem i d‑smarent wallen‑im ass‑n, nekk yid‑sen nemyehdar. Maca, s yixef n jeddi d jida, i yerran timedlin ɣef temẓi‑w, ard n‑uɣaleɣ !» I cennuɣ yal mi ara d‑yaweḍ yiḍ. Ass yessawal i gma‑s, asirem‑iw yettneqḍaɛ. Ɛerḍeɣ ad rewleɣ acḥal d tikkelt, maca, abrid ɣer uxxam nneɣ ur t‑frizeɣ, ttarran‑iyi‑d si gar yiberdan. Imir i ẓriɣ, tebrek tessa‑d i temɣer‑iw. Ṣṣut‑nni n lḥara ideg d‑kkreɣ urǧin yeǧǧi timeẓẓuɣin‑iw. Yuɣal wurar‑iw, d isewwi ɣef yisɣaren, d tarda n yicettiḍen, d uẓu n tebḥirin iyi‑d‑yesmektayen s leqdic n yemma i bdiɣ si temẓi, ula d lmal ttawiɣ‑ten ɣer lexlawi ad ksen, maca, tamɣart, dima rrif n uqerru‑w.

Tilemẓit‑nni, yeẓẓan asirem‑is di tewwurt, tin akken yettnadin leslak, tuɣal, truḥ‑as lbenna n tudert, tuɣ tannumi d zzher‑is uɛwij i iruḥen d asfel n leɛwayed d lqella n Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
tmussni. Ixser lxaṭer, urɛad yessin iman‑is. Uɣaleɣ d tameṭṭut n uxxam, akka iyi‑d‑qqaren. Bdiɣ ttizmireɣ i ttɛebgat yesseknayen d lḥif yeṭṭabaɛen iɣes. Mi ssawḍeɣ mraw d ṣa n yiseggasen di leɛmer‑iw, tusa‑d tebrat i wergaz‑iw, ad yunag ɣer tmurt taberranit.

Ass‑n i as‑sliɣ i umɣar‑iw yenna‑as « Ad n‑teqqimeḍ aseggas di Fransa, ilmend n yizen‑agi i k‑id‑yewwḍen ». Din din tenbeddal liḥala‑w. Ur ẓriɣ d acu ay d‑walan s udem‑iw, ɣlin‑d yimeṭṭawen, maca d imeṭṭawen n lferḥ, ur ẓriɣ ma ad t‑id‑iniɣ, xas akken ahat, d lɛib « Tuɣal‑iyi‑d tlelli‑iw! ». Tuɣal‑iyi‑d terwiḥt amzun akken acḥal aya seg‑i teffeɣ.

Ḥulfaɣ i tefses deg tnefsit‑iw, yertaḥ wul‑iw « Ad ruḥeɣ s axxam nneɣ, ad d‑ẓreɣ imeddukal n uzniq nneɣ, ad caliɣ berra » I nniɣ deg yiman‑iw.

Yezri umalas ɣef rrwaḥ n urgaz‑iw, yusa‑d baba ad iyi‑yawi, ad ɛawneɣ yemma, ad tger aẓeṭṭa. Mi nekker ad d‑neffeɣ, tendeh temɣart‑iw fell‑as: « Nniɣ‑ak anef‑as kra n wussan meqqar ɣur‑wen, ad tesgunfu, simi ara ruḥeɣ ɣer wetma ad d‑tuɣal ad d‑tezgi deg uxxam ». Mi wwḍeɣ s axxam, yennecraḥ‑d wudem‑iw, maca mi ffɣeɣ ɣer berra ur ufiɣ tizya‑w ukkud lliɣ tturareɣ, imi tettwamḍel temẓi‑nsent urɛad d‑kfin yiferrawen‑is s ucerraq d ubeddel n yinan, am temẓi‑iw, yettwagezmen ur temmid.

Urɛad yewwiḍ useggas mi d‑yewweḍ lexber n lmut n urgaz‑iw, mmaren‑d yimeṭṭawen deg yiẓri‑w, iɣaḍ‑iyi, imi ziɣ bdiɣ ttaɣeɣ tannumi yid‑s ur ẓriɣ, uɣaleɣ bdiɣ fehhmeɣ d acu ay d zzwaǧ, d acu ay d axxam‑nni iyi‑teqqar jida ad t‑terreḍ.

Yebda usmekti yettuɣal‑d, amzun d acelyaḍ i itettin isebtar n wayen sɛeddaɣ deg wallaɣ‑iw s lemɣawla. Sḥassfeɣ, sḥassfeɣ ɣef lɣiba‑s akken sḥassfeɣ ɣef temẓi‑w yettwaɣedren.

IMADUCEN Linda

Ayen yuran

Azwaw rzaget ddunit fell‑as, imi yemma‑s temmut, akked d zzwaǧ n baba‑s da Rezqi d temeṭṭut d tamaɛurt tesarwa‑as lemaḥna, ur telli ara deg umḍiq n tyemmat, diɣ d zzwaǧ n ultma‑s Faḍma sennig lebɣi‑s d umɣar. Netta igzem‑itt di rray iruḥ, yezger ilel s ttawil n lḥerraga, yeǧǧa akk ayen yessaram acku ul‑is yeččur am teqarɛet n lgaz seg uqbaṛ.

Zrin wussan Azwaw atan deg wakal n Fransa deg yir liḥala am umeslub, ur yezri ara anda ara iger iḍarren‑is, si tesebḥit almi d tameddit ala yettnadi axeddim ma deg yiḍ yeggan seddaw n teqenṭert, yettidir tudert n tuffra mi iwala kan imsulta ad yerwel amkan d amakraḍ. Yewwas atan yufa‑d axeddim di leqahwa yefreḥ atas acku bab‑is d aṛumi d azuran, yestewḥic, imi tiwala s tudert‑nni iḥeqqer‑it, yall ass yekkat‑it s wawal yeqqar‑as: « xedem neɣ ad k‑siwḍeɣ ɣer yimsulta, macci tettidireḍ tudert taberkant ad tarnuḍ asemusken.»

Azwaw yeqqar deg ull‑is yewwi‑iyi‑d kan ad sebreɣ, yewwas tella tukarḍa aran‑tt‑id fell‑as seyin akkin amɛellem yessawel i yimsulta, Azwaw yeǧǧa‑t almi yeɣfel kan yerwel‑d, yettazal yeqqar: « ukt ukt selkeɣ seg umcum‑inna ».

syin akkin teruḥ‑as‑d tikti nniḍen ta‑agi d zwaǧ d trumit s ciṭ n yidrimen i yesɛa, atan yufa‑d yiwet isem‑is Jusifin d tazurant, d tameɣert, ṣut‑is d areqaq, alamaɛna tɛemel‑it tewwi ‑as akk idrimen‑nni seg assen ur d‑ban. Almi d yewwas ileḥḥu deg ubrid yettnadi axeddim am yall ass, atan yemlal‑d sin yemɣaren udem‑nsen d acebḥan, deg‑sen laman, qeḍan‑d, yenna‑asen: « ma ad ken‑ɛiwneɣ » ihi qeblen, yekcem deg ull‑nsen yettidir ɣur‑sen, ɛwenen‑t atas atas ɣef lekwaɣed.

Iɛedda useggas yussa‑d ɣer temurt s wudem nniḍen, inuda ɣef ultma‑s Faḍma, yufa‑tt deg yerr liḥala arran‑tt d taxeddamt, yennuɣ yennuɣ almi is‑d‑yebra, diɣ iruḥ ɣer baba‑s yezra‑t‑id ideleb‑as‑d semaḥ xas akken tameṭṭut‑is mazal‑itt kan akken am ɛezrayen.

Asmi iyi‑d‑yules wuzwaw yenna‑iyi‑d: « ta‑agi i taqsit‑iw, xas akken mačči akken sarameɣ ad idireɣ acku aql‑i ttidireɣ deg Fransa d temeṭṭut‑iw d ultma Faḍma attan la teqqar, diɣ akked d tafat n ddunit‑iw tagi d yelli iwumi semmeɣ Wezna ɣer yemma ɛzizen aṭas, aqli tidireɣ deg leferḥ, d axeddam, mi celheɣ tamurt terruḥuɣ‑d ».

deɣa waleɣ ‑t yettaḍsa, yecmumeḥ, yefreḥ.

Bulus Azwaw

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Liy akked Ili

Yiwen akken wungif yettmeyyiz weḥd‑s weḥd‑s, isteqsay deg yiman‑is acu ara yeḍfer di tudert‑is: yesmenyaf gar tilin d ssɛaya neɣ gar umdan yelhan neɣ win yesɛan. Yeɛweq acu ara yefren. Yeqqim akken ittemɛebbar d ṛṛay‑is acḥal, igguma ad as‑yaf ixef‑is.

Yiwen n was tusa‑as‑d ɣer yixef‑is tekti. Ad iruḥ ad isteqsi igellil d umerkanti, ahat ad as‑tt‑id‑frun rnu ad iḥṣu s tedmi n yal yiwen.

Yaɣ lḥal akken i yexdem. Iruḥ iqsed tikkelt tamenzut, Ameṛkanti. Acu i as‑id‑yenna: “Argaz neɣ amdan yeswa ayen yesɛa d wayen ila. Ma ulac, ihi kečč d ulac. Ma yella lǧib‑ik yeččur, isem‑ik mechuṛ; ma yella lǧib‑ik yexla, ad k‑rekben medden am uɣyul.”

Ungif iserreḥ kan akken i yiman‑is, ibren tikli yenna‑as “ad waliɣ ziɣ Igellil. Yesteqsa‑t yerra‑as‑d: “Amdan yeswa s wayen yellan deg‑s d afrayen metwal wiyaḍ. Ma tettḥulfuḍ s tlufa yerzan imdanen, s yiɣeblan n wiyaḍ, aqel‑ak seg wat talsa.”

Ungif meskin ɛerqent‑as akk, snat n tririyin ur msadant ara akk, yiwet deg usammer tayeḍ deg umalu, ur yelli wassaɣ ara ten‑yarzen?. Ikemmel abrid‑is, imugger‑d kra akken n umeksa, inher‑d lmal‑is, yettraju tineggura ad d‑qeḍɛent. Ungif yekna ɣer lqaɛa, iddem‑d takemmict n wakal, ittmuqul‑itt ileḥḥu, yaweḍ s ameksa yesteqsi‑t:

- Deg leɛnaya‑k ay argaz‑agi ma ur iyi‑d‑tenniḍ acu n wazal I tla tkemmict‑agi yellan deg ufus‑iw?.
- Gar ciṭ d waṭas: almend n waken yella wakal; ma yesɛa ttra (yenwa wakal), imɣi ad yaf iman‑is, ad yimɣur ad yennerni. Meɛna ma yeqqur, aman ffɣen‑t, anwa imɣi ara yeɣren i tudert, lmal‑a acu ara iniwel? Wama ccbaḥa n uḥriq, fiḥel ad nmeslay fell‑as.

Imir‑n, ha‑t‑aya uferṭeṭṭu yekka gar‑asen, ameksa isikkid deg tfulki‑s, yeldi imi‑s yecmumeḥ, hwan‑as yiɣman n yiferrawen‑is. Ungif‑nni yemmeɣ yeṭṭef‑it‑id akken ad t‑iwali mliḥ, din din isuɣ‑d fell‑as umeksa‑nni:

- Anef I uferṭeṭṭu d yuwi waḍu ad yidir, ur yelli d ayla‑k! Wagi d aferdis seg ugama, d mmi‑s n twennaḍt.
- Arju! Bɣiɣ kan ad t‑waliɣ, daya!
- Twalaḍ tura! Ma d awali kan, ur yuḥwaǧ ara tuṭṭfa, d wa i d Tilin; ma d arruz ara t‑tarzeḍ, tesfunngeḍ‑as tilelli, wa I d seɛɛu.

Ungif yebra i uferṭeṭṭu, isuter asuref, dɣa yenna‑as‑d Umeksa: “a mmi, akken ad nidir ilaq ad nesɛu axeddim akked ciṭ n ttawil iwulmen ara yalellen amdan i Tilin. Maca Timesɛiwt n waṭas, tsadar Tilin, acku nnig lewqama d tiwuɣa. Tuget n ssɛaya tsawal i 3
