# Tutlayt n umaḍal n yimal

Yiwen wass tameddit, seld imekli; am wakken nuɣ tannumi, qqimeɣ d twacult‑iw nettwali yiwen usaru di tiliẓri n tmaziɣt, azwel‑is “tutlyt n umaḍal n yimal”. Akken kan, yebda, truḥ trisiti dɣa nessens tilivizyu. Rniɣ cwiṭ, ffɣeɣ ɣer ufrag ad iyi‑d‑yewwet ubeḥri, qqimeɣ din almi i d‑yeɣli ṭlam ur husseɣ i wakud amek i yessenser, si thuski n tugna iyi‑d‑ibanen. Ttuɣ iman‑iw, zedreɣ di tsussmi i tegled tebrek n yiḍ, ddiɣ di lebɣi i umaḍal n yitran.

Qqimeɣ ttwaliɣ itran ttwalin‑iyi‑d nekk ttxemmimeɣ ɣef usaru‑nni, gar ddqiqa d tayeḍ ad d‑yebreq yiwen gar‑asen amzun yebɣa ad iyi‑d‑yini kra. Wehmeɣ, ur ẓriɣ ma d tidet neɣ d targit, ttawiɣ kan lewhi s wallen; bdiɣ ad ten‑hessbeɣ; ggumeɣ ad ten‑qeḍɛeɣ, ṭṭuqten mačči yiwen mačči sin d imeyyaten ur nkeffu ara. Mi iyi‑yeɛreq leḥsad ad ɛawdeɣ d acu kan d awezɣi! ttɛawadeɣ, ttɛawadeɣ… almi dayen ɛeyyiɣ. Serseɣ aqerru‑iw ɣer tmurt refdeɣ‑t‑id, d ayen yessewhamen ɣaben yitran‑nni! din tsebeddi‑yi‑d tuggdi?. Cwiṭ kan akka ha‑tt‑a tafat tezzi‑d am tagut, tɣum akk ayen yellan, temmundel tegnawt azal n 10 ddqayeq.

Imir kan uɣalen‑d yitran‑nni, d acu kan tikkelt‑a yal itri yura fell‑as usekkil, dewwiren di tegnawt wa deffir wa, yal tikkelt ad iɣab yiwen, alami i d‑qqimen kra seg‑ses. Isekkilen‑nni banen‑d deg yiwen n uzrig am wina i xeddmen igerdan uqbel ad kecmen ɣer tesmilt, ssuffɣen‑d tanfalit‑a. D acu i d‑yuran? ẓriɣ ur tettamnem ara, akken kan kkreɣ ad d‑ɣreɣ tanfalit‑nni, iruḥ‑d yiwen n ṣṣut: yenna‑d “tutlayt n umaḍal n yimal”; ha‑t‑a wayen id‑yuran di tenfalit‑nni.

Cwiṭ kan akka, walaɣ kra n yimdanen, wa d imicbiḥ wayeḍ d imibrik, wa d aɣezzfan, d awezzlan, lḥaṣul mgaraden. Inṭeq yiwen yenna‑as: “azul”, wayeḍ yerra‑as‑: “Amek i tettilim” wayeḍ, wayeḍ…, ttutlayen s tmaziɣt. Deg usmenɣer n tiṭ ufiɣ‑d iman‑iw gar‑asen, dɣa nnan‑iyi‑d: “Ansuf yis‑sem, aqel‑ikem deg umaḍal n uzekka”; rriɣ‑as “d acu‑t daɣen umaḍal‑agi n uzekka”; ttaḍsan; ttemyexzaren gar‑asen; imir Inṭeq‑d yiwen “d amaḍal n tallit urɛad nedder”, wahmeɣ! Amek! urɛad neddir!?; amek yeɛni? “Yenna‑yii‑d: “kra leqrun ɣer sdat, asmi ara d‑taweḍ tallit‑a, agdud d yiwen; ad d‑yefrir seg yiwen n uẓar, ad yedder sufella n tegnawt, ad yutlay kan yiwet n tutlayt”, din mmekteɣ‑d asaru‑nni walaɣ “tutlayt n umaḍal n yimal”; imir suɣeɣ d anti‑tt? Yemmeɣ ɣer lǧib‑is, yejbed‑d taferkit deg‑s yettwaru uḍris d aɣezzfan: “tutlayt n umaḍal n yimal d yiwet gar tutlayin ttutlayen yimsawalen yeddren di tmurt, gar tutlayin timenza i d‑yesneqren deg yimi n yimawlan‑is, imezdaɣ‑is ttidiren di tefriqt n ugafa, tlul‑d ass 950 n yiseggasen uqbel talalit n sidna Ɛisa; yinar neɣ yennayen d ixef n useggas, uqbel ad kemmleɣ taɣuri, uɣaleɣ srid ɣer uzwel n uḍris‑a, yeswehem‑iyi!? “Tamaziɣt d tutlayt n umaḍal n yimal”.

Akken kan zziɣ ad kemmleɣ taɣuri n uḍris‑nni, ha‑tt‑a yemma tekkat‑iyi‑d6 gar tuyat, teqqar‑iyi‑d: “yaɛni dagi ad teṭṭseḍ”, dɣa dduqseɣ‑d seg tergit.

Qqimeɣ ttxemimeɣ; ččurent wallen‑iw d imeṭṭi, menneɣ ayen zriɣ di target ad yili d tidet, maca tidet‑nni ad teqqim d target; ula d targit ad teqqim d target.

SAƐDI Zuhra.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Tamurt n Leqbayel, deg useggas n 3000 !

Deg useggas n 3000, rziɣ ar taddart ufiɣ‑tt tbeddel, tbeddel aṭas mačči d kra, ayen akk yellan d tajaddit ihudd lsas‑is, ayen akk bnan imezwura yeɣli. Yal ci ibeddel udem, nettwali kan nessusem, agama ibeddel udem. Yeɣli‑d ddel, imi yezzem, iẓri yemmundel. Tullas yettmagaren tafsut ḥejbent deg yixxamen, tettru tefsut imi ur tent‑wala ara, ulac tinna ara tt‑yemmagren, ulac tid ara yeglilzen deg yigran, ijeǧǧigen negren, tuɣal d anebdu aɣurar deg wulawen n yimdanen.

Taddart‑nni i deg iyi‑teɣli timiṭ; acḥal n yiseggasen‑aya ur tt‑twali ara tiṭ; ǧǧiɣ tettru. Tettru, ttruɣ imi tt‑ufiɣ tbeddel. Ur tt‑εqileɣ ara, ur d‑ufiɣ ara iman‑iw sdaxel‑is. Ǧǧiɣ‑tt, am nekk d yimdukal; neǧǧa amkan d ilem i wid‑n i as‑ibeddlen udem. Udem n taddart‑nni zeddigen, εzizen ɣef wallen. Tifelwiyin sebɣen inaẓuren di tesgiwin n ugni qecrent, mḥant. Izenqan‑is d ilmawen, ssewḥcen... neǧǧa‑tt, neǧǧa ilem ṭṭfent wid i as‑ibeddlen udem, yeqqur ujeǧǧig n usirem.

Ufiɣ irgazen ɣeḍlen tajmaεt. Ufiɣ‑ten wa yugad, wa yessagad; beddlen akk iselsa, ǧǧan akk ičumar, ǧǧan tamart yellan d azamul n trugza n urgaz Aqbayli. Wiss‑n ma bessif neɣ d lḥif, wiss ? Qqimen‑d at nnif uɣalen di rrif, sexlaεen akk wudmawen‑nsen, win d‑yeldin imi‑s, ad t‑rren deg yidis.

Ruḥeɣ s aɣerbaz‑nni i deg ɣriɣ, waleɣ igerdan ṭṭfen tilwiḥin seddaw tɣerdin‑nsen, fettun, qqimen ɣef tgertilt lsan tacacit.

Ɛeddaɣ‑d abrid n tala, zik yettačar d tullas, tura yexla, yuɣal d lexla. Teḥzen tmila asmi i as‑hudden tala. Acercur yeqqur, asariǧ d ilem. Abrid‑is swadda s ufella yul‑it inijjel d tmetwala. Dayen yergel, ibeddel udem, agama i yicennun yessusem, ifrax nnejlan qqimen ala iẓiwcen d yitbiren.

Uliɣ ar tzeqqa n tiddukla tadelsant, ufiɣ tawwurt‑is temdel, ur d‑yeqqim ula d yiwen umddakkel, yal ci din ibeddel. Anda akken ncennu tizlatin, anda akken netturar amezgun yuɣal d lǧamaε. Tamekerḍit‑nni yeččuren d idlisen yuli‑tt uɣebbar d ucebbak n tissist, di tencirin‑ines ur d‑yeqqim ara ula d yiwen udlis.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
D tutlayt-iw i ferneɣ gar tutlayin Mi lliɣ qqareɣ deg tesdawit n Mulud Meɛmmri n Tizi Wezzu, zedɣeɣ deg yiwet n teɣremt iwumi qqaren ILE, u qqaren‑as d aɣen tiɣremt n Diduc Murad, ttidireɣ di talwit ɛedleɣ akked tnelmadin yellan dina, ulac anta iyi sseluɣen aman, dɣa tameddakult‑iw Nura n tizi ɣenif tella di yal akud ɣer tama‑w, leɛmer nemgarad ɣef kra n tɣawsa ayen akk ara as‑iniɣ ad ay‑t‑aɣ awal, tezga tetteddu d rray‑iw, ula d nekk akken. Ur zemireɣ ara ad as‑xedmeɣ ayen n diri, netett akken neddukul akken, nesseɛday uḍan deg uqqeṣar d unecraḥ yal tikelt anta deg‑nteɣ ara yeruḥen ɣer tzeqqa n tayeḍ.

yiwen n wass neqqim deg tzeqqa‑inu deg yiḍ nettmeslay ɣef kra n tɣawsiwin iccuden ɣer leqraya, dɣa awal yettawwi‑i d wayeḍ almi newweḍ ɣer tamesalt n tutlayin. Nniɣ‑as: « A weltma tutlayt n tmaziɣt d lmexyer gar tutlayin, ulac anta tutlayt i d‑yekkan s nnig‑s. » Tessusem kra n wakud tenṭeq‑d ɣur‑i tenna: «Ala a weltma deg waya‑agi ur ddiɣ ara d rray‑im, tutlayin tibeṛṛaniyin i d‑lmexyer gar tutlayin. »

Nniɣ‑as : «Amek akka?! ɛiwed‑d kan d acu i d‑tenniḍ! » Tenna‑d: « Ara am‑qqareɣ d tutlyin tibeṛṛaniyin i d‑lmexyer. » Rriɣ‑as: « Wagi d awezɣi dayen ur iqebbel leɛqel. Ihi ulac tutlayt i d‑yekkan nnig n tutlayt‑iw tayemmat tmaziɣzt, u yernnu d acu i am‑d‑fkant aka tutlayin tibaṛṛaniyin?. »

Terra‑i d: «Tutlayin tibaṛṛaniyin fkant‑iyi‑d assirem i tuddert‑iw, yis‑sent i yezmeraɣ ad aẓeɣ ɣer sdat, d tidan ara yissuffuɣen ɣer tafat, ayen akk i yebɣiɣ ad txeddmeɣ yis –sent, ma yella ixuṣ wumdan deg‑sent ulac d acu i yessen. » Nniɣ‑as: «Awah a Nura taxemmam‑agi‑inem ur yella ara deg umkan‑is , ulac tutlayt i d‑yekkan s nnig tutlayt‑iw tamaẓiɣt xas ulama ssuffuɣen‑t tutlayin niḍen ɣer tafat, tutlayt tayemma‑tt d nettat i am ‑xedmen ifadden si tlallit‑im almi d assa n wussan.»

Terra‑i d: « Ur tzemiraḍ ara akk ad ayi‑teqqenɛaḍ. D acu i aɣ‑ d‑tefka tutlayt tayemma‑tt!?, nettmeslay‑itt kan seg ugar‑nneɣ deg uxxam.» Wahmeɣ deg wayen selliɣ yuli‑ d wul‑iw.

Nniɣ‑as : « A Nura a weltma aṭas n tɣawsiwin ur tessinaḍ ara ɣef tutlayt‑im.» Terra‑i d s teḍsa : « D acu akka ur issineɣ kulci zerriɣ‑t ulac d acu yettwafaren.» Nniɣ‑as: « Ihi aṭas n tɣawsiwin i yefran ur ten‑twaleḍ ara sell‑i d ad ten‑tissineḍ.»

Deg tazwara tutlayt n tmaziɣet d tutlayt tayemma‑tt, d tutlayt tamezwarut ara ad yelmed umedan seg wasmi i d ‑yekker meẓẓi almi d asemi ara yimeɣur. Yettisin teqbaylit is‑it‑d‑luɛan imawlan‑is mi i d‑ilul almi d asemi ara yekcem ɣer uɣerbaz , dina ad yebdu yettisin ilugan n tutlayt‑agi, amezruy‑is, tasekkla‑ines, tasenalsit, tajeṛṛumt.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Rennu ɣur‑s yal aɣref di ddunit yettmeslay tutlayt‑is, ur yettak ara fell‑as afus ladɣa deg wudem n yemccumen i as‑d‑yezzin yal tama akken ad teɣḍlen.

Tutlayt tayemmat d tasellalt iǧehden i ugdud‑is akken ur iɣelli ara, yis‑s i nezmer ad nerr negab ɣef yiman‑nneɣ ma taǧhed tutlayt‑nneɣ ur ad yettes ara win ara aɣ‑iḥeqqran, neɣ win ara aɣ‑yawwin deg yir abrid.

Teneṭeq‑d ɣur‑i tenna‑d: « Ula d tutlayin tibaṛṛaniyin sɛan azal, acku aṭas n tmussniwin ara ad ternuḍ, ma yella tessnaḍ tutlayt n tmurt tabaṛṛanit ur d‑tafeḍ ara uguren ɣer sdat xas ulama telliḍ tezedɣeḍ deg tmura‑nsen.»

Rriɣ‑as: « Wagi d awezɣi tettxemmim‑am kan ɣef tuffɣa ɣer tmura tibaṛṛaniyin, tutlayt‑nwen ur as‑tgam ara azal, tettnad‑im ad d‑tissin‑am tutlayin niḍen, lukan add‑tmuqqeleḍ s tmuɣli igerrzen ad tafeḍ d akken tutlayt tayemma‑tt d allal n taywalt, d tuget n yizamulen, d tamerkanit di yal taɣult tineqqiṭ ɣur‑s azal, ajerriḍ n tuqna ɣur‑s azal, asekkil, tussna, amawal amerkanti, u yerna ula d tutlayt tamaziɣt tessuffuɣ ɣer wayen yelhan, u tezmereḍ ad teffeɣeḍ yis‑s.»

Teqqim tettxemmim tuɣal terra‑i d: « Ula d tutlayin tibaṛṛaniyin ad teklaḍ fell‑asen‑t ma yella tekesbeḍ tamusni‑nsen‑t ad akk selkan‑t di yal taɣult, acku yis‑sent i tettdu tdamsa, lumur n ddunit akk atenin deg ufus n tmura tibaṛṛaniyin yuẓan ɣer sdat di yal taɣult, ɣer wanda i ten‑tariḍ awwin‑d iman‑nsen, ladɣa ma truḥaḍ ɣer tmurt n Marikan ma yella ur tessineḍ ara tutlayt taglizit ur tettselikeḍ ara ɣur‑sen.»

Wahmeɣ deg‑am a Nura: «Ur am denniɣ ara ur nettisin ara tutlayin tibeṛṛaniyin, lamaɛna a nezwir di tutlayt tayemma‑tt d tina i d‑aferdis n tuddert‑nneɣ, d nettat i d‑tajjadit, fell‑as i yemmuten aceḥal d ilemẓi. D timudrusin tutlayin ibeddan ɣef yiɣalen‑sen‑t am tutlayt n tmaziɣt, u yerna d tutlayt n Ccecnaq, Yugurten, Massensen, Dihiya, Tineḥinan. Tutlayt n tmaziɣt s laɛteb d tiddi n yimussnawen am Dda Lmulud Maɛmri, Bulifa, Dallet,...atg. D wigi itt‑i d‑jemɛen, i as‑igan azal am nettat am tutlayin nniḍen i d‑yufraren.»

Ma nemuqqel ass‑a ɣer tmura n medden merra fkant azal i tutlayin‑nsen, i yimyura i d‑yessuffuɣen idlisen ara affent tsutwin i d‑teddun, xedmen akken ara as‑ nernin idles‑nsen.

Walli merra timura yettwaqdmen ṭṭefan di tutlay‑nsen, ayen i ten‑yeǧǧan simal taẓen ɣer sdat, yettnerni rebeḥ‑nsen, ssiwḍen ullin ɣer waggur, ɣef waya‑a ilaq ad aɣ‑d‑yess nnif ula d nnukni ur nettbeddil ara tutlayt‑nneɣ s tutlayin nniḍen, anect‑agi d lessas n unegmu n talsa, d lsas n tɣerma.»

Ɣer taggara am ad‑inniɣ sin wawalen ur am‑d‑rennuɣ ara: « Ma yella tenekreḍ tutlayt‑im nneker ula d yemma‑am i kem‑i d‑iseɛan.»

Tessusem ciṭuḥ tenna‑i d: «D tidet ayen akka iyi d‑tenniḍ terriḍ‑i d ɣer leɛqel‑iw, d tutlayt‑iw i d‑tamezwarut ɣef tutlayin tibaṛṛaniyin.»

Akken beɣun‑t seɛun‑t azal tutlayin nniḍen, tutlayt tayemma‑tt ad tilli i d‑lmexyar d tamezwarut i ɣef yennadi wemdan, acku ma ulac tutlat‑ik tettwakkes‑ak tudert‑ik d nnif‑ik.

AYT BENƐLI Cahrazad.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Zik‑nni deg tmurt n Yiqbayliyen

di tallit‑nni mi ttutlayen yiɣrwsiwen, yella yiwen unegmar n yiselman, ssawalen‑as Aksil, di tudert‑is 35 iseggasen. Anegmar‑agi i tteffeɣ ɣer yilel, yal tanzayt, yettuɣal‑d tameddit n wass, deffir n uɣelluy n yiṭij. Ittidir s wayen i d‑igemmer. Mi d‑yeṭṭef kra n yiselman ad ten‑yezzenz, d tadrimt‑nni i d‑yettawi seg yiselman i ittserrif deg tudert‑is. D win kan i d‑aɣrum‑is, akken i ixeddem yal ass.

D acu‑t wass‑nni am wansayen‑is Aksil anegmar, yekker‑d send tafrara, yeffeɣ s teflukt‑is, i d‑yesnulfa s yiskla n teẓgi. Yewwi yid‑s tacmuxt yeččur‑itt d aman, mi ifud ad isew, yerna yewwi yiwet n tegrabt deg‑s kra n yifessasen n tazart, d zzit n uzemmur, mi yelluẓ ad yeṛz laẓ‑is, rnu ɣer waya ilel islaẓzẓay nezzeh, ɣas seɣli‑d učči seg tegenawt.

Aksil yewweḍ ɣer wanida ara d‑yegmer, ur iɛeṭṭel ara iḍegger acebbak‑is, am yal tikelt yettraǧu amer ahat ad yeččar, neɣ xerṣum ad yeṭṭef ayen ara yessenz seg yiselman. Akud izerri, tacebbakt‑nni ur tembawel ara. Anegmar yuɣen tanummi yettaṭaf‑d iselman, yerǧa yerǧa ulac, d ayen yuyes seg uraǧu, yerna akud iɛedda, drus i mazal ad d‑teɣli tallast.

Yenna deg yiman‑is, ad jebdeɣ kan acebbak‑inu, ad d‑ffɣɣeɣ s teflukt‑inu, azekka ad d‑uɣaleɣ, wissen ahat ad yaki sseɛd‑iw.

Anegmar Aksil yeddem‑d acebbak‑ines, mi t‑d‑yessers deg teflukt, yufa yedda‑d deg‑s yiwen n uslem d amecṭuḥ, yefṛeḥ, yecmummeḥ, yenna: "Meqqaṛ ur teffaɣeɣ ara s yifassen‑iw d ilmawen. Yerna ɣas aslem‑agi d amecṭuḥ, ad yelhu, ad t‑wteɣ ɣef tirgin, mi d‑yewwa ad t‑ččeɣ..."

Din din ineddeh‑d uslem amecṭuḥ, yenna i unegmar Aksil: "Awah a mass, ur yelli d acu ara d teččeḍ deg‑i, aqli‑i meẓẓiyeɣ maḍi, ur k‑seṛwuyeɣ, ur yi‑t‑znuzuḍ ad as‑tiniḍ ad trebḥeḍ kra n tedrimt. Meqqar err‑yi ɣer waman, xerṣum aseggas neɣ sin, uɣal‑d ṭṭef‑iyi‑d, ma terriḍ ad yi‑teččeḍ yella d acu ara teččeḍ deg‑i, ma tzenzeḍt‑iyi ad rebḥeḍ idrimen s waṭas, ad tafeḍ deg wacu ara ten‑tesqedceḍ, ad ak‑id‑awin lfayda d tameqqrant ..."

Anegmar Aksil, yebda yettxemmim, yufa d tidet i as‑d‑yenna uslem‑nni amecṭuḥ, maca ikcem‑it lḥir. Acḥal d iseggasen nettat deg yilel urǧin teḍra‑as tedyant am tagi, ad yuɣal s yifassen d ilmawen. Ixemmem tallit, iger‑d nnehta, yeddem‑d lmus‑is, ixdem yiwet n tecreḍt s uzamul (ⵣ) i uslem‑nni amecṭuḥ i yellan gar yifassen‑is, syin yebra‑as ɣer yilel, yessegra‑d awal, yenna: "D tidet i d‑tenniḍ ay amecṭuḥ, maca ɣas ur k‑ččiɣ ara nekk, ad k‑yečč kra n uslem ameqqran din deg yilel, ma ur tmeččeḍ ara ahat ad nemlal kra n wass, ihi ḥṛec uɣal‑d".

Yerra‑as uslem‑nni: "D tidet ay anegmar, ahat ad yi‑ččen yiselman‑nniḍen akka i d‑tenniḍ, maca acimi i yi‑tweccmeḍ s lmus, yak teẓriḍ ad teqqim d ccama deg tfekka‑w ? Yeḍsa unegmar Aksil, yenna i uslem amecṭuḥ: "Cerḍeɣ‑ak i wakken ad cfuɣ fell‑ak, yerna, akken ara tettimɣureḍ ad yettimɣur yid‑k uzamul‑nni. Ǧǧiɣ‑ak talwit ay aslem amecṭuḥ".

Akli MUHUBI.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Imessukal n Bremen

Yella zik yiwen urgaz, yesɛa aɣyul i ixedmen fell‑as d iseggasen armi i d‑yewweḍ wass i t‑ǧǧant tzemmar, yuɣal simmal yettaẓay i uxeddim. Dɣa bab‑is yebda ittxemmim ad ihenni iman‑is seg‑s maca aɣyul iḥulfa kan yella wayen ur nessefraḥ, ihi yerwel, yeṭṭef abrid ɣer temdint n Bremen². « Dina meqqar zemreɣ ad uɣaleɣ ad amẓawan³ n temdint », i yenna deg ul‑is.

Akken yella ileḥḥu, yemlal‑d deg ubrid yiwen n uqjun n ssyaḍa i yeẓẓlen deg ubrid, ittqezmimmir am win yeɛyan.

— D acu i k‑yuɣen tettqezmimmireḍ akka ay amdakel ? i t‑yesteqsa.

— Iiih ! i s‑d‑yerra uqjun, a niɣ tura ɣliɣ d amɣar yerna ineqqes lǧehd‑iw yal ass armi uɣaleɣ ur zmireɣ ad dduɣ ɣer ssyaḍa, daymi yebɣa ad yi‑yenɣ baba‑iw, dɣa rewleɣ‑d ; maca amek ara xedmeɣ tura akken ad d‑ḥelliɣ aɣrum‑iw ?

— Ihi nekk aql‑i tedduɣ ɣer Bremen akken ad uɣaleɣ d amẓawan, i s‑yenna uɣyul ; yya ddu‑d yid‑i ad tgeḍ akken ula d kečč, nekk ad kkateɣ lɛud, kečč d tiqerqabin.

Yeqbel dɣa uqjun, kemmlen akken lwaḥi. Syin, rnan kan ciṭuḥ, ufan‑d yiwen n wemcic iɣef iban leḥzen.

— D acu i d‑yeɣlin akka fell‑ak ay amcic ? i t‑yesteqsa uɣyul.

— Ulamek ara ihenni yiwen ma yugad ɣef uqerruy‑is, i s‑d‑yerra umcic ; acku tura mi ttaẓeɣ deg leɛmer, bdant rekkunt tuɣmas‑iw, uɣaleɣ ḥemmleɣ ad qqimeɣ ɣer yiri n lkanun kan wala ma ttazzaleɣ deffir iɣerdayen, dɣa mi tebɣa ad yi‑tḍeqqer lal‑iw ɣer waman, rewleɣ‑as‑d, maca tura amek ara geɣ, sani ara rreɣ ?

—Yya‑d yid‑neɣ ɣer Bremen ; kečč d tessneḍ‑as i uẓawan n yiḍ, meqqar ad tuɣaleḍ d amẓawan n temdint am nekni.

Amcic iɛǧeb‑as rray, yekker yedda yid‑sen. Syin ur ɛeṭṭlen ara imennaṭriyen kkan zdat yiwen n wefrag anda walan ayaziḍ yuli ɣef tewwurt tameqqrant, yeɣɣar seg ayen i d‑yewwi.

— A tesɛuẓẓgeḍ‑aɣ a wayi ! i s‑yenna uɣyul, acimi tettsuɣeḍ akka yeɛni ?

² D tamdint deg Lalman.

³ Amẓawan : win i d-iceɣlen d uẓawan (musicien).

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
— Lliɣ mmaleɣ‑d kan addad n tegnawt i wass usired iceṭṭiḍen, i d‑yerra uyaziḍ ; maca imi llan yinebgawen ara d‑yasen ass n lḥedd, attan lal n wexxam‑a teqqar‑as i tḍebbaxt‑is ad yi‑tezlu azekka iwakken ad yi‑yeččen, ma d tura aql‑i la ttruɣ kan.

— Yerbeḥ a bu ucerur azeggaɣ ! i s‑yenna uɣyul ; ihi yya‑d kan ad tedduḍ yid‑neɣ ɣer Bremen axir ma nɣan‑k da. Aql‑ik tesɛiḍ taɣect tgerrez, ad ternuḍ ad tcebbḥeḍ meqqar tarbaɛt uẓawan ara nessali.

Ayaziḍ iɛǧeb‑it usumer, dɣa qelɛen akken deg rebɛa. Maca imi tamdint n Bremen ur d tin ara awḍen deg yiwen wass, kkan kan deg yiwet n tiẓgi, kecmen ad nsen din. Aɣyul d uqjun ẓẓlen ddaw yiwet n ttejra, amcic d uyaziḍ ulin ɣef ifurkan‑is, yerna ayaziḍ ikemmel yefferfer ɣer yixef‑is akken ad yili i laman. Dɣa uqbel ad yeṭṭes, akken yella yettmuqul akka d wakka, ikad‑as‑d iwala yiwet n tafat tamecṭuḥt ɣer lebɛid ; ihi iɛeyyeḍ, yenna i irfiqen‑is ahat yella kan kra n wexxam deg leqrib‑nni imi d‑tettban ṭṭya.

« Ma yella akken, i yenna uɣyul, ɣas kkret kan ad nruḥet s tɣawla ɣer tama‑nni, acku nekk azebriz‑a⁴ ur yi‑d‑yeɛǧib ara yakk. » Yerna uqjun ileqqem‑d deg awal‑is : « D tidet, acu ara rnuɣ ma ufiɣ kra n yiɣes d ciṭuḥ n weksum ! »

Rran ihi metwal amkan anda i d‑tettbin tneqqiṭ‑nni n tafat, syin ur ɛeṭṭlen ara walan‑tt simmal a tetteflali tettimɣur, armi wwḍen ɣer zdat yiwen n wexxam ixennaben i yeḍwan akken ilaq. Dɣa imi d netta i d ameqqran, iɛedda uɣyul yeccelbeb ɣer ṭṭaq ad imuqel ɣer daxel.

— Acu tettwaliḍ ay aɣyul ? i t‑yesteqsa uyaziḍ.

— Acu ttwaliɣ ? i s‑d‑yerra uɣyul ; atta da ṭṭabla teččur d učči d tissit si yal lxir, teqqim‑as‑d terbaɛt ixennaben a tetten s lecraha.

— D ayen ara ɣ‑yelhun i nekni, i yenna uyaziḍ.

— Iban ! i d‑ileqqem uɣyul ; awufan din i nella !

Qqimen ihi ttemcawaṛen amek ara ssufɣen ixennaben‑nni syin, ɣer tagara ufan‑tt‑id. Dɣa ata uɣyul ibedd ɣef sin iḍarren ineggura iɛerrec ɣer ṭṭaq, aqjun yuli‑d ɣef uɛrur‑is, amcic ineggez‑d ɣef uqjun, ayaziḍ yufeg yers ɣef uqerru n wemcic. Mi ifat bedden akken, msefhamen, bdan a cennun ɣef tikelt : aɣyul yesreɛruɛ, aqjun yesseglaf, amcic yesmiɛiw, ayaziḍ yeɣɣar ; syin aten‑a ẓedmen seg ṭṭaq ɣer texxamt, armi iɛad zzaj i d‑rẓan yettafeg d iceqfan. Ma d imakaren akken kan slan i dderz‑a yesserhaben, bedden‑d

4 Azebriz : asensu amecṭuḥ i yettilin deg iberdan iḍulen, ɛennun-t medden i wučči, i usgunfu neɣ i yiḍes (auberge).

akk  s  ddihcan,  ɣillen  d  kra  i  sen‑d‑yekkren  deg  tzeqqa‑nni,  dɣa  ṭṭfen  tarewla,  wwin
tallaɣṭa ɣer tiẓgi. Imir rebɛa‑nni n yerfiqen qqimen‑d ɣer ṭṭabla, ɣlin ɣef ayen i d‑yegran
ad s‑tiniḍ ɣur‑sen ayyur ur ččin.

Akken mi fukken, imẓawanen ssensen tafat, ruḥen nudan‑d anda ara ṭṭsen, yal wa akken
yennum d wamek i s‑iwulem. Aɣyul iruḥ yeṭṭes ɣef leɣbar yellan deg ufrag, aqjun deffir
tewwurt, amcic ɣer yiri n lkanun ideg yeḥma yirrij, ma d ayaziḍ yuli ɣef yiwet n tgejdit ;
dɣa  imi  ten‑tuɣ ɛyan  seg  tikli,  ur ɛeṭṭlen  ara  yewwi‑ten  nadam.  Mi  ineṣṣef  yiḍ,  aten‑a
imakaran  i  d‑imuqlen  seg  lebɛid,  dlan‑d ɣef  tafat  yensan  deg  uxxam‑nsen  yerna  iban‑
asen‑d  kulci  yerked,  ihi  yenṭeq  umeqqran‑nsen,  yenna  :  «  Awah,  ziɣ  neɣleḍ  i yeǧǧan
iman‑nneɣ  nettwaḥaḥi‑d  akken  »,  yekker  yumeṛ  urbaɛ‑is  ad  ruḥen  ad  d‑sfeqqden  i
uxxam‑nni.  Win  i  iceyyeɛ  mi  yewweḍ,  yaf  kra  ur  yembawel,  yekcem  dɣa ɣer  tkuzint
akken  ad  yessiɣ  tafat,  yekkes‑d  aɛeqqa  n  zzalamiḍ,  ihi  mi  yeẓra  allen  n  wemcic  i  d‑
iceɛlen deg  ṭṭlam, iɣill d irrij,  yessuẓ ɣur‑sent aɛeqqa‑nni akken ad  t‑id‑izenned,  maca
ɣer umcic mačči d aqeṣṣer,  ineggez‑d  din  din  ɣer  wudem‑is,  ixbec‑it.  Argaz  i  teṭṭef
lxelɛa u ad yazzel ɣer tewwurt ad yerwel ; maca ata uqjun yellan igen din kan sdeffir,
yerrubbi‑t  fell‑as,  ikerrec‑it  deg  uḍar  ;  syin  mi    iɛedda  deg  ufrag  ɣer  yiri  n  leɣbar,
yettasseɛ fell‑as uɣyul iṣukk‑it ṣṣekk arehbani, ma d ayaziḍ tuɣ yuki‑d yakan ur yeɣfil s
lḥess‑nni yakk yekkren, iɛad ihi yeɣɣar ɣef tjegdit‑is : ququɣuuq, ququɣuuq..

Amakar yuzzel seg ayen i d‑yewwi ɣer umeqqran, yenna‑yas : « Attan din deg uxxam‑
nneɣ  yiwet  n  temkerrert    tucmit  i  d‑isuḍen  fell‑i  terna  texbec‑iyi‑d  deg  udem  s
waccaren‑is iɣezfanen, zdat n tewwrt d argaz i yeṭṭfen lmus iwet‑iyi‑d yess ɣer uḍar, deg
ufrag ibedd yiwen n wemẓiw  d aberkan i d‑iḥerrken fell‑i s tehrawt, ma ɣef ssqef d jjuj
i yulin, sliɣ‑as la yeqqar : “Awit‑iyi‑d ɣer da ambaṣ‑nni !” Daymi i d‑rewleɣ sellkeɣ‑d
iman‑iw. »

Seg  imir  ur  qdifen  yixennaben  ad  uɣalen  s  axxam‑nsen,  ma  d  imẓawanen  n  Bremen
ufan iɛǧeb‑asen lḥal din, dɣa ugin akk ad d‑ffɣen.

Samir Tiɣzert

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Tamacahut n Yeḥya izrem d Muḥ ubexsis

Macahu! Tamacahut‑iw ad telhu, ad tiɣzif annect n usaru. Zik‑nni, rrif n teẓgi ẓḍan yiskla, llan sin watmaten, Yeḥya izrem d Muḥ ubexsis, yal wa yettidir d twacult‑is tamezzyant.

Yiwen wass, iruḥ Yeḥya izrem ɣer teẓgi, am wakken ixeddem yal ass, ad d‑iqedder kra n usɣar i lkanun, neɣ ad d‑yekkes kra n lɣella yufa, ihi, ass‑n yesseɣzef cwiṭ amecwar, almi d talemmast n teẓgi, simmal yettqerrib, simmal isell i leswat… yuẓa ar sdat iwala atemmu d ameqqran, dlen‑t yisekla n lfakya yal d ṣṣenf, d ayen ur iwala di leɛmer‑is!

Argaz yeffer deffir yisekla ittḥessis, cwiṭ kan akka, ha‑ten‑an ffɣen‑d ṣa n yiwaɣezniwen. Mi kkren ad ruḥen, yenṭeq umeqqran deg‑sen: « Ɣleq a lbab, ɣleq a tawwurt! » Tawwurt ha‑tt‑a teɣleq‑d, imir‑n kan ṭṭfen abrid nsen ruḥen.

Yeḥya izrem, iḍfer‑iten s yiẓri almi ur tezmir tiṭ ad ten‑teqḍeɛ. Yekker iruḥ srid ɣer tewwurt, kkes‑d amek ur yeɛriḍ, tgumma ad d‑teldi. Kra n wakud, argaz yuɣal s axxam‑is.

Azekka‑nni ssbeḥ, yuɣal, yeḥder i tewwurt mi teɣleq, iruja almi d‑uɣalen mi yeɣli yiṭij, wwḍen‑d ɣer tewwurt, yesla i ṣṣut yendeh « Fteḥ a lbab fteḥ a tawwurt! » Tawwurt teldi, nutni kecmen.

Yeḥya izrem yal ass yettuɣal almi i iwala akud ideg tteffɣen keččmen yiwen‑is. Almi d yiwet n tikkelt, iruḥ, ikcem ɣer utemmu, igugem seg wayen ẓrant wallen‑is, yal d lxir yella; ṣa n tbaqyin n seksu, ṣa n yigduren n waman, ṣa n tjeɣlin, tiwiztin, lḥaṣul dayen ur yeẓri di ltudert‑is.

Yeḥya izrem, yečča‑d akk tijɣelt si al tarbut, yeswa‑d yiwet tejɣimt si yal abuqal, tacriḥt tacriḥt si yal tabaqit, yeddem‑d cwiṭ n twiztin akken ur as‑ttfaqqen ara. Yal ass ad yexdem akken almi d yiwet tmeddit, iceggeɛ tameṭṭut‑is tewwi‑as‑d amud seg uxxam n gma‑s, akken ad yektil yis‑s, iwzen tiwiztin‑nni, mi t‑yerra tedda yiwet lqaɛ‑is ur ifaq.

Akken tt‑yufa gma‑s iruḥ‑d srid ɣer‑s. Argaz yeḥres‑it almi i as‑d‑yenna tidet, yekker yewwi‑t almi d amkan, yessefhem‑as‑d akk amek i ilaq ad yexdem akken ad d‑yawi lxir mebla ma ṭṭfen‑t syin uɣalen‑d s axxam.

Muḥ ubexsis ur yezmir ad yesber, azekka‑nni tafejrit, yewweḍ s atemmu, yerǧa almi ffɣen yekcem ɣer daxel, yeɛweq ansi ara d‑yebdu, yečča, yeswa, almi ur yezmir ad iḥerrek, yekker yerfed‑d tacekkart n twiztin. Kkes‑d amek ur yeɛriḍ ad tt‑yerfed ur yezmir ur ixemmem ad yawi kan cwiṭ, yebɣa rrbeḥ deg yiwen wass.

Akken d‑tewweḍ tmeddit yesla i ṣṣut n yiwaɣezniwen, yeẓra ulac tarewla. Iruḥ yeẓẓel iman‑is gar lǧessat n wid yemmuten akken ur as‑ttfaqqen ara. Cwiṭ akka kecmen‑d, yekker yenṭeq umecṭuḥ deg‑sen: « Heemm! A baba… ! Ass‑a nesɛa inebgawen!

‑ Ulac inebgawen a mmi!

‑ Heemm nniɣ‑ak a baba… ! Nesɛa inebgawen!

Awaɣezniw amecṭuḥ yeqqim yettales‑d i wayen d‑yenna, akken almi kkren ad nadin, ufan kullec yenqes, ttin‑d akk atemmu, almi wwḍen ɣer lǧessat‑nni, sserɣen aseffud bdan neǧǧɛen deg‑sent, akken wwḍen ɣen Muḥ ubexsis yuɣwas. Din din zzin‑d fell‑as am umeqyas, mi t‑yeṭṭef wa ad yejbed seg‑s kra, ad as‑d‑yessiwel wayeḍ ad as‑yini: « Rwel‑d ɣur‑i ad k‑ḥaddeɣ! ». Ad yerwel ɣer‑s ad yeclex seg‑s tacriḥt. Akken akken almi d‑yedda leɛmer‑is, jjan‑d afwad‑is ɛellqen‑t ɣef wuskum.

Azekka‑nni, iruḥ Yeḥya izrem ɣer uxxam n gma‑s, yesteqsa fell‑as tameṭṭut‑is, tenna‑as: « Seg yiḍelli mi yeffeɣ tafejrit ur d‑iban » Yeḥya izrem yeẓra anda yella « Nniɣ‑ak ur tezmireḍ ara!

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Nniɣ‑ak ! »  i  yenna  d  yiman‑is.  Din  din  yeṭṭef  abrid  s  wurfan  srid  ɣer  utemmu‑nni,  mi  ffɣen yiwaɣezniwen,  yufa  afwad  n  gma‑s  yettwaɛelleq  mazal  yettqudur  d  idammen,  iger‑it‑id  ɣef tuyat‑is yerra‑d s axxam.

Cwiṭ  akka,  yewwet‑it  wugur  yeɣli,  iwala  tabuzlegrayezt  tettɣummu  timiqwa‑nni  dɣa  seg wurfan isabb‑itt, dɣa yessenṭeq‑d Rebbi tabuzlegrayezt‑nni : «  Huuk !!   Nwiɣ  sergel  sergel, ihi tura  sekfel sekfel ».   tekker tessekfel‑d akk tid termel , d ayen yeǧǧan iwaɣezniwen ad ẓren abrid  yuɣ  win  yewwin  afwad‑nni.  Yekker  umeqqran  deg‑sen  yeddem‑d      sdis  n  yiyeddiden, issames‑asen zzit sufella, yessekcem yal awaɣzeniw ɣer yiwen ma d  netta yelsa iselsa n ssayel, iruḥ amzun d win ara yessenzen zzit, yeqsed axxam n Yeḥya izrem iɣer tewwint tmiqwa‑nni.

Kra  n  wakud  yewweḍ  yid‑s  iyeddiden‑nni,  yesṭebṭeb  s  axxam  n  wuḥric‑nni,  yeffeɣ‑d  netta  d yelli‑s d tmeṭṭut‑is, dɣa yenṭeq uɛeṭṭar :

- Usiɣ‑d ad ssenzeɣ zzit ma ad taɣem, maca, tura, yeṭṭef‑iyi lḥal ma ad tessensem inebgawen n Rebbi.
- Mreḥba yis‑k ! inebgi n Rebbi, d inebgi nneɣ.

Waɣzen yekcem s yigeddiden‑is, cwiṭ akka, truḥ teqcict ɣer yemma‑s tenna‑as : «  A yemma ! Mudd‑iyi‑d tissegnit neɣ amessak,bɣiɣ ad fluɣ cwiṭ ayeddid‑inna, ad d‑geɣ cwiṭ n zzit i uqerru‑iw »  Tmudd ‑as yemma‑s amessak, truḥ tessenta‑t  deg uyeddid‑nni amecṭuḥ, din din yeffeɣ‑d ṣṣut si daxel : «  A baba ṭṭsen ! Nekker nečč‑iten ? ». Netta yuɣ lḥal waɣzen iweṣṣa arraw‑is, mi ten‑yenǧeɛ,  ad  d‑ffɣen  ad  ten‑ččen. Taqcict, d tazzla ɣer  baba‑s,  tules‑as‑d  ayen  tesla.  Yeḥya izrem yeḥṣa ayenni, yufa‑d lḥal ihegga‑asen ttawil iwulmen. Yekker yessuter di tmeṭṭut‑is  ad tawi yelli‑ s,  ad truḥ s axxam nsen. Uqbel ad truḥ, thegga‑asen imensi igerrzen daxel n ugrur n berra yeččuren d asaɣur.  Uḥric  yessawel‑asen ad ččen imensi, mi kecmen yerra fell‑asen tawwurt  si  berra,  yuli  ɣer  usfaylu  ,  yesmar‑asen  lgaz  syin  iḍegger‑as  taxellalt.  Kra  n  timar, agrur yerɣa akk, ddan daxel‑is yiwaɣezniwen‑nni, maca, yegra‑d umecṭuḥ deg‑sen yemneɛ.

Yeḥya  izrem,  yeɛweq  amek  ara  yexdem,  awaɣezniw,  mazal  mecṭuḥ,  akken  ad  t‑ineɣ  iɣaḍ‑it. Ixemmem, yenna d yiman‑is : «  Nekk arrac ur sɛiɣ ara, wagi urɛad yessin. Ad t‑rebbiɣ amzun d mmi, ad as‑settuɣ laṣel‑is ». Ihi irebba‑t, yettimɣur d yelli‑is amzun d gma‑s. Almi d yiwen wass,    yettwaɛreḍ ɣer  tmeɣra  n  tlalit  n ṣṣebyan  di  taddart,  yekker  yewwi  awaɣezniw‑nni.  Mi wwḍen, iserreḥ‑as ad yurar d warrac, imi ṣṣifa‑s amzun d lɛebd, ma d netta yezha d wat taddart, ccḍeḥ  ṭṭbel  d  lɣiḍa.  Akken  zhan  deg  wurar  i  yezha  uwaɣezniw  di ṣṣebyan‑nni,  yuli  ɣer‑s  ar dduḥ yečča‑t akk.

Tekfa  tmeɣra,  Yeḥya  izrem,  yerra‑d  mmi‑s  ɣef  tuyat‑is,  iga‑as  čuɛella.  Akken  bdan  abrid yenṭeq: A baba aqrur‑nni ɣef waydeg yeḍra dihdih ɣeẓẓaɣ‑t si tfednin almi d qriruc.

‑   Maɛlic a mmi, ḥader kan ad as‑tɛiwdeḍ. Netta yeẓra acu ara yexdem Ihi kemmlen abrid‑nsen. Simmal leḥḥun, aẓɣal, yettzad, imeẓẓaɣ n urgaz, ttizwiɣen. Cwiṭ akka, yenṭeq  waɣzen :  «   A  baba !  timeẓẓuɣin‑ik  zeggaɣit… !  A  wi  tent‑iɣeẓẓan… ! ».  Din  din, uḥric ,  yuki‑d si ttexmam ideg  yezder ,  imi d‑yufa belli, d aweẓɣi  ad  yettu wuccen tigad‑is, yenna    deg‑yiman‑is : «   Ihi  akka,  Rebbaɣ‑d  izrem  s  iri‑w !  Ma  d  tter  n  gma    rriɣ‑t‑id  deg yimawlan‑ik, ma d tura, tasa‑w,  ad tt‑ meḍleɣ, ad rreɣ fell‑as timedlin». Yerna cwiṭ n tikli almi yewweḍ ɣer yiwet n ticcewt meqqren, yeṭṭef‑it seg yiḍarren yewwet‑it ɣer‑s yenɣa‑t.

Tamacahut-iw tekfa, uḥric ,ad tt-isif, ungif, ad tt-yerr di rrif.

Sɣur Massa IMADUCEN Linda

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Mḥend d Mḥend

A macahu tamacahut-iw ad telhu, ad tt-iɣzif am uɣeddu, ad teḍbeɛ am usaru. Yella yiwen urgaz zik‑nni, temmut tmeṭṭut‑is, teǧǧa‑as‑d aqrur qqaren‑as Mḥend. Ur iɛeṭṭel ara urgaz yeɛɛawed jwaǧ, yewwi‑d tameṭṭut, yerna yesɛa‑d yid‑s aqcic, tefka‑as isem Mḥend. Mḥend d Mḥend yiwen n yisem, yiwet n tugna‑nsen, tt‑myaken anzi am snat n tmiqqwa n zzit. Tameṭṭut t‑zedɣ‑itt tismin, tettasem ɣef warbib‑is, mi ara asen‑d‑ffk imekli neɣ imensi, tḥemmel ad tefk amur n lɛali i mmi‑s, maca, tuɣal ur t‑ɛeqqel ara anwa i d arbib‑is, anwa i d mmi‑s.

Truḥ s amɣer azemni, teḥka‑as tenna‑as: « A baba amɣer, ini‑id amek ara ɛeqleɣ mmi ». Yenna‑as: « Mi ara d‑sserseḍ ad ččen, mi d‑wwḍen yizgaren ruḥ ad ten‑id‑qqneḍ, synna akin ɛeggeḍ ini‑as: « ayuh a mmi ameɛzuz, a nekk nɣan yizgaren. », Arbib‑im ad d‑yecɣel d lmakla‑ines, mmi‑m ad n‑yazzel, imiren qqen‑as tageṭṭumt i umeẓẓuɣ‑is akken ad t‑ttaɛqaleḍ ».

Tameṭṭut tuɣal‑d s axxam, texdem ayen i as‑d‑yenna umɣar azemni. Seg wasmi i as‑teqqen tageṭṭumt i mmi‑s, tɛeqqel‑it, tuɣal tettḥiz‑asen aɣrum. Mi ara kksen, mmi‑s‑nni tettak‑as aɣrum n yirden, ma d arbib‑is tettak‑as aɣrum n ureɣli.

Yiwen wass ruḥen kksan, qegglen deg yiwen n lɛinsar, mi ruḥen ad ččen imekli, kksen‑d aɣrum‑nni, yenna‑as Mḥend abujil i gma‑s:

- Yyaɣ agma, yal yiwen deg‑neɣ, ad i ḍegger talqimt n uɣrum‑is ɣer lɛinsar‑agi.
- Winna n yirden yezzer ɣer lqaɛa, acku ẓẓay. Winna ureɣli ffsus, yuli‑d ɣef waman.
- Yenna‑as wali agma ɣer telqimt‑iw akken d tuli, akkihin id uliɣ ɣef wul n yemma‑k. Ma d kečč akka tezzer telqimt‑ik i tezzerḍ deg wul n yemma‑k. Ihi teẓriḍ agma:
- Nekk ur tt‑uɣaleɣ ara yid‑k s axxam, kečč ruḥ uɣal ɣer yemma‑k. Aqleɣ ad neẓẓu aseklu deg umkan‑a, sfiqid‑d ɣur‑s, ma tufiḍ‑id aseklu‑a yettreɛriɛ, ḥesb‑iyi garzeɣ s tezmert‑iw. Ma tufiḍ‑d aseklu‑a warreɣ neɣ sellaw ḥesb‑iyi uḍneɣ. Ma tufiḍ‑d aseklu‑a yeqqur, ḥesb‑iyi mmuteɣ.

Mḥend yezzi s axxam, Mḥend abujil yewwi abrid icerreg tiẓgi, ileḥḥu ur yeẓri sani i teddu. Yemlal‑d ameksa n tɣeṭṭen yettru, yenna‑as:

‑D acu akka k‑yuɣen, ayen akka tettruḍ a winnat ?

Yerra‑as‑d umeksa‑nni yenna‑as:

‑Yenɣa‑iyi wuccen, yal ass i tett‑iyi aqelwac.

Yeqqim yid‑s, ɛussen uccen‑nni, akken d‑yuɣal, yekker Mḥend yenɣa‑t. Yefreḥ umeksa‑nni yenna‑as:

‑Tanmirt‑ik, gulleɣ ar k‑fkeɣ d aqelwac.

Yerra‑as Mḥend yenna‑as:

‑Mačči ass‑a, ar asmi ara d uɣaleɣ.

Ikemmel Mḥend abrid‑is, yemlal‑d ameksa n wulli yettru, yenna‑as:

‑D acu akka k‑yuɣen, ayen akka tettruḍ a winnat ?

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Yerra‑as‑d umeksa‑nni yenna‑as :

‑Yenɣa‑iyi wuccen, yal ass i tett‑iyi ikerri. Yeqqim yid‑s,  ɛussen  uccen‑nni,  akken  d‑yuɣal,  yekker  Mḥend  yenɣa‑t.  Yefreḥ umeksa‑nni yenna‑as :

‑Tanmirt‑ik, gulleɣ ad k‑fkeɣ d ikerri.

Yerra‑as Mḥend yenna‑as :

‑Mačči ass‑a, ar asmi ara d uɣaleɣ.

Ikemmel Mḥend abrid‑is, yemlal‑d ameksa n yizgaren yettru, yenna‑as :

‑D acu akka k‑yuɣen, ayen akka tettruḍ a winnat ?

Yerra‑as‑d umeksa‑nni yenna‑as :

‑Yenɣa‑iyi yizem, yal ass iẓeddem‑d ɣef yizgeren‑iw. Yeqqim yid‑s, ɛussen izem‑nni, akken d‑yuɣal, yekker Mḥend yenɣa‑t. Yefreḥ umeksa‑nni yenna‑as :

‑Tanmirt‑ik, gulleɣ ar k‑fkeɣ d agenduz.

Yerra‑as Mḥend yenna‑as :

‑Mačči ass‑a, ar asmi ara d uɣaleɣ.

Ikemmel abrid‑is i teddu, alarmi yewweḍ ɣer yiwet n taddart. Taddart‑nni sɛan tala, yal aseggas, alamma tečča amdan ad ternu ljefna n seksu ara ad tefk aman. Netta ass‑nni d nnuba n yelli‑s n ugellid. Yeqqim di tejmaɛt, alarmi i tt‑iwala tɛedda‑d tewwi‑d ljefna teččur d seksu ɣer tala‑nni netta yelluẓ iruḥ ad yečč, tenna‑as :

‑Ala ! tura ad d‑ffeɣ tlafsa ad tečč seksu‑a ad iyi‑ternu nekki, akken tala ad d‑ffek aman neɣ ma ulac ur d tettak ara.

Yerra‑as yenna‑as :

‑Aha tura ! anef‑iyi ad ččeɣ, mi tt‑twalaḍ tessufuɣ‑d aqerruy‑is nnal‑iyi‑d.

Akken i d‑tuki tlafsa‑nni, tebda tessuffuɣ‑d aqerruy‑s, taqcict‑nni tuggad yettru, tuggad ad as‑tini i Mḥend. Nngin imeṭṭawen‑is ɣef uqadum n Mḥend yekker iwala talafsa‑nni tessuffeɣ‑d aqerruy‑is, yemmeɣ yekkes‑as‑t ; Tenna‑as :

‑Mači d wagi i d aqerruy‑iw, yella wayeḍ

Yerra‑as Mḥend yenna‑as :

‑Nekk mačči d tagi i d tiyita‑w.

Terna tessufeɣ‑d aqerruy‑is wiss sin, yemmeɣ yekkes‑as‑t, tenna‑as :

‑Mači d wagi id aqerruy‑iw, yella wayeḍ

Yerra‑as Mḥend yenna‑as :

‑Nekk daɣen mačči d tagi i d tiyita‑w.

Mi  as‑yekkes  aqarruy  ad  tessuffeɣ  wayeḍ,  mi  as‑yekkes  aqarruy  ad  tessuffeɣ  wayeḍ, alarmi  i  as‑yekkes  7  iqerray.  Temmut  tlafsa,  tala  tfeggeḍ  d  aman.  Taqcict  twala  tasebbaḍt tenser‑d deg uḍar n Mḥend, tewwi‑tt yid‑s, tuzzel tekcem s axxam, teḥka‑as i baba‑s. Mḥend yezzi ar tejmaɛt yeqqim.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Lɣaci walan yelli‑s n ugellid i mi terwel, ttɛeǧǧiḍen qqaren :

- ‑Ass‑agi yelli‑s n ugellid tuggad, trewl‑d d acu ara nessew.
- Lɣaci ggunin ɣef tewwurt n uxxam n ugelli. Yeffeɣ‑d ugellid ɣur‑sen yenna‑asen :

I mi wwḍen ɣer tala, ufan acercur yettgenniz talafsa temmut, lɣaci uzlen wwin‑as isalli i ugellid.

Agellid yenna i at taddart :

- ‑Wagi yenɣan akka talafsa‑agi, ad as‑ffkeɣ yelli.

Awal yewweḍ akk lɣaci. Lɣaci yal yeqqar : « d nekk i tt‑yenɣan ».

Tenṭeq teqcict ɣer baba‑s tenna‑as :

- ‑H‑a‑tt‑aya a baba tsebbaḍt n wwin yenɣan talfsa, tenser‑as i mi i as‑i‑tekkes iqerray. H‑a‑tt‑an kktil‑asen‑tt akk i at taddart, win iwumi d tezga d win.

Irgazen akk n taddart wa deffir wa akken ad kktilen tasebbaḍt‑nni, wa tɛedda‑t wa iɛedda‑tt, ulac i win iwumi d tezga. Yenṭaq yiwen deg yixeddamen n ugellid yenna‑as :

- ‑Mazal yiwen d inebgi n Rabbi, h‑a‑t‑an di tejmaɛt i yeqqim.

Ssawel‑as i Mḥend, iruḥ‑d yektal tasebbaḍt‑nni, tezga‑as‑d, d ayla‑s. Agellid yefka‑as yelli‑s, xedmen tameɣra n sebɛa wussan d sebɛa wuḍan. Agellid yefka‑as i Mḥend aɛewdiw, ssin wuccayen, ssin lbizan yerna‑as tamegḥelt, yenna‑as : « H‑a‑tt‑an tmurt akk inek, segged anda tebɣiḍ anagar tamadaɣt‑ina d‑yezga akin i wasif. ».

Iɛedda wayen iɛeddan, Mḥend yetseggid anda yebɣa, tamurt akk ines, maca yebɣa ad iẓer ayen i as‑yegdel ugellid tamadaɣt‑nni, yebɣa ad iẓer d acu yellan deg‑s.

Yiwen was iruḥ yudaf ɣer tmadaɣt‑nni, i mi yewweḍ ɣer dinna, yufa tezdeɣ deg‑s ttaryel. I mi t‑id‑wala tenna‑as : « Ansuf yis‑k a Mḥend mmi ɣer tmurt‑iw, ɛeddi qqen uccayen‑ik, ternuḍ lbizan‑ik d uɛewdiw‑ik, teyyaḍ s axxam ad neqqim. »

Akken i ad ten‑yeqqen dayen, yekcem s axxam n tteryel, tečča‑t. Mḥend yeɛraq acḥal n wussan ur iban s axxam, agellid yessufeɣ iserdasen‑is ad t‑id nadin.

Gma‑s‑nni seg yal ass netta yettruḥ ɣer lɛinsar‑nni akken yessefqad i useklu‑nni. Ass‑nni yufa‑t werraɣ, yenna‑as : « yella d acu yuɣen gma, ha‑t‑an ihi ! ur uɣaleɣ s axxam ».

Yewwi abrid‑is ileḥḥu. Yewweḍ ɣer umeksa n tɣeṭṭen, iwala‑t‑id, yenna‑as‑d :

- ‑A Mḥend, yyaɣ ad tawiḍ aqelwac‑ik.

Netta ad as‑yerr, ad as‑yini :

- ‑Anef‑as ar d‑uɣaleɣ

Yegza syenna i iɛedda gma‑s, ikemmel abrid‑is, yewweḍ ɣer umeksa n wulli iwala‑t‑id yessawel‑as‑d, yenna‑as‑d :

- ‑A Mḥend, yyaɣ ad tawiḍ ikerri‑k.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Netta ad as‑yerr, ad as‑yini :

‑Anef‑as ar d‑uɣaleɣ

Yegza syenna i iɛedda gma‑s, ikemmel abrid‑is, alarmi yewweḍ ɣer umeksa n yizgaren iwala‑t‑id yessawel‑as‑d, yenna‑as‑d :

‑A Mḥend, yyaɣ ad tawiḍ agenduz‑ik.

Netta ad as‑yerr, ad as‑yini :

‑Anef‑as ar d‑uɣaleɣ

Yegza syenna i iɛedda gma‑s, ikemmel abrid‑is, alarmi d i mi yewweḍ ɣer taddert‑nni, yeqqim di tejmaɛt ad yesgunfu. Walan‑t lɣaci n taddart ruḥen ɣer ugellid nnan‑as :

‑Ay agellid, aḍeggal‑ik, Mḥend, ha‑t‑an di tejmaɛt yezdew.

Yerra‑asen‑d, yenna‑asen ini‑t‑as ad d‑yass.

Iruḥ ɣer ɣur‑s lɣaci nnan‑as : « A Mḥend, yenna‑ak ugellid yyaɣ s axxam. »

Iruḥ yedda d lɣaci‑nni, yegza syenna i iɛedda gma‑s, i wwḍen ɣer ugellid yenna‑as‑d :

‑D acu akka i ak‑yeḍran, aɛni ɛarran‑k, ukren‑k, kkess aɣbel i yiri‑k, kksen‑ak aɛewdiw ak‑teɛɛiwdeɣ, kksen‑ak tamegḥelt, ad ak‑tt‑ɛɛiwdeɣ, kksen‑ak uccayen ad ak‑ten‑ɛɛiwdeɣ… Yegza syenna i iɛedda gma‑s, syenna iɛedda gma‑s.

Agellid yefka‑as aɛewdiw yerna‑as tamegḥelt d sin wuccayen d sin lbizan, yeɛɛawed yenna‑as :

‑H‑a‑tt‑an tmurt akk inek, segged anda tebɣiḍ anagar tamadaɣt d‑yezgan akin i wasif.

Yegza ɣer dinna ay iruḥ gma‑s. Azekka‑nni yeddem aɛewdiw‑is d tmegḥelt‑ines yezzwer ssin wuccayen‑is d sin lbizan iruḥ icerreg tiẓgi. Twala‑t‑id tteryel tenn‑as :

‑Ansuf yis‑k a Mḥend a mmi ččiɣ‑t iḍelli ilul‑d ass‑a…

Yegza d tteryel i yeččan gma‑s. Tenna‑as :

‑Qqen uccayen‑ik, ternuḍ lbizan‑ik d uɛewdiw‑ik, teyyaḍ s axxam ad neqqim.

Iɛedda yurez uccayen‑nni s yiɣri, mačči s umrar, yenna‑asen :

‑Mi iwen‑d‑ssawlaɣ :  « aḥerremram, azerremram, ay arraw n aɣrib anda tella‑m », ad d‑zedmem  ɣef  tteryel,  ad  tt‑feqrem  ad  telli‑m  aɛebbuḍ‑is,  maca  ḥader‑t  ayen  illan  deg  uɛebbuḍ‑is.

Yekcem Mḥend s axxam, dɣa tkemmecit tteryel, Mḥend yessawel i wuccayen‑ines.

Uccayen jebden, yedda‑d yeɣri‑nni deg yimegraḍ‑nsen, snesren, zeddmen ɣef tteryel.

Gezren‑tt, fetken aɛebbuḍ‑is, dɣa ufan akk ayen akken tečča. Yessufeɣ‑d Mḥend gma‑s d uɛewdiw‑is yerna‑d sin wuccayen‑is d sin lbizan‑is, iḍelqin dinna deg ufrag n tteryel, yeṭṭaqef deg‑sen nnefs. Mḥend yeqqim s idis n gma‑s yettru, iwala snat n tzermemmuct zdat‑s ttnaɣent, yiwet tenɣa wultmas‑s, inṭaq ɣer ɣur‑s, yenna‑as :

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
‑Ruḥ akem‑id‑ɛezzin, teḍra yid‑m akka am nekk.

Terra‑as‑d tzermemmuct, tenna‑as :

‑Nekk, nɣiɣ‑tt s ufus a yeffus, ad tt‑id yaḥyu ufus azelmaḍ.

Truḥ tewwi‑d imɣi, teddez‑it teẓẓemi‑as‑t i wultma‑s ɣef tanzarin‑is, tuki‑d. Dɣa Mḥend iruḥ ula d netta yekkes‑d imɣi‑nni, yeddez‑it yeẓmi‑t ɣef tanzarin n gma‑s akk d uɛewdiw‑is d sin wuccayen‑is akk d sin lbizan‑is, dɣa ukin‑d.

Dɣa kkren‑d akk wwin abrid‑nsen ɣer uxxam n ugellid. I mi wwḍen ɣer ugellid, yewhem deg‑sen, Mḥend d Mḥend kifkif‑iten, ttaken anzi am snat n tmeqwa n waman, yiwet n tugna‑nsen, yiwet n thuskayt‑nsen.

Mḥend d Mḥend aḥkan‑as tadyant i asen‑yeḍran. Agellid jerḥen tasa‑s, yerna yefka‑asen idrimen, d wayen akk uḥwaǧen, Mḥend d gma‑s uɣalen s axxam‑nsen, xedmen tameɣra 7 wussan d 7 wuḍan, Mḥend yuɣal yesɛa dderya d yelli‑s ugellid, ma d tameṭṭut n baba‑s tuɣal terra aḍar, tendem deg wayen i as‑texdem i warbib‑is, tessuter deg‑s smaḥ.

Msamaḥen, llin asebter amaynut itudert‑nesn.

Tamacahut‑iw asif asif, uḥric ad tt‑yeddem ad tt‑yessif, wayeḍ ad tt‑yerr di rrif.

Fahim MESƐUDEN

Seg tgemmi-nneɣ

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Amacahu, ahu!

Zik‑nni, yella yiwen umɣar, yesɛa kraḍ n warraw‑is; ttidiren deg yiwen uxxam aqdim i d‑yezgan deg yiwet taddart ibeɛden atas ɣef tiyyaḍ. Amɣar‑agi, yerwa lḥif akken ad d‑isker tarwa‑s, yaɛteb mačči d kra deg uxeddim n tfellaḥt, maca yefreḥ s wayen ixeddem.

Yiwen n wass, yeɣli‑d fella‑s lehlak acku meqqer, dɣa yekker iweṣṣa arraw‑is di tlata ad xedmen akal‑nsen imi d wagi ara ten‑yessukksen si lḥif. Ԑuhden‑t ad kemmlen tafellaḥt‑nni yessemras deg wakal‑is. Asmi yewweḍ laεfu n Rebbi, bdan axeddim n wakal‑nsen am baba‑tsen. Maca, yiwet n tikkelt, llan kerrzen, dɣa ufan izra n ddheb s ddaw n wakal; ferḥen atas acku ad kksen tigullelt ɣef yiqerra‑nsen.

Bdan ttmeslayen amek ara xedmen; ameqqran yebɣa ad iruḥ ad ibeddel tamurt akken ad yidir tudert n umerkanti deg leqser yernu ad d‑yaɣ takerrust n lεali. Alemmas yebɣa kan ad iṣubb ɣer temdint ula d netta ad yezhu, ad yels ad yessebleε ayen yebɣa. Amecṭuḥ‑nni, yerfa imi ur ṭṭifen ara deg wawal‑nsen, mi εuhden baba‑tsen yemmuten.

Ṭṭfen iberdan ruḥen, ma d netta yeqqim deg wakal n baba‑s; ixeddem tafellaḥt, yesnerna ttawilat iqdimen s yimaynuten, yulɣal yebna axxam ajdid, yuɣ‑d, tafunast iwezziwen, ikerriyen. Asmi yesεa aṭas n lmal, yebda yessexdam arrac n taddart‑is deg uxeddim; taddart, tuɣal yal lxir yella deg‑s, lḥif akk yennejla fell‑asen. Ma d atmaten‑nni‑ines, uɣalen ɣer wansi i d‑kkan, lḥif‑nni aberkan, acku ur ṭṭifen ara deg wawal i as‑fkan i baba‑tsen asmi yettmettat, yernu ur ḥmiden ara Rebbi deg rreẓq i d asen‑d‑yefka.

Ameqqran d ulemmas, uɣalen‑d ɣer gma‑tsen amecṭuḥ s ndama, maca netta ur yettu ara d atmaten‑is xas akken tɣur‑iten temẓi akked ssaεaya; ddren akked‑s deg lehna d talwit.

Tamacahut-iw, tekfa. Ad tt-nekfu s usefru-agi n Wat-Zik:

|Win iḥemmlen lxedma|I tmeddit telha|Ad yaf yesεa lfayda|
|---|---|---|
|Win iḥemmeln tiɣimit|I tmeddit diri-t|Leqqrar-is d timetrit|

Benmuhub Ḥuriya (Bucali)

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Aɣerda d yizem.

Inna‑ak, illa yan uɣerday ameɛnan⁵ ittidir g yat teẓgi, maka netta itteggʷad aṭṭaṣ, tanna⁶ seg ukɛeb⁷ d tawwukt⁸, ɣas ad d‑izzuff imikk n uzwu, ar aha ittiɣil d tawwukt ay d‑izzuffen. Manaya ayd t‑yujjan ad igg taḍṣa i yiɣaṛṣiwen n tagant.

Tadmut: wa a baba ecḥal ay itteggʷad !

Agbur: itteggʷad agʷed azwu !

Agḍiḍ: aɣerday amaggʷad, aɣerday amaggʷad ...

Imudar: aɣerday amaggʷad, aɣerday amaggʷad... (ttalsen⁹ i wawal s tqbbaḍt)

Iwa inna‑ak, ijj wass, iɛɛurrem¹⁰ uɣerday, iwɛed (iwads) ɣer yizem, agellid n yidurar d iẓuɣaṛ, yufa‑t‑inn illa igen ɣef yimi n yifri‑nnes.

Mani imudar yaḍen, ur‑asen‑t igi lḥal, ggallen ḍeffṛen aɣerday ad‑ẓṛen mani ira.

Issenti¹¹ uɣerday ittali ɣef tadawt¹² n yizm, netta waxxa tebbi‑d tasa‑nnes s‑tiwdi, makan¹³ iɛɛurrem ur sul iri ad igg taḍṣa n yimudar.

Yan imikk, ha yizem yuki‑d, netta izzlez yaɣ‑d uɣerday akal, izlem diges yizem s lhiba nna illan ɣef wudem‑nnes, allig ɣaln yimudar is yiweḍ wass n‑uɣerday.

Awtul: a iyi yuɣen d ad t‑ičč yizem g tuffiẓt !

Izem: a matta tɛurrma‑ad ! mayd ak‑ifkan tirrugza‑ad ! is ur ak‑nnin agellid n yidrarn d yiẓaɣaṛn ayad ? d ad k‑cceɣ¹⁴, ad cceɣ tamurt ɣef teggured¹⁵ !

Aɣerday: ɛemmi ameqran ! rareɣ‑enn ɣer‑k udem n Ṛbbi, ad ur iyi‑tecced a ɛemmi ameqran a taxxamt tameqrant, nekk tteggʷadeɣ ḥalla¹⁶, ggiɣ taḍṣa n umeẓẓyan d umeqran, cegg tessaggʷaded amata, addag tnedred ttergigin yislman g wasif, amur‑nnek, riɣ ad iyi‑tawsem ass‑a !

Iqqim yizem ittxemmam, imikk day yini‑as s yijj wawal issarn d taḍṣa :

Hahah ! a mayd‑anɣ iccarn ḥma ad ak‑awseɣ, max ur k‑tetteɣ helli ssyenfiɣ !

Aɣerday: ad ak‑qawleɣ awal ttawseɣ‑ak kra n wass s wayenn ufiɣ !

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Inna‑ak, inder yizem allig irrgig wakal, day yini‑as:

Mami iɣiy uzgen n usekkin am cegg ad t‑igg ? irra‑d ɣurek  Ṛebbi s wudem‑nnes umi iyi‑d tufid jjawneɣ, yallah ntel‑iyi udem‑nnek !

Izzuttel  uɣerday,  iffeɣ  abrid  i  yizem,  mani  imudar  nitni  behḍen  g‑uɣerday  mayd  gan allig ur t‑ičči yizem !

Yan  wass,  ar  irezzu  yizem  di  teẓgi  ɣef  mayd  igemmer,  netta  ur  irri  ɣer  yiḍaṛen‑nnes allig t tumeẓ tẓeqquṛt n yinegmaren. Netta iqqim ittxemmam ma ɣa igg, iddeɣ¹⁷ ur iṛḍi ad iɣer i mayd as ittawsen, aha iggʷd altu ad d ɣers issrar taynit.

Cwayt  kan,  ha  imudar  raren‑d  ɣurs,  maka¹⁸  agʷed yan ur iẓḍaṛ  ad  t‑id‑issufeɣ  seg uḥeddiq‑enn, mani‑k a aɣerday taru‑t‑id, intab aha s tfessi‑nnes ittebbi ifilan i tratsa nna yumẓen izem, dat ad d‑taru inegmaren.

Iffeɣ‑d yizem si tratsa, irwel ntta d‑uɣerday ɣer yifri‑nnes, issnimmer‑t, yini‑as: Ur‑k uminɣ, ass nzi¹⁹ iyi‑tennid tezmerd ad iyi‑tawsed kra n wass, ɣalɣ ur inejjim ijj am cegg i umya, maka ass‑a ssneɣ is‑s tgid aɛerrim, tanemmirt‑nnek !

Aɣerday: s taḍfi a agellid n yimudar !

Izem: seg wass‑a d usawan ur illi mayd ttaggʷaded, mala ggiɣ nekk agellid n yimudar, cegg d‑aɛerrim‑nnsen !

Qqimen  ḍeṣṣen,  wten  qaɛ²⁰  imudar  abeqqa  i  uɣerday  aɛerrim,  seg  tizi‑enn  i  uɣerday teffeɣ‑t tawda, iqqim aha netta d yizem d imeddukkal.

Yusef AWRIR

Yelli-s n ugellid

G yat tmurt yaggugen, ittidir yiǧǧ ugellid i ɣur tella kṛaḍt n teḥanjirin²¹, nitenti ad igan iẓṛi n wallen‑nnes, yat tawala, ixes ad iẓeṛ man‑ta t‑iḥemlen s tidet.

Iɣra‑d ugellid i yissis, iseqa‑tent akkʷ yan useqsi “ecḥal ay i-teḥmlemt ?”

“Uuh a baba ɛezzi ! cegg d mummu n tiṭṭ-inu, ḥemleɣ-k anect n telwizin d tewdiɛin illan g umaḍal akkʷ.” Ayed as‑d‑tenna yillis tamenzut i ugellid.

Inna‑as ugellid s tumert: “iɣuda mayad !”

Tenna‑as‑d tlemmasiyt : “baba-inu tasa inu ! ttiriɣ-k ugar n wanect n wureɣ d uẓeṛf ikturen tiserfin n yigelliden.”

17 Minzi, acku, ani

18 Makan, macan, maca, mac

19 Umi, llig

20 Akkʷ, qaḥ

21 tiqcicin

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Icmummeḥ²² ugellid, day yini‑as: “waxxa, iẓil !” Tgula‑d²³ tedwilt n tmaẓuẓt, tini‑as daɣn nettat : “baba-inu, agellid n udrar d uẓaɣar, tɛezzed ɣuri ugar n tisent illan di dduniyt.” Ibheḍ ugellid, iqqim iṛẓem imi‑nnes, ur ɣifes ihan²⁴ wayen d‑tenna yillis, yini‑as : “ales-as i mayed tennid, waqila wesserɣ, ur sul sseflideɣ ameki nna kkiɣ !” day tals‑as tmaẓuẓt‑nnes : “nniɣ-ak ttiriɣ-k a baba am tisent niɣ-d ugar.” Ur issusem mayan agellid, inna‑as “istmam ḥemlent-i ugar n wureɣ d tizuzaf akkʷ illan, kemm tga-d ɣurem tayri-inu ɣas zun d tisent !” issufeɣ ugellid illis tamẓuẓt seg ibergemmi‑nnes.

Tṛaḥ ssyin, teffɣ tamurt n babas, ar yat teẓgi, umi tuḥel, tekcem iǧǧ yifri, teqqim ar talla imeṭṭi²⁵, mani memmis n ugellid n tmazirt‑enn, izri‑d s wagmar‑nnes aḥmami²⁶. Cwi, isell i tarut, yasi allen, yanni yat terbat am wayyur, s udlal aberkan, ur‑ǧǧin iɛla am nettat di kra n tmazirt.

Imun ssyin ugeldun²⁷ aked terbat‑enn s aɣerm n babas, itter‑tt i yiwel. Tenna‑as nettat, ur tettawl ɣas mala yusa‑d babas ɣer tmeɣra‑nnes, agellid n tmurt n Ayt Uflla, i tt‑d‑issufɣen si tmurt‑nnes.

Ilkem²⁸ wass n yislan, ur enn‑iqqim umeqran ula ameẓẓyan, yuzen ugellid n Ayt wadda imazann‑nnes s tmizar nneḍni, ur enn‑iqqim ufeṛḍi, yiweḍ‑d ula d babas n teslit, netta urta issen u ilin tarbat ittawey memmis ugellid.

Ha imensi iwweḍ, ssentin sserusen‑d uččiten imxalafen, makan, umi yurem ugellid n Ayt Ufella, inker s ibeddi, yini‑asen : “a matta wučči-ad amessas ɣurun ? awit-aɣ-d tisent !”

Imikk, ha yat terbat, tella tewta‑d anettal i wudem‑nnes, ternu‑as tisent i ugellid, tini‑as : “s tazmert-nnek a agellid n Ayt Ufella, ssarmeɣ ad ak-yaḍfut dɣi !” deɣya yukez ugellid ageṛd‑enn²⁹, ur fellas ixefi yiri n yilli‑s.

Tekkes yilli‑s n ugellid ɣef wudem‑nnes, ibheḍ ugellid, mani seg d‑tekka yillis ɣer daha. Yukez max allig as‑d‑fkan učči amessas, idwel issen, taḍfi n tiram d tisent, yuḍa ɣef ifadden, itter asuref i yillis, tuḍa ɣifes tenna‑as s tumert : “uh, baba inu, ansa-nnek idis n tasa-inu !” tegra‑as iɣallen, tessudem‑as iɣef.

Tawel memmis n ugellid n Ayt Wadda, ddren g tayri d ufra.

Yusef Awrir

22 izmummeg 23 Tiwḍ 24 Ihan fellas: iɛejb-as 25 Talla imeṭṭi: tettru 26 Yan wanaw deg yiysan s yiɣmi (aklu, llun ) yudsen ɣer uberkan 27 Ageldun niɣ-d amnukal, netta d memmis n ugellid 3 28 Yiwḍ 29 Ageṛḍ: iri, ṣṣuṭ

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Bu umekli ičč-it, bu tgersa yiwi-tt.

“Ssusmat ziɣ, iḍehṛ-i tella dihin temɣirt.”

Tenna‑as i warra‑nnes, i illan ttmenɣan ɣef ma ɣa isun deg walkas aḍeṛḍaj, umi tsell i ḥedd iqqar‑d seg beṛṛa, netta sulen warra‑nnes ttemejɣan, tsell i temɣirt diɣen, tikkelt‑a, iferrz‑d wawal, d wenn urgaz.

# A Leḥsen u Ɛeqqa ! a Leḥsen !

Tenna‑as i tarwa‑nnes: “Ɣawlit san30, ṛaɛat31 may d-iqqaren i baba-twen.”

Maɣawalen yirban, manwa i ɣa yizzaren ɣer ssellum, ad‑iregb ɣer may‑d iɣrin, iǧǧ ur iri ad issers ḍḍṣaṛt i wenneḍni, lumenna amaẓuẓ, ittafraw am yired seg ufan, d imikk helli, uɣulen‑d, inna‑as-d umeqran: A baba, illa dihin urgaz-enn baba-s n Muḥend u Mimun !

Ikker aha Leḥsen ɣef wučči, ikka tawwurt, iffeɣ ɣires, dat ad t‑yaweḍ, illa ittini‑as‑d kra, maka, ur t‑yujji yigdi s tazut ad issfeld, yusi iẓṛa, inbbeh ɣifes, irwel awarn i taddart ar d ittzu, yini‑as i urgaz‑enn:

# A Mimun u Sɛid a inn, a rna-d ɣer dat !

Iṛẓem Mimun i yiẓṛa nna ittasi deg ufus, irar‑as d:

Iwa azul, mayd teɛnid !

Teɛnud lxir, adef ɣer jaj ad neg atay.

Kecmen ɣer tneṣṛiyt, qqimen ar ttmeslayen, ussan‑a n Ktubeṛ, idrus mani ttafen awnul i wawal, takrza n yigran ɣef yidis‑a alqaḍ n usengar ɣef idis‑enn, azemmur yiwi‑d abrid, tutf‑it‑id tbexni, idrus wayenn iɣaman i unfaḍ, uglen midden si teqdudin g wussan‑ddɣ, ur sɛin akud i ukmaz, awal inezzɣ‑d awal, wa yuli wa iḍṛa, ta tiwel tenn tellf, ur iǧǧi ṛebbi mani ɣer ur iwiḍn, drus kan, ha lal n uxam tessers‑asen‑d atay d yiwen umeḍli n uɣrum, tella‑as talussi g tuẓẓumt, ssentin tetten, ha igdi ar diɣ isetten, din din, inna‑as d yiwis axatar: A baba, inna-ak Xali Ɛli u Iccu, wec-as d tagersa.

Ixemmem imikk, yini‑as: Eddu, ha tt enn nnig umnar, g unwal, ssufeɣ-as-tt.

Teqqur‑as a Mimun u Sɛid tuga g yimi, ur yufi ma ɣa yini, am wenn as‑ibbyen iles, cwi ibedd, ur as‑iggi lḥal qaɛ ula is ad ilmeẓ ayelli as‑illan deg yimi, yini‑as: A Leḥsen ! a wa hann tagersa a iyi-d-yiwin.

Ixzer ɣers Leḥsen, uca iḍeṣ, irar‑as: A wa wenn di illa unezgum n tkerza, ur da iṛeẓẓ ifadden, iwet aɣejdim.

Bu umekli ičč-t, bu tgersa yiwi-tt

Yusef AWRIR

30 San: kan, ukan, helli

31 Walit, ẓṛat

# Sɣur Fahim Mesɛudden

Urar‑agi yebna s talɣa n tseddarin, yal mi ara d‑nṣubb taseddart ad nernu asekil akken ad naf awal ɣezzifen ɣef wawal‑nni yellan nnig‑s. Isekilen imezwura ur ttbeddilen ara.

# Sɣur Fahim Misaɛudden

# AMCIC-IW

1. Γur‑neɣ yiwen n umcic
- AMCIC -IW
- Ur yettazzal ur yettɣawal
- Ur yeččeqlal
- Yezga yeṭṭes
- Ur ixebbec ur yettkerric
- Minuc ay s nessawal
- Ur yettazal
- Iḥemmel iḍes
2. Mi yesla i uskerwec
- Ad yettcexxir ur yettagad
- Ad yettḥekkir
- Ad iqarreb
- Ad ibedd ad yetturrec
- Yeḥrec yeɣleb aṣeggad
- Ad yettcexxir
- Mara ijelleb.
3. iḥemmel ad yurar atas
- Mi d‑yeɣli yiḍ ad yeṭṭes
- S tqejjirt‑is
- Di texxamt‑iw
- Mi tid ṭṭfeɣ deg wammas
