Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Asmuḥyet n Tala uMaziɣ

# Aɛudiw d uɣyul

Yiwen urgaz yesɛa aɛudiw d uɣyul. Yiwwas llan merra deg ubrid, aɣyul yenna i uɛudiw : « Rfed aḥric seg tezdemt-inu, ma tebɣiḍ ad ddreɣ. ». Aɛudiw yerra iman-is d aɛeẓẓug. Cwiṭ akka yeɣli uɣyul-nni seg ɛeggu, yemmut. Dɣa argaz-nni iɛebba kullec ɣef uɛudiw yerna ula d aglim n uɣyul. Aɛudiw yerra-d nnehta, yenna-yas « Annaɣ i yi-iga rray-iw ! Imi ugiɣ ad refdeɣ taɛkemt fessusen, atan tura ɛebbaɣ kullec rniɣ ula d aglim. ».

# Lemmer bedden imeqranen ɣer tama n wid meẓẓiyen tili ddren merra deg lehna d talwit.

# Aqjun yeṭṭfen tacriḥt n uksum

Aqjun yeṭṭfen tacriḥt n uksum yella izegger asif. Iwala tili-ines deg waman, iɣil d aqjun-nniḍen i iṭṭfen tacriḥt n uksum yugaren tinna-ines. Dɣa, iserreḥ i tecriḥt-nni-ines, ijelleb iwakken ad d- yekkes tinna n umeddakkel-is. Ur yeṭṭif ula d yiwet imi tameqqrant ur telli ara s tidet, tamecṭuḥt yewwi-tt wasif.

Akka, win yebɣan ad yawi ayla n medden, ad isruḥ ula d ayla-s.

# Tasedda d ubareɣ

Yiwen ubareɣ yella yettɛayar yiwet n tsedda imi tettarew kan yiwen. Tasedda teḍsa-d deg udem-is, terra-yas-d : « D tidet, yiwen kan maca d izem ! ».

Ur ḍlimen ara leqbayel imi qqaren deg yinzi : « Takemmict n tzizwa tif aqecwal n yizan ».

# Ibuqalen

Sin n yibuqalen, yiwen n talaɣt wayeḍ n wuzzal, yewwi-ten wasif. Abuqal n talaɣt yenna i ubuqal n wuzzal : « Ttxil-k ɛum mbaɛid fell-i mačci rrif-i ; acku ma tennuleḍ-iyi-d, ad bḍuɣ d iceqfan. ».

Tudert n ugellil tuɛer ma yesɛa amerkanti ur irewwun ara d lǧar-is.

# Abeḥri d yiṭij

Abeḥri d yiṭij ttemɛebbaren. Yiwen yenna i wayeḍ win ara yekksen iselsa-ines i umessikel-ihin yugar wayeḍ. D abeḥri i ibdan, iṣuḍ-d s teqseḥ. Imi argaz-nni izeyyer iselsa-ines ɣef tfeka-s, abeḥri yerna deg teqseḥ. Mi iwala argaz-nni yerna aselsu wis sin seg usemmiḍ, abeḥri yeǧǧa abrid i yiṭij. Di tazwara, yebda-d kan s cwiṭ n lḥamu. Mi iwala argaz-nni yekkes aselsu-nni wis sin yerna deg teqseḥ. Dɣa, argaz-nni ur nezmir ara ad yesber i uzɣal, yekkes merra iselsa-ines, iruḥ ad icucef deg wasif.

Taqsidt-a tettbeggin-d belli aɛekkaz werǧin ad imel abrid i wallaɣ.

Sɣur Juba TALA i d-yesquccḍen ɣer Esope

Tala uMaziɣ - adrar-inu.blogspot.com

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# inkizfin I MVIVM

Deg taggayt-agi ad tafem iḍrisen n yimesfukel, ama d imesfukel bu yiwet n turda neɣ imesfukel bu snat n turdiwin …

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Deg yiseggasen‑agi ineggura, nezmer ad nini belli taɣuri tuɣal txuṣ maḍi, yerna tannumi ɣef leqraya n yidlisen d abaɣur ameqqran; maca aṭas ur as‑yefkan ara azal. Imi tennerna tetiknulujit imdanen merra s tilifun d antirnat, dayen i ten‑yerran ɣeflen fell‑as.

Di tazwara, taɣuri d addal i wallaɣ: amek i nezmer ad nḥareb ɣef tdawsa nneɣ s waddal; inezmer ad nḥareb ɣef wallaɣ nneɣ yis‑s, imi win yeqqaren amzun yesseḥbaber iman‑is ɣef isekna n tewser ɣer zdat am: Taleɣcit deg unecfu d wuguren deg twuriwin n wallaɣ. Rnu ɣer waya taɣuri n yiḍ tettawi‑d iḍes i yimeɣri war atqelleq, ladɣa wid umi ittiwɛir ad ten‑id‑yas. Xerṣum mraw n tesdatin seddaw n tafat taxfifant kan; tettεawan amdan ad yesgunfu.

Syin akin, amawal n umdan ad yuɣal d amesbaɣur ama d awalen, tinfaliyin ama d iremma ... yezmer ad yesfaydi deg tudert‑is yis‑sen, neɣ deg uxeddim‑is. Dayen i ara as‑id‑imudden taflest tameqqrant i yiman‑is, d tezmert ussileɣ n ufecku n waṭas n tutlayin am: Tafransist, tanglizit d teɛrabt... Akk aya, dayen ara yeǧǧen anelmad ad ixdem akatay‑is akken iwata ad yili igerrez, bla tuccḍiwin n tira, neɣ ayen yerzan taseftit d usemres n tenfaliyin i ṣeḥḥan deg wadeg‑nsent. Akka ad nissin tutlayt nneɣ yerna ad tuɣal teǧhed.

Bla ma nettu dakken taɣuri d aremmud adelsan, s wazal ara yerren imdanen ttemεacaren way gar‑asen, i d‑yettawin tamusni tamaynut amedya: Asegzi ɣef ddunit d wamek ttεicint tsutiwin nniḍen; ama d ayen yeεnan idles‑nsen neɣ ddin‑nsen ... dayen ara yessuffɣen amdan di ṭṭiq neɣ deg uguren i yesεa di tnefsit‑is, ad yefteḥ ɣer ddunit ad iẓer d akken ulac lxilaf ger yimdanen. Akken i d‑tenna ¨SIMUN BUBWART¨: «taɣuri d tasarut i aɣ‑d‑itteldin amaḍal».

Taɣuri, d amsakay n rruḥ d wul, d lferḥ i yiḥulfan. Γef waya tlaq mliḥ tebɣest d tekci n ufud i uḥareb ɣef tigawt‑a, imi d tadawsa n usnerni ur ilaq ara ad tunegzem. Awufan ad yili useḥbiber fell‑as iwakken ad tt‑id‑afent tsutiwin nniḍen d tannumi icebhen di tudert‑nsen, yerna ad tili d abrid ara iḥarben ɣef usnerni n tmeti.

Siǧillali Naziha

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Awalnuten di tutlayt tamaziɣt?

Yal tutlayt deg umaḍal iwakken ad tidir yessefk ad tili ɣef yiles n wid i tt‑ittmeslayen yal ass, Ilaq ad teddu d wakud, imi tutlayt simal ittbeddil lweqt tettbeddil yid‑s. Tutlayt n wass‑a temgarad ɣef tin n yiḍelli, akken ara temgarad ɣef tin uzekka.

Ula d tutlayt tamaziɣt iwakken ad tidir isefk ad teddu d tallit. Mi ara d‑nemmeslay ɣef tmaziɣt n wass‑a ad nwali llan wawalen ittruḥun, ur ten‑ssexdamen ara medden, llan wiyed rennun‑d, keččmen‑d ɣer tutlayt;d wi iwumi neqqar “awalnuten” neɣ “awalen imaynuten”.

Ihi, ayɣer tutlayt tamaziɣt teḥwaǧ iwalnuten?

Di tazwara, si tmunnent n Lezzayer d asawen, tutlayt tamaziɣt tuɣ abrid nniḍen, tenfel‑d seg urebbi n timawt ɣer win n tira, d ayen i yeǧǧan tussna‑a tebda tettnerni, teṭṭef amḍiq s wazal‑is. Afares amezwaru i deg d‑banen wawalen imaynuten “Tajerrumt n tmaziɣt tatrart –tantala taqbaylit” i d‑yessuffeɣ Lmulud At Mɛemmer deg useggas n 1970, d “umawal n tmaziɣt tatrart”, deg‑sen i d‑banen aṭas n wawalnuten seld anadi i yexdem ugraw n yimussnawen, iswi‑nsen “d aselmed n tmaziɣt s tutlayt tamaziɣt”, d usizdeg n tutlayt‑a seg wawalen ireṭṭalen ledɣa tutlayt taɛrabt d tefransist.

Tin ɣur‑s, Di tallit‑a uggten yirmad d tigawin i d‑yellan, tikliwin deg yiberdan (di temnaḍt n Leqbayel d tmurt n Lezzayer), inejmuɛen n yigduden, timsirin n uselmed n tmaziɣt di temnaḍt n Leqbayel d temdint n Lezzayer ta deffir ta.. Iswi‑nsen d asuddes n ugezdu i uselmed n tmaziɣt d unadi deg unnar‑a ama di temnaḍt n Tizi‑Uzzu neɣ di Lezzayer tamanaɣt, Ɣer taggara sawḍen ad llin agezdu n tutlayt d yidles amaziɣ di Tizi‑Uzzu deg useggas n 1990, aseggas kan di Bgayet 1991, syin di Tubiret 2007, ɣef waya tamazight teḥwaǧ amawal atrar iwakken ad yeddu uselmed‑is akken iwata war uguren.

Rnu ɣef waya, seg useggas n 1990 d asawen yessefk ɣef yimaziɣen ad seddun tutlayt nsen s wudem ussnan mačči s wudem n wafrayen, imi assar ussnan yettili‑d mi ara d‑yaf umdan iman‑is sdat n taɣulin n tussna anda amdan yessefk fell‑as ad d‑yaf awalen ilaqen neɣ tanfalit yeddan d tussna‑a. Anecta yeǧǧa imussnawen xeddmen i wakken ad d‑afen tifrat, xas akken tamsalt ur teshil ara, dɣa ad nwali tussniwin akk i yellan deg umaḍal, ama d tid i cudden ɣer tmussniwin tussnanin seg‑sent (tusnakt, tujjya... ) ama d Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
tid i cudden ɣer tsekla am d tamedyazt ama d iḍrisen. Tussniwin‑a ur d‑llint ara kan akka maḥsub yal yiwet seg‑sent tesɛa amusnaw neɣ imusnawen i iqeddcen fell‑as, rnu ɣer waya yal yiwet seg‑sent tesɛa timental i tt‑yeǧǧan ad d‑tili neɣ i yeǧǧan imusnawen‑a ad nadin, wa ad d‑mmeslayen fell‑asent. Md: Amawal n tusnekt n Mḥend Saɛdi, i d‑ssuffɣent tezrigin n ,Asegzawal ameẓẓyan n tsekla, Muḥend Akli Ṣalḥi, Amawal n tsenselkimt n Samya Saɛd Buzerfan, Amawal n tesniselt n berkay.

Ula deg unnar n tmedyazt, yessefk ad d‑yili usnerni n umawal s tudfa n wawalen atraren, dɣa ad naf amedyaz Ben Muḥemmed d amezwaru i d‑yeskecmen awalen imaynuten deg yisefra‑s i yecna Yidir di tesfifin‑is timezwura. Ur nzeggel ara tasuɣelt, Kateb Yasin ula d netta isedda‑d kra n wawalen atraren di tsuɣelt i d‑yexdem i tecqufin n umezgun.

Ɣer taggara, Awalen imaynuten turez‑iten tutlayt n wass‑a, imi tutlayt terfed‑itt tallit i wakken ad teddu di yal taɣult di tudert n yal ass, ɣes ma yella‑d uselmed n tmaziɣt zik yebna ɣef tɣuri n kra n yiḍrisen d uglam n tefyar s ubrid n tjerrumt tqdimt, maca si 2003 ɣer da imussnawen ɛawden tamuɣli ɣef wamek ara yeddu uselmed n tutlayt‑a.

Ihi; nezmer ad d‑nini tutlayt tamaziɣt tedder acḥal d leqrun di timawit, maca yusa‑d wass ideg tutlayt‑a terfed‑itt tira. Aṭas n yimussnawen xedmen ssawḍen ad d‑snulfun kra n wawalen urǧin llan di tutlayt‑a, ɣef waya yessefk usnulfu n wawalen ledɣa di taɣulin icudden ɣer tussna iwakken ad yeddun uselmed n tmaziǧt s tmaziɣt.

Saɛdi Zuhra.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Tikli ɣef uḍar d yiwen n waddal isehlen maḍi

imi yezmer umdan ad t‑yexdem di lweqt yebɣa neɣ deg umekkan yebɣa, akken daɣen yezmer ad t‑yexdem yal yiwen deg‑nneɣ ama d agrud, d ilemzi, neɣ d amɣar. Ihi iwumi telha tikli ɣef uḍar ?

Di tazwara, tikli ɣef uḍar ɣur‑s aṭas n yibaɣuren i tezmert n umdan, imi win ileḥḥun azal n yiwet n tamert i wass ur yettaḍen ara aṭṭan n wul.

Di tis snat, tikli n uḍar tseqɛad tikli n yidamen di tfekka n umdan.

Syin akkin, tikli ɣef uḍar tesrusuy allaɣ n bnadem, imi win ixeddmen addal‑agi yezga yers lmux‑is ittafqaɛ ara.

Ɣer taggara, tikli ɣef uḍar tsefsay tadunt di tfekka n umdan, ɣef way‑agi amdan ileḥḥun aṭas ur ittqewway ara.

Ɣaf way‑agi i telha tikli ɣef uḍar imi tesɛa aṭas n yibaɣuren i d‑igellun s lfayda i tezmert n umdan. Akken qqaren tazmert yelhan d nettat i d agerruj n ddunit.

Sidhum Kusayla

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Timetti tamaziɣt, am tmettiyin n umaḍal akkit, semrasen deg yinawen‑nsen awalen d tenfaliyin n lmeɛna d lehdaqa, am azul ar tufat, ǧǧiɣ‑ak talwit, s tezmert n yimekli inek … awalen‑a, ggaren assaɣen gar yimdanen, sentimen tadukli yerna mmalen‑d tafesna n tɣerma uɣur tessaweḍ tmetti‑nni aladɣa, d talsa s umata.

Gar wawalen‑a, yella wawal « azul » yellan d amaynut ɣer yigduden imaziɣen, taggara‑ay kan i d‑yekcem ɣer yidles‑nneɣ. Yeṭṭuqqet / icaḍ wawal fell‑as, iseggasen‑a ineggura.

Aṭas i yesteqsayen ɣef unamek‑is? aẓar‑is, ansi d‑yekka? Melmi i t‑qqaren? Azul, d awal n wadaf ɣer yinaw usrid neɣ arusrid. Yes‑s ibeddun medden tameslayt, qqaren‑t mi ara mlilen d yiwen i ssnen neɣ ɣas ulamma ur t‑ssinen. Imezwura‑nneɣ, qqaren‑d timucuha sdeffir n yimensi. Send ad tt‑id‑yales, izewwir‑d s « amacahu », ayɣer? I wakken ad d‑yejbed lwelha n yiɛeggalen n twacult, xersum arrac ad d‑fken tameẓẓuɣt, ad tt‑gzun.

Ad iruḥ yiwen ɣer taddart ur yessin, yaweḍ gar sin n yiberdan, yehsel anwa i d win yettawin ɣer taddart‑nni, ilaq ad isteqsi ḥedd. Ur telli ara d lehdaqa ad as‑yini: « Mel‑iyi‑d abrid yettawin ɣer Tbuɛmucin! ». Yuwi‑d ad as‑yini azul send ad t‑yesteqsi; ilaq ad as‑t‑yini s uzmummeg. I wakken yiwen ad yaweḍ ɣer yiswi‑s, i wakken yiwen ad d‑yeqḍu ccɣel‑is, ilaq awal lɛali.

Ihi, azul, d awal lɛali s‑i nleddi inaw‑nneɣ d win ukkud nettmeslay srid, udem ɣer wudem, neɣ deg yinaw arusrid, am yineɣmisen deg tilizri neɣ deg umaṭṭaf n radyu, neɣ d izen iraw, d tabrat, d amedya. Neqqar‑it, tanezzayt, deg uzal neɣ tameddit.

Aṭas i ttwaliɣ di facebook ttarun‑d ɣef uẓar n wawal‑a « azul ». Qqaren‑d d awal uddis yekka‑d seg temlilit n sin n wawalen (aẓ+ul), fkan‑as asnamek n « Aẓ ɣer wul! » Aṭas i wumi yeɛjeb usnamak‑a, qqaren‑d tecbeḥ tenfalit‑a « aẓ‑d ɣer wul! »

Ɣas yecbeḥ usnamek i as‑gan, nekki yessusef‑itt‑id wallaɣ‑iw, yugi uqerruy‑iw ad yeqbel tamuɣli‑agi. Acuɣer? 1ut, targalt "z" deg « azul », ur telli d tufayt; limer d tidet d « ẓ » tili nsusruy‑d « aẓul » mačči azul. Tis snat amyag aẓ inumek qerreb, wehd‑s kan war tazelɣa n tnila « d », ur tban tigawt ɣer wul n win yettmeslayen i terra; deg wawal azul, ulac deg‑s tazelɣa n tnila « d ». Ma tigawt akkin i terra, am wakken ara as‑tinid i yiwen: « Az akkin », tafyirt « aẓ ɣer wul » ur tesɛi ara anamek.

Tis 2, amer d tidet anamek‑is qerreb‑d ɣer wul‑iw, ad negzu da, amzun akken d yiwen i yettgabaren taqcict akken ad t‑teɛceq. Netta, awal‑a teqqar‑it teqcict akken i t‑yeqqar uqcic. Sxedmet allaɣen‑nwen ciṭuh, ma deg yidles‑nneɣ d leɛwayed‑nneɣ, tezmer ad tini tlemẓit i yilemẓi "Qerreb‑d ɣer wul‑iw" neɣ ulama ad as‑tini "ḥemmleɣ‑k sdat n medden? D awezɣi!

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Di tilawt, awal‑a azul, yekka‑d seg yisem "ahel" n tmahaqt/tamaceɣt, anamek‑is ass neɣ azal. Imucaɣ qqaren ahul /tahult i d‑yekkan seg ahel, anamek‑is am wakken qqaren s taɛrabt "طاب نهارك" neɣ "Ad yelhu wass‑ik". Imi Imaziɣen n ugafa mmgaraden deg ususru n kra n yimesla, akka am "h" i susruyen. Imucaɣ s waṭas deg wadeg n "z", imnuda imeɣnasen n tmaziɣt deg yiseggasen n 1970, uwin‑d awal‑a, beddlen‑as "h"‑nni s "z", fkan‑as talɣa "azul".

Ula deg tmurt n Sinigal, Imaziɣen n Zenaga qqaren awal‑a azul s unamek "asrad neɣ talwit". Mi ara yemlil yiwen d wayed ad as‑yessirem ad yili wass‑is d asrad neɣ ad t‑isɛeddi deg talwit.

Sdat n unessig‑a i d‑yekkan seg wid ur nferrez timsal, fursen tagnit yicenga n tmaziɣt iwakken ad zḍen tineḍruyin tisugnanin i usaru i d‑urwent tismin‑nsen, win i umi fkan azwel « Tikerkest tamaziɣt.

Llan kra n yiqijɛen, d imeɛfan, ttesṭaden deg umejriw; qqaren‑d dakken awal‑a azul yekka‑d seg wawal n taɛrabt « ahla » أهال i rran Yimuhaɣ ahul, syin Mulud Mɛemri ibeddel‑it, yuɣal azul. Wigi, nessen‑iten, tessnem‑ten, neẓra d tismin i ten‑isderɣlen, ɣunzan Imaziɣen, ɣunzan idles‑nneɣ, ur zmiren ara akk ad slen i wawal‑agi amaziɣ; kan akka i ttrajun ad yecceḍ yiwen i wakken ad d‑ssufɣen tisuqas‑nsen iwakken ad gren ccekk, ɣef tumast‑nneɣ d yidles‑nneɣ, deg wallaɣen n Yimaziɣen iɛerbawalen yebɣan ad uɣalen ɣer tnaslit‑nsen.

Ihi, taggrayt n wawal d ta, awal‑a azul yennulfa‑d deg tazwara n yiseggasen n 70, sumren‑t‑id yimassanen d yimeɣnasen n tutlayt tamaziɣt, yuzzel deg yilsawen, qeblen‑t Yimaziɣen, ula d Yimucaɣ, ass‑a, qqaren azul Ur yezmir ara yiwen ad d‑yekker deg 2020, ad as‑yefk asnimek ixulfen ɣef usnimek n wid i t‑id‑yesnulfan.

Ma Leqbayel di facebook, segzayen‑d awal‑a s tenfalit « Aẓ‑d ɣer wul » iwakken ad dhun, ad nnecraḥen, ulac fell‑as. Ur nuksan ara ad ilin yilemẓiyen d telmeẓyin‑nneɣ rumuntik! Ma yella d aselmad n tmaziɣt, ur d‑yuwi ara ad iselmad i yinelmaden tikerkas. Win ur nelkin ara deg unamek n tɣawsa, ad inadi; ur yeggar ara iman‑is deg teḥsilt.

Madani Afia

Asnimek: interprétation

Iqijɛen: minables

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Uraren n tbidyutin am PUBG, Free Fire, Among Us, Ludu… d uraren i tturaren waṭas n yimdanen; imeẓẓyanen, imeqqranen abeɛda deg wussan‑a n ukman. Aṭas i d‑yeqqaren belli uraren‑a lhan aṭas i usɛeddi n lweqt, maca daɣ aṭas i d‑yeqqaren belli uraren‑a ur lhin ara i tezmart.

Deg wudem amezwaru, uraren n tbidyutin ḥemmlen‑ten waṭas n yimdanen almi i asen‑uɣalen am lehyuf acku dinna kan i sɛeddayen lwaqt‑nsen.

Tamezwarut, deg wussan‑a anda aṭṭan n kuṛuna yezmer ad d‑yawi lada ama i yimdanen neɣ i twaculin‑nsen, leqhawi d tjemmuyaɛ megdulit, imdanen  ufan‑d anda ara sɛeddin lewqat‑nsen mebɛid ɣef waṭṭan‑a.

Tis snat, deg wuraren‑a i yezmer yiwen ad d‑yissin imdanen ijdiden i izemren ad uɣalen d imdukal n tidet ar sdat.

Tis kraḍt, deg wuraren‑a i yezmer yiwen ad d‑yelmed titiknikin n lgirra d yismawen n leslaḥ, d tɣara‑nsen…

Maca deg wudem niḍen aṭas i yettagin i warraw‑nsen ad uraren uraren‑a; ttekksen‑asen tilifuyat‑nsen.

Si tama acku aṭas i d‑yettawin udem n ssbaḥ nutni ad tturaren uraren‑a, sakkin ass‑nsen yuɣal d iḍ, iḍ‑nsen yuɣal d ass.

Si tama niḍen, ɛyan ǧǧan lecɣal‑nsen llethan d wurar, yezmer ad d‑teḍru ddana deg uxxam ur d‑yettawi ara s lexbar abeɛda ma yerra akitman ɣef yimeẓẓuɣen‑is.

Rnu ar waya, aṭas i yettaṭṭafen ama d aṭṭan n wallen neɣ d tteqlaq, d ɛeyyu n wallaɣ ɣef demma n usɛeddi n waṭas n wakud deg wurar, anda ara naf win yetturaren uraren‑a icennif aṭas, txesser ṭṭbiɛa‑s ɣef kra ur yelli.

Nekk iban‑iyi‑d belli uraren‑a lhan meɛna ilaq yiwen ad yissin ad ten‑yessexdem, ad asen‑yefk kan kra n wakud.

Tafrara AT WEJQUQ

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Tasuqilt d ayen yettuḥwaǧ umdan seg zik n zik.

Deg yiseggasen iɛeddan sexdamen‑tt kan i tsuqilt n lekwaɣeḍ neɣ n yisura d tebratin. tisuqilin‑a d imdanen i tent‑ixeddmen; ama d wid yessnen tutlayin neɣ d imdanen yeɣran tasensuqilt deg tesdawit. Tineggura‑ya nnulfan‑d yisezɣanen d wasnasen n usuqel am Google traduction. Aṭas n yimdanen i yessexdamen asnas‑a i usuqel n yimagraden d wayen niḍen.

Deg wudem amezwaru, tasuqilt s net d ttawil i sexdamen waṭas n medden. Tamezwarut, acku yeshel i usexdem, ad ttaruḍ neɣ ad tkupyiḍ aḍris i ak‑ihwan s tutlayt tebɣiḍ ɣer google traduction, deg kra kan n tasinin ad d‑yuɣal ɣer tutlayt i tebɣiḍ.

Tis snat, ttawil‑a n usuqel mačči kan d tasuqilt n wawalen i ixeddem maca tzemreḍ ad d‑tsuqleḍ yes‑s ama d iḍrisen, imagraden, tiwlafin neɣ leṣwat udyu.

Tis kraḍet asexdem‑is yeshel yerna ur yettuḥwaǧ ara tadrimt meqqren akken ad d‑tsuqleḍ kan iccer n lkaɣeḍ ɣer wabɛaḍ yessnen tasuqilt akken iwata.

Deg wudem niḍen aṭas n yimdanen i yettruḥun ar yimsuqlen unṣiben akken ad d‑suqlen ayen uḥwaǧen xas akka aṭas i ttxelliṣen; Si tama, acku tasuqilt n google tikwal ur tesɛi ara akk lmeɛna, acku tsuqul‑d awal s wawal am wakken deg usegzawal i d‑tettqellibeḍ awalen‑nni ad ten‑id‑tesnetḍeḍ ad d‑yeffeɣ uḍris.

Si tama niḍen, tasuqilt s google yezmer ad tɛeṭṭel neɣ ur tettili ara yakk ma yella ur tesɛiḍ ara tuqqna iǧehden neɣ ma truḥ‑ak.

Mačči kan d aya, tin i tent‑yugaren akk, yezmer google ad k‑yesseɣleḍ deg unamek n tefyar, ad tfehmeḍ anemgal n wayen yettwarun deg uḍris anaṣli.

Rnu ar waya, llant kra n tutlayin ur tent‑id‑yessuqul ara Google, am tutlayin tiqdimin neɣ tid ur nesɛi ara ddula‑nsent.

ɣer taggara, nekk iban‑iyi‑d belli tasuqilt s google traduction d ayen i yezmer yiwen ad issexdem melmi tt‑yuḥwaǧ abeɛda ma yettɣawal maca ilaq ur yettkil ara fell‑as 100% acku yezmer ad k‑yesseɛleḍ deg unamek n uḍris anaṣli.

Tafrara AT WEJQUQ.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Assirem i tudert

Agrud d azamul n nniya d lferḥ d ijeǧǧig n tefsut d ixulaf iwumi tlaq tudert. Ɣef waya isuḍaf d yizerfan igraɣlanen ttḥaraben ɣef yixulaf n tudert. Xas ma tikwal tilawt temmal‑d udem nniḍen imi agrud yella anda tettawakkes ‑as temẓi‑is, ur d‑yettidir ara targit‑nni n temẓi d tiẓeḍt ‑ines anceta nettwali‑t deg tudert n yal ass.

Agrud d axalaf yuklal tudert, yettidir izerfan‑is degmi ara as‑d‑ldint wallen, ula d ass deg tfada rran‑as‑t d tajmilt yal amenzu deg yulyu ad ferḥen akk izenqan d tzeɣwa.

Tamezwarut, imawlan ad as gen aḥric di tudert, ad nnaɣen d tudert alma yuɣal d argaz, am ufrux daxel n llɛec, ad yečč, ad yels, ad iḥewwes, ad yurar …

Tis snat, yesɛa azref ad yidir deg tdawsa yelḥa ɣef waya agrud segmi ara iwali tafat, ad as‑heggin tafekka i yal aṭṭan neɣ anfafad, ad‑t‑qabel amedya acraḍ deg wayyur amenzu almi 16 n yiseggasen.

Deg taggara agrud ila azref ad ilmed imi taɣuri d tafat n ddunit imawlan nutni i d aɣerbaz amenzu syin ad as‑gen afud i yisurrifen imezwura ɣer ulmud, acku ẓran azal‑is i yimmal, ula d isuḍaf d yizerfan ttḥraben ɣef uzref‑agi aya‑agi nettwli‑t deg tmurt n Lezzayer, agrud yesɛa azref i ulmad seg 5 n yissagasen d asawen ulac anwa ara as‑t‑yekksen.

Xas ma tidukliwin tigraɣlanin d isuḍaf ssawalen ɣef uḥader n ugrud maca deg wattas n waddaden d tebrek kan ɣef temlel acku igerdan yella wanda ur ttidiren ara izerfan nsen, tettwacelqef temẓi nsen tuɣal‑asen d ilili.

Si tama, ad naf imawlan i ixeddmen takriḍt ɣef tfekka neɣ tnefsit n ugrud: mazal agrud yettwat alma qqiment‑d ccwami ɣef tfekka‑s anecta yesswaɣay tanefsit‑is, llan imawlan daɣen lebɣi n warraw ttaran‑t deg rrif anecta yettaǧa agrud ur yettidir ara ayen yebɣa ilaq ad yeffeɣ dayen bɣan, ad yini ayen bɣan …

Deg tama nniḍen, asexdem n yigerdan am aklan, tugniwin yettḥazan ul mi ara nettwali agrud d aleqqaq yettɛebbi neɣ yesnuzuy tiɣawsiwin deg yiberdan lḥif deg uxxam ad yernu lḥif n ubrid wissen akked ara d‑yemlil? Acu ara as‑yeḍrun?

Rnu ɣer waya, tikwal ttekksen‑as tafat i wallen, suffuɣen‑t‑id deg uɣerbaz am akkan ulac acu ara yexdem yis‑s anecta yettara agrud deg ṭṭlam n war tamussni. Melba ma nettu timura anda mazal ṭṭradat (ligirrat), din igerdan mazal ttexnunusen d lxuf d lhif d tugniwin n yidammen n yal ass: ttwanɣan, ttwajraḥen, ggujlen s ufus n wid yettun talsa.

Ayen i d‑nenna drus acku tugniwin n tekriḍt mgal igerdan mzal nettwli‑tent xas ma assirem d lwaǧeb ad yili imi taggara agi aṭas n tukliwin n yisuḍaf i d‑yekkren mgal aya kkaten akken agrud ad yidir di tumert di talwit, targit mazal ad tḍul maca amer ad teffeɣ ɣer wayen yelhan “nekk d agrud isem‑iw leḥnana, d ajeǧǧig n tefsut anwa ara yagin tafsut?

Jeǧǧiga ƐACURI

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Amihi n internet ɣef udlis d wallalen n zik

Asnulfu n ttawil n internet, yewwi‑d yid‑s taneflit d ubaɣur i talsa merra d umdan s timmad‑is. D ttawil yesqerben imdanen, yesdukkel timura, ijmeɛ‑d aktayen d yixemmimen ɣer yiwet n tbewwaḍt, yerra amaḍal zun d taddart.

Anekcum‑ines ɣer tmurt n Lezzayer, yella‑d deg yiseggasen‑nni n 2000 d asawen, ɣas ma tuɣ‑it yettwaseqdac deg tdebliwin n uwanek uqbel, maca s wudem azayez, armi d iseggasen‑a ineggura i yuget s waṭas. Uɣalen Yizzayriyen ur zmiren ar ad xḍun i l’internet, yes‑s i gganen, yes‑s i ttnekaren. D ttawilat n uzeṭṭa inmetti neɣ d wiyaḍ, drus maḍi n Uzzayri ur nettadef ara ɣer internet. Tineggura‑a yuɣal‑asen d amwanes n yal ass, d ameddakel yelhan, d ttawil n usedhu, n leqraya, n lxedma d taywal.

Maca, seg tama‑nniḍen, yessenqes timliliyin gar yimdanen, yessebɛed tiwaculin gar‑asent. Ula deg wussan n leɛwacer, ttaznen yimdanen gar‑asen iznan n facebook, war ma mwalan, ɣas myeqraben. Yesseqreb imdanen seg tmurt ɣer tayeḍ ɣas msebɛaden, maca yessebɛed at twacult way gar‑asen ɣas mqaraben.

Tiliẓriyin ur tent‑ttwalin ara yimdanen s waṭas am zik, armi i asen‑tḥettem l’internet ad d‑snulfunt isebtaren deg‑s akken ad tent‑walin s tefses deg uglaway. Iɣmisen neqṣen maḍi, ama deg tnezzut, ama deg tɣuri. Tisutwin ara d‑yekkren, ur ttissinent ara dacu i d tamlilt n uɣmis n lkaɣeḍ di tmetti. Ma nebder‑d adlis, ad naf yeɣba wadeg‑is di tlemmast n tmetti tazzayrit, d imexḍa wid mazal qqaren idlisen, drus‑iten maḍi maḍi wid i ten‑id‑yettaɣen. aṭas seg wid yesɛan timkerḍiyin deg yixxamen‑nsen, uɣalent kan i ccbaḥa segmi i d‑tudef l’internet imnaren‑nsen. Zik, adlis s wazal‑is di tmetti, daxel ufurgu, mi ara yettraju yiwen nnuba‑s deg kra n wadeg, mi ara yeqqim deg uxxam, d adlis kan i ttafen d aḥbib n dima. Ass‑a, tinedlisin qrib ad tent‑yali uɣebbar, anagar kra deg‑sent deg temdinin timeqqranin am Lezzayer, Ɛennaba, Wehran Qsenṭina d tamiwin n tmurt n leqbayel ideg mazal beddent temkerḍiyin acemma ɣef yiḍarren‑nsent, anida‑nniḍen, tuɣal tnedlist d tigemmi i tewwi tatut d asfel.

Amihi n internet, ur yeqqim ara kan deg usenger n wallalen‑a i d‑nebder, maca iqerreb ula ɣer tdawsa n umdan. D amihi ɣef yiẓri‑ines, acku yessenqas asekkud, akken daɣen i yettarra amdan yetqelliq, ifeqqeɛ s sshala, imi tafat‑nni txeddem deg wallaɣ, tettaǧǧa amdan ur yettrus ara lxaṭer‑is.

Ɣef waya, yewwi‑d ɣef umdan ad yessenqes deg l’internet, ad yessuddes akud‑is, ad yerr azal i wallalen iqburen, acku dima mazal abaɣur‑nsen. Akka allal n internet ad yeqqim s wazal‑is, allalen‑nniḍen ad d‑yuɣal wadeg‑nsen di tmetti, amdan ad d‑yeqqim d netta i irebḥen, acku deg‑sen merra ad yesfaydi.

Khaled Achoui.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Aṭas n wawal i yellan ɣef tmeṭṭut deg tmetti. Iles fell‑as, yezga iteqqes. Leɛyub ma llan deg tmetti, d tameṭṭut i ten‑iseffḍen. Iles ɣezzif, xas d aksum, yeqqur am yicc. D anezgum i as‑d‑rennun i tmeṭṭut mi rran fell‑as arejdal. Tiṭ tremmaq deg tmetti, d lemri n tudert ɣer‑s kan i tsikkid; maca daɣen yella humm u ɣumm! Lbaḍna n tmeṭṭut deg tmetti, werǧin tezger i umnar. Wid yettarun ɣef tmeṭṭut taqbaylit deg tmetti‑ines, war ma gzan tidet yellan, d rrekya iwumi tt‑id‑ksan. Azeṭṭa n tmetti ur tefizen, ṭṭbiɛa n lejdud texḍa‑ten. Ay iles yellan d aksum, d acu i k‑yerran d asennan?

Awal, yessawal; yettnawal. Tidet, tettkebbid, tḥerrez; ur temmal. Ɣef wamek nnan yimusnawen yettwalin timetti, ur tt‑lin. Tameṭṭut ɣer Leqbayel, deffir yexf i tettili, ur tuwi ur terri; d lfayda ɣur‑s ur telli. Argaz, s udeqqem i tt‑yessexdam, ur as‑yeɣri leḥsab ma tenṭer neɣ tennegdam. Temẓi‑s ɣur‑sen, d afares; ttɣelliten seg‑s tazmert mi tella. Mi twan dayen, teɣli tgecrart teɛya; deg terkent i as‑tteggen amkan. Tettun‑tt tella alamma yeḥder‑d uẓekka.

Ay‑agi akk d asekkak, d arejdal i as‑id‑rnan. Aɛerqub n Uqbayli yeṣfa, aẓar‑is seg yemma‑s n ddunit i d‑yeswa. Tameṭṭut ɣur‑s, d taxriḍt n tudert ay tella. Deg‑s tarwa, deg‑s ttrika, d leɛmara n lḥara; tettezzi fell‑as leɛnaya. Rray fell‑as ur ixuḍ, win ifuden seg‑s i d‑yeswa. Teɛna axxam, terna berra; win ixaben ɣur‑s ad d‑yuɣal. D tamrayt, tezḍa axxam d tmetti; d agaraw n lbaḍna ay d isem‑is i lebda.

Deg tejmaɛt, ur tettemqabal d wat tmira; deg uxxam leṣran‑is yella. Yettban‑d lɛezz d ttnefxa ɣef ubernus yeddlen tuyat. Ferrunt timsal deg lbaḍna, ɣur‑sent i yettuɣal ccwer, neẓra; d tisiri akka ay tella. Tasuta yezwaren, deg tmeẓẓuɣt i as‑teɣra; tettaǧǧa‑d ttewṣaya i tsutwin i d‑iteddun. Awal deg yinzi yecfa, mi akken i asen‑yenna: « Tameṭṭut d lsas, argaz d ajgu alemmas. »

SEHAKI – HAMDANE ROSA

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Ḥaraga d yiwet n tumant tamettant (tadermant) iḥuzan tuget n yilmeẓyen ladɣa deg iseggasen‑agi ineggura acku tzad mačči d kra, xas akken nettat d amahi ameqqran anda yezmer umdan ad yeǧǧ tarwiḥt‑is ad yernu ula d imawlan‑is imeddukkal‑is d wid i as‑d‑izin mara s lmut n uɣilif.

Ihi d acu akk inezmer neɣ i tezmer ad teg tmental n tedyant‑a neɣ tumant‑a deffir n umdan neɣ i ugdud?

Ḥaraga, dayen yelhan imi d yiwet n temsalt neɣ ttawil s wayes tteffɣen yilmeẓyen seg tmurt‑nsen ɣer tmura tijenṭatin (tibaraniyin) iwakken ad nadin lxedma s wayes ara ad squcḍen aɣrum‑nsen, imi ulac lxedma di tmurt‑nsen, iwakken ad teffeɣ seg‑sen twaɣit‑nni n tuttra d tigellelt‑nni anda yuweḍ umdan ɣer‑s.

Di tazwara, d allal neɣ dettawil akken ad ibeddel abeḥri, daɣen akken ad d iḥelli taleqqimt n uɣrum ama i yiman‑is ama i twacult‑is ancta akk d asayes s tidi‑ines akken ad yeddu yes‑s.

Si tama nniḍen ad yebru i tunḍa‑nni d tuzya deg yiberdan d unekcum deg yir timkečmin (yir iberdan, zedwa‑t ... ). Tin yernan ɣer‑s ad yerfed iman‑is ama s tedrimt ama s wayen nniḍen. Taneggarut, anda yezmer ad yesnerni, ad yessiweḍ awal ɣef yidles d wansayen d leεwayed n tmurt‑is ama s ttawil‑at itraren neɣ s isaragen ... i ugdud ajenṭaḍ aken ad tiseḍmeε yes‑s.

Ḥaraga ad tt‑id‑naf si tama nniḍen d ayen ur nelhi ama i tmurt ama i yiman acku tgellu‑d ala s lexṣara. Di tazwara, tamurt ad teggri d tilemt s yilmeẓyen ad teqqel d tagellilt seg‑sen.

Si tama nniḍen, lmut n dir i umdan akken yegla s yiman‑is netta iruḥ ur d as‑teččur tcekkart‑is, ur yečči ur yeswwi, iruḥ akken d aleqqaq, iruḥ akken d amegur meskin. Tin yernan ɣer‑s, ad d arew i tmurt tawaɣit n lexsas di tedrimt d yiɣalen (ifasen) n lxedma (ixeddamen). Taneggarut, tesseggray‑d imawlan deg yir taswiεt, deg yir tudert nutni ḥarqen teḥreq tassa‑nsen tezlef teknef dayen kan.

Ihi ulayɣer ad isebbel temẓi‑is neɣ tudert‑is s lekmal akken kan ad iruḥ ad yinig daxel n ucabcaq n lluḥ anda akken tεelleq tudert‑is gar lumut d tudert.

Billal Luni.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Ili-k d amxalef...

Ur tezmireḍ ad ttḥettmeḍ i umdan akken ad yefhem acu txeddmeḍ, ṭṭaqa ttwaceklen, ttagaden ma banen‑d xulfen.

Ɣer kra, anadi d tuffɣa seg lqaleb d aḥtiter, ttmenyafen ad ɛanden ; izdeɣ‑iten ukukru werğin i tt‑fran di ṛṛay‑nsen.

Ɣer waṭas, asnulfu d unadi ɣef ujdid d tiselbi, kerhen ayen yellan d taẓuṛi neɣ d tiḥeṛci, ɣunfan ayen i ten‑izeglen.

Af‑d i yiman‑ik abrid, ddu i lebɣi‑ik mebla ndama, ur k‑id‑cliɛ seg wahat d wayen neɣ d wamek, sɛu kan iswiyen.

Eḍfer lğeṛṛa n wayen tḥemleḍ d wayen tebɣiḍ, d akessar neɣ d asawen, s ttawil, maca ilaq ad tezreḍ ayen ik‑ilaqen.

Ur kennu i wuguren n ddunit, ur yelli wayen ara k‑yeḍmen zheṛṛ, kullec yettas‑d s uxeddim, yal wa deg wayen yessen.

Ur ttɣim ara i lebda mebla ma tgiḍ kra, yessefk ad tebduḍ, sel i wul‑ik, di yal tagnit, anda tḥesleḍ d netta ara k‑iselken.

Wiyyaḍ ur tezmir ad sen‑t‑taɛjeb tɣawsa alamma tekfa, akka ttewhamen di kullec ! D ccek d tyita kan imi zewṛen.

Yewɛeṛ‑asen ad k‑fahmen neɣ ad ḥussen yis‑k, ur zṛin tigert, ẓẓay fell‑asen; tmuhun kan, ad s‑tiniḍ tedderɣel tmuɣli‑nsen !

Anef, ur tezmireḍ ara ad sen‑tesfehmeḍ kullec skud kečč mazal‑ik di tigawt ; kemmel, ala ayen tekfiḍ ara k‑yesfeṛḥen.

Ay akka d cbaḥa ! Tezdeg‑inek ak d lɛez‑inek jebbden ulawen, d iḥulfan werğin zmiren ad sen‑ḥussen ; wicqa ma deɣlen !

Imi i d‑tessakayeḍ ṛṛuḥ d kra n wayen i iṛuḥen i wid yegguman ad seṭɛeṛfen yis‑k ; dɣa s tidet‑nsen ad k‑ḥemlen ?

Kan akka, tessewhameḍ , ur k‑fhimen ara, acku d kečč i d amxalef ! Ur sḥissif ara, ḥsu belli qlilit wid i zemren ad k‑ssiweḍen.

Hamza Sahoui

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Illu n Spinoza (Dieu de Spinoza)

Dɣa d tidet Rebbi yettmeslay, ihedder ? Wis ur zriɣ ara, maca ma d sseḥ ha‑t‑an wacu izmer ad d‑yini, ladɣa i wid yettamnen. Ur tẓẓala, ur sgejdir, ur kkat aqerru‑ik(im) ɣer lqaɛa, ayen bɣiɣ ad xedmeḍ, ilaq ad tesfezwiḍ ɣef iɣallen idir tudert. wali, bedd, inig, efk azal i yiman‑ik(im), uwumi cced n uyeddid.

Bɣiɣ ad tezhuḍ, ad tecnuḍ, ad teɣreḍ… Ad tfarseḍ deg wayen ik‑d‑xelqeɣ. Xḍu‑k (kem) i tmezgida, d tɣemmar leǧwamaɛ i terriḍ d axxam –iw. Axam‑iw d idurar, d izuɣar, d isaffen deg‑sen i ttidireɣ, yis‑sen i d‑sefrayeɣ tayri‑iw ɣer tama‑k(m). Ur lliɣ d azaglu ɛebbant tuyat‑ik(im), werǧin hedreɣ s yir awal fell‑ak(am).

Kečč d aseggad(ut), ur ẓriɣ sani ara k‑tawi tuzuft‑ik(im). Ihi, ur ttlumu deg‑I ma shetrifen fell‑ak(am), neɣ ttkelixen yis‑m(k). rran‑k(m) d bwafif. Xḍu‑k(m) i uslebleb n tsurtin, d yeḍrisen ideyaniyen, acku ur zdin aẓar yid‑i.

Ur lliɣ deg yedlisen, anamek‑iw yezdi tafrara, yetteddu deg uɣelluy n yiṭij, neɣ bitt deg tmuɣli n umdakel neɣ tamdakelt, tmuɣli n tmeṭṭut‑ik, n urgaz‑im, n mmi‑k(m) d yelli‑k(m). Ur ttagad, ur tezzem iman‑ik(im), ur reffu, nekk d awezɣi ad ḍurreɣ imdanen i d‑xelqeɣ. D Nekk i d tayri yeṣfan, yeččuren ul‑ik(im) d afrayen, d tilisa, d iḥulfan akk d lebɣi d ccek…

Fkiɣ‑ak(am) aleggam, rriɣ‑ik(kem) d anefray neɣ d tanefrayt n tuder‑ik(im). Amek ara ak‑sḍelmeɣ ma yunef wallaɣ‑ik(im) ɣef wayen ẓẓiɣ deg‑k(m) Ula amek ad sḍelmeɣ tilin‑ik(im), acku d nekk i isuḍen izɣer deg‑k(m). Dɣa d tidet tumneḍ belli tella tmes i deg ara greɣ arraw‑iw yeffɣen i ubrid yerna i lebda?

Anwa ababat (yakuc) izemren ad yexdem tawaɣit yecban, anwa iwumi yefka wul‑is ad ger tasa‑s deg tmes n lebda? Mmer lliɣ s tugna‑agi, ur liɣ la leqder, la azal. Mmer bɣiɣ annuz‑nwen telli ɛemreɣ‑tt s yiqjan, qader iman‑ik(im), ur beqqu ad ak‑xedmen ayen akken ur tebɣḍ i yiman,‑ik(im).

Asirem‑iw, irwala tudert‑ik(im), frut tizza, zdit assaɣ gar‑awen d ugama. Serseɣ deg gar ifassen –ik(im), yal lxir, sbaɛdeɣ fell‑ak(am) ḍḍellam ssekniɣ‑d ɣer‑k(m) tiseḍwa ibaɛden. Sugen‑d times, neɣ lǧennet, kečč d ilelli, d awezɣi ad ak‑iniɣ ma tella tudert seld tamettant, maca bɣiɣ kan ad ak‑weṣṣiɣ, ad kem‑weṣṣiɣ:

Beddel abrid, mačči akka i tezmreḍ ad sbeggneḍ belli tumneḍ, tixer i usugen, d uɛezem warǧin nelli, ur k‑nniɣ amen yes‑i, maca ḥalfu, deg yiman‑ik(im), am akken zedɣeɣ deg‑k(m), ḥalfu yes‑i mi ara tettmeslayeḍ d warraw‑ik(im). Freḥ, zhu, sbeggen‑d tumert(im), ini‑d s ṣsut ad yebeɛzeq ayen triḍ. Tudert‑ik(im) tessefraḥ, fareṣ, ssew seg tala n usirem, mmeɣ ɣef wayen ters tiṭ‑ik(im), ur ttnadi fell‑i deg berra, acku d awezɣi ad iyi‑d‑tafeḍ.

Aqli da, deg ugama, sani wehhant wallen‑ik(im) ad maggrent tamuɣli‑iw.

Tasuqilt: TAYEB LOUNES

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Deg taggayt-agi ad tafem iḍrisen n tceqqufin n umezgun …

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# seqquitp umcrtm fYemseriyichad

# Iwudam :

1. Amɣar (Dda Muḥ), ireffu aṭas.
2. Tamɣart (Nna Saɛdiya), d nneyya.
3. Mmi‑s n umɣar (Qasi).
4. Tislit‑is (Werdiya).
5. Sin warrac (Aɣilas, Aksil).
6. Snat tullas (Kahina, Taninna).
7. Tiwelliyin

# Adeg: Deg uxxam

# Akud: Deg tegrest, ass n umenzu n yennayer

# Agzul n tceqquft:

D ass amenzun n yennayer; ɣef tafrara n wass, Dda Muḥ yenhewal, yessak‑id akk iɛeggalen n uxxam, yessseqdec‑iten akk akken ad heggin imensi n yennayer.

Deg tceqquft‑agi, ad d‑nerr tamuɣli d lwelha‑nneɣ ɣer yiwen wansay gar wansayen n Yimaziɣen d umezruy‑ines: wagi d yennayer.

# A. Tafelwit Tamenzut:

*Asayas amenzu 1

Aẓwan n Yidir (Ay alxir-inu) neɣ n Newara (Ad ak-weṣṣiɣ a mmi ɛzizen)

Yekcem‑d Dda Muḥ, yelḥa ɣef telwiḥin, imuqel ɣer ssaɛa‑ines( tamert), yewwet taɛekkazt‑is.

Dda Muḥ :Wa tamɣart! Wa tamɣart!

Nna Saɛdiya, tekcem‑d ɣer telwiḥin akken kan i d‑tekker seg tguni, tafunart‑is teɣli, acebbub‑is yeẓẓuffi.

Nna Saɛdiya: Anɛm, d acu yeḍran ay amɣar? Niɣ d lxir kan?

Dda Muḥ :Ass yecban ass-a, kunwi mazal-iken tegnem!

Nna Saɛdiya: D acu yellan ass-a?

Dda Muḥ :Mmekt-id neɣ ad kem-ddzeɣ! Ula d kemm tettuḍ!

Nna Saɛdiya: Waqila ad tgeḍ tameɣra, nekkni ur naɛlim, ur negza?!

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Dda Muḥ: Ahya Rebbi! Akra n lehḍur! A d imensi n yennayer. Ayya saki-ten-id akk!

Tamɣart: S ttawil s ttawil ay amɣar. Aɛni ddan-d fell-aneɣ. Ar d yali wass, ad d-kkren.

Dda Muḥ: Wa Qasi! Wa Werdi! Wa Aɣiles! Wa Aksel! Wa Kahina! Wa Taninna! Nna Saɛdiya, terra ifassen‑is ɣef uqerru, tessetbaɛ‑it s tmuɣli. Yekcem‑d Qasi (mmi‑s n umɣar), yewwi‑d yid‑s taɛekkazt, iɣil d imakaren i d‑yewwḍen ɣer tqaɛet.

Qasi: Wa baba! D acu yeḍran?

Terna tekcem‑d tmeṭṭut n Qasi (Werdiya), tettcuddu aggus‑is akken kan i d‑tekker seg yiḍes.

Werdiya: Ay amɣar! D lxir kan?

Arrac akk, mseḍfaren‑d wa deffir wa, kecmen‑d ɣef telwiḥin, xelɛen seg uɛeggeḍ‑nni n jeddi‑tsen.

Dda Muḥ: Ayya qimet! Qimet

Dda Muḥ, yewwi‑d aɣerbal d terbut, yefka‑ten i teslit (Werdiya); yeddem‑d acekkar n lxeḍra, yerna‑d sebɛa n yimenda (neɣ asqi aquran) akken ad ten‑yefk i temɣart ad theggi asqi.

Dda Muḥ: A tamɣart! Ax acekkar-agi n lxeḍra akked sebɛa-agi n yimenda. Arrac, ttwalin kan, wehmen deg wayen ixeddem umɣar‑agi.

Dda Muḥ: Wa Qasi! Kečč, siwel i twelliyin-nneɣ!

Arrac: A jeddi! D acu yeḍran? Ayen i d aɣ-d-tessakiḍ ɣef lefjer? I wacu tarbut? I wacu imenda? ɣef wacu ara d-tɛerḍeḍ tiwelliyin?

Amɣar: A terwa! Ass-agi, d amenzu n yennayer.

Arrac: D acu i d yennayer?

Dda Muḥ: Yyaw a terwa! Ma d kunemti aya dhumt tur d ccɣel-nkent!

Tamɣart: Ay amɣar! Cacnaq, ur tt-yeṭṭif ara deg ccedda akken i tt-teṭṭfeḍ keččini!

# B. Tafelwit tis snat:

*Asayas wis sin 2

Aẓwan n Yidir (A baba-inu ba…)

Tislit, tfettel seksu; tamɣart, tesselxes imenda yernu txeddem lxeḍra; Qasi, iruḥ ad d‑yeɛreḍ tiwelliyin; amɣar, yessaɣay times; arrac, qimen ad slen I wayen ara asen‑d‑ 3 yini jeddi‑tsen.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Amɣar, yekker‑d ileḥḥu ɣef telwiḥin.

Amɣar: D acu i d yennayer a terwa? Ass yecban ass-a, di 950 uqbel talalit n Sedna Ɛisa, tella-d tedyant n Cacnaq akked Yiferɛunen anda sekkren ṭṭrad ɣef yiwet n temnaḍt n Yimaziɣen i wum qqaren Siwa.

Ur d‑yekfi ara umɣar awal, tamɣart tenteq‑d.

Tamɣart: Yennayer, yebḍa ɣef sin yiḥricen, a terwa! Yen= d yiwen neɣ d amenzu, ma d ayer d aggur neɣ d ayyur; meḥsub d aggur amenzu ɣer Yimaziɣen.

Kahina: Anwa i d Cacnaq a jeddi?

Amɣar: D amaziɣ yesseɣlin agellid n Maser RamsesII, tessbedd tagelda tis 22 dinna.

Aɣiles: Ayen nsewway seksu s uyaziḍ a yaya?

Tamɣart: Deg ṭṭrad-agi a terwa, Cacnaq, yessawel akk i yimnayen-is akked yirgazen yesɛan tazmert d tebɣast, ad mɛawanen acku d ṭṭrad iweɛren akked yiferɛunen; dɣa ula d tulawin, tebɛent imnayen-a ɣer wasif n nnil, wwint yid-sent iyuzaḍ. Tin iluḥqen ɣer din ad as-tefk ayaziḍ-nni i Bucḥiḍ, netta ad t-yezlu, syin ad t-yerr ɣer daxel n Nnil, akken alammi yuɣal akk d azewwaɣ s yidammen-nni. Imnayen iferɛunen mi walan annect-a, uggaden ad d-qarben ɣur-sen, ɣilen d yimnayen-nsen akk i yekfan, uɣalen ɣer deffir, dɣa ɣelben-ten yimazaiɣen. Tameddit-nni, sewwen akk iyuzaḍ-nni i zlan sfuglen yis-sen rrbeḥ-nsen. Seg wass-nni i zellun iyuzaḍ i yimensi n yennayer, ma d aṭṭan n yiyuzaḍ semman-as Bucḥiḍ (ɣer win i ten-yekfan s tmezla)

Aẓwan (A yimensi n yennayer…)

Werdiya: A tamɣart! Ula d nekk ad kem-seqsiɣ, ayɣer sebɛa n yimenda i nxeddem di yennayer?

Tamɣart: Ula d kemm ur teẓriḍ ara! Akken ad ǧǧuǧǧgen Wat-Uxxam akken ǧǧuǧǧugen yimenda-agi.

Amɣar: Ayen sebɛa n yisufar a yelli? D ayen i aɣ-d-tettak lqaɛa-agi iɣef nleḥḥu akked wakal-a iɣef nettnaɣ. Yal ass, nesɛa asafar ara nečč, maca ass n yennayer nesdukkul isufar-a ɣef tikkelt akken ad neḥmed Sidi Rebbi.

Tekker‑d Tninna.

Taninna: A jeddi! D acu nniḍen i xeddmen deg yennayer?

Amɣar: Ttseṭṭilen i warrac imescṭaḥ: win ilulen uqbel yennayer, ttekksen cwiṭ seg ucebbub-is; ma d win yemmden, ttekksen-as-t akk, d asfillet akken ad yimɣur.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
Tamɣart: di yennayer, mmi ara nebḍu ayaziḍ-nni:

- Tifertin, nettakk-itent i tullas akken ad ferfrent am tsekrin.
- Timessaḍin i warrac akken ad qewwin.
- Ma d ayen nniḍen, i yiɛeggalen i d-yeggran.

Amɣar: A tamɣart! Tettuḍ belli nettaǧǧa amur i win yunagen, nettakk-it i win ixussen, d asfillet akken ad d-yuɣal s axxam bxir.

Tamɣart: Tanemmirt ay amɣar, wellah ar yeffeɣ akk seg uqerruy-iw. Yernu yella ula deg usefru n At-Zik:

# Yennayer

|*Cfiɣ-as i wass-nni|*S tumlilt, iɣerban selɣen|
|---|---|
|Negga-d imensi|Inyen ttwabeddlen|
|S uyaẓiḍ akked seksu|Abeɛɛuc s yimensi-s|
|*£as iminig ur yelli|*Arrac, ass-nni ttseṭṭilen|
|Ur yeffiɣ tidmi|Akken ad imɣuren|
|Amur-is ur t-ntettu|Tisirit-a s wazal-is|
|*Tawwurt n useggas teldi|*£ur-wat ay imeẓyanen|
|Yennayer ad d-yezzi|Ad awen-kellxen|
|S talwit d tdawsa ad d-iglu|Yal aɣref s wansayen-is|

Asefru seg udlis n useggas amenzu n ulmud alemmas sb 65

C. Tafelwit Tis kraḍet:

*Asayas wis kraḍ 3

Imensi, yewwa; Qasi, yuɣal‑d, yewwi‑d yid‑s tiwelliyin, msalamen akk, temlal tasa d wayen turew. Qimen, zzin‑d i terbut‑nni n seksu s yiyuzaḍ i d‑yersen.

Aẓwan n ṭṭbel (Iḍebbalen).

Sɣur Benmuhub Ḥuriya (Bucali)

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Tirga-w d asefru:

# ASEKKIR AMEZWARU.

Asenked : Amnay, d yiwen yilemẓi i tɣur tmurt, d amdan ittfeggiḍen d tiktiwin; uwḍen tura ukuz n yiseggasen segmi i d-yeffeɣ tasdawit n Blida, ideg yeɣra "l'aviation": tagi d yiwet tussna icudden ɣer tmesrifgin. Daɣ netta tirga-ines urzent akk ɣer tmesriffegt-agi. Maca seg yimru ɣer lbala. Ih d acu tenwam ad t-id isaḥ deg tmurt yeččan … Ahbuh ad nessusem axir.

‑ Amnay : Wa yesbeṛ, wa yeqbeṛ, wa yettnadi amek ara yezger lebḥer.

D inzi agi i d-yesselḥeq Silas deg yimi n Amnay tasebḥit n wass-a mi d-yerza ɣer lxedma.

‑ Silas : A sbaḥ lxir a ben ɛemmi, acu akka tesgarmudeḍ tasebḥit n Rebbi.

‑ Amnay : Azul a Silas, tixer kan a wlidi meqqar d lehdur ad ten‑id nini.

Ass mi niqal yeffeɣ i ubrid, yettaṭaf agirru d leḥyuḍ deg tzerbatin n taddart, yekker mmi-s n ɛemmi-s Silas yessukes-it-id seg tkerkas, yewwi-t ixeddem yid-s, reggin taxmirt, ssalayen llajur, srusuyen sselɛa ...

‑ Silas : Ayen akka tessusmeḍ kan ay Amnay, mačči niqal tebɣiḍ ad ten‑id‑tekfuḍ, trefdeḍ ula d asefru.

‑ Amnay : Ma nenṭeq ad aɣ‑ddmen, ma nessusem ad nettwaɛfes.

‑ Silas : Waqil s tidet‑ik, allen‑ik bezgent, imi‑k isereḥ. Cukkeɣ iwet‑ik ṭaglal, neɣ d aḍu‑nni n leɛca i ihuzzen allaɣ‑ik, yessaki‑d tirga‑k ?

‑ Amnay : Acu ak‑iniɣ, yecweḍ wul yegla s tasa, ma d tagi i d tudert nekk ɣuri tif‑itt lmut.

‑ Silas : Amen‑iyi ar qrib ur k‑ɛqileɣ. Seg yimi‑k ad‑ttefɣen yimeslayen yecban terẓeg n qeḍran ? Anida yuɣal uqcic‑nni i yebnan s tirga, i iheddren ɣef tirga, winna akken yecɣeb usirem, yettwalin tafat n uzekka.

‑ Amnay : dayen qeḍɛeɣ layas, ufiɣ‑d ula s leqraya‑w d awezɣi ad awḍeɣ lebɣi n wul‑iw, wissen ahat ma d lǧameɛ i nhudd imi yura lḥif ɣef unyir. Mačči d deɛwessu tura tagi ?

Ifassen xeddmen, imawen heddren. Xaḍen-tt-id akk sya w sya, ayen yellan deg wulawen yuli-d ɣef yilsawen, yeffeɣ-d yeṭṭerḍeq-d am rrɛud.

‑ Amnay : (si lɣiḍ nni i t-ikecmen yenna-as) Teẓriḍ, ma tkemmel akka, ulac win ara y‑id‑yessuksen seg yirebbi n ḥerraga. Ih ! d acu i ten yuɣen wigi i icergen ilel s teflukin.

‑ Silas : (ibat, s yiwen n ṣṣut ideg tettban tugdi) Amek ? ma ɣur‑k tagi d tifrat, nekk ttwaliɣ‑tt d tawaɣit, d tinifift. Tɛemdeḍ ad tegreḍ iman‑ik ger wuglan (tuɣmas) n yilel !?

‑ Amnay : Nekk d wagi kan i d abrid i d‑yeggran ad taɣeɣ ma bɣiɣ ad idireɣ tirga‑w, yak lmut fell‑ 3 aɣ tettgani tarewla ula sani, ad mmteɣ da neɣ dihin.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
‑Silas :(iwala ssaɛa) Attan tewweḍ d ttnac, iyan tura ad nečč talqimt, xas akken d aɣrum s zzit maca Rebbi iɛuzz‑it, syin ad d‑nesseqɛed tiktiwin, ad nennaɣ layas i d‑yerzan ass‑a.

Qqimen ɣer lqaɛa, bdan tuččit. Talqimt tamenzuti i iger Amnay ɣer yimi-s iwala ifassen-is

‑Amnay : Ttemyif icerrigen n yifassen‑iw wala wid n wul‑iw.

‑ Silas : Iḥqa dɣa, ur ẓriɣ ara ayen i temɣi tekti‑agi n yinig deg wallaɣ‑ik.

Ǧɛel‑as ass‑a ldint tewwura tewwiḍ‑d ttriḥ (le visa) ɣer fransa.

‑Amnay : (ihuzz aqerru-s yerra-as-d s usefru-a) Acḥal yeccbeḥ wass‑a, akustim ihegga Ttesriḥ ɣef ṭṭabla, tenṭeq tenna‑yi yemma Ruḥ a mmi di lehna, sellem‑iyi ɣef sut Fransa.

‑Silas : (ittecmumuḥ) Kemmel, kemmel, twenneɛ.

‑ Amnay :Fɣeɣ‑d seg uxxam s teḍsa, abrid‑iw uɣeɣ‑t qbala :

Γer unafag n Dar Lbiyḍa, ṭṭfeɣ timesriffegt syinnaDeg yigenni tɛella, walaɣ‑d Lzayer imerra.
‑ Silas : (Yeḍsa) I tura tewwḍeḍ neɣ mazal ?

‑  Amnay :

|Ɛefseɣ akal n Fransa|Ṭjur‑is segment ta ɣer ta|
|---|---|
|I iqeblen tirga|Tilewḥin si yal tama|
|Tirumyin sya w sya|Lpari mi i d‑iyi teẓra tefreḥ teḍsa|
|Acḥal teccbeḥ tmurt‑a|I yilemẓẓi tefka lqima.|

Aqcic, yeɣreq deg targit-is ihedder amzun yettidir taswiɛt, sya ɣer da ad d-yeḍs, yenwa dayen yewweḍ ɣer lɣerba. Mmi-s ɛemmi-s iwala d akken d lawan ad t-id yessaki si tnafa.

‑Silas :

Ekker, ekker a gma Timesriffegt ters‑d ɣef lqaɛa Dayen tirga‑k tekfa Nunag, nuɣal‑d almi d da.

‑Amnay : (iger‑d nnehta, s usḥissef) Tirga‑w d ayen n lɛali Γef uzref nneɣ ur t‑id fki Mennaɣ‑tt i yal ilemẓi Ad nruḥ deg yigenni ad nɛelli Imi tamurt tegguni Ulawen ad awḍen lebɣi.

‑  Silas  :Wid  i  aɣ  icewwlen  wwḍen  lebɣi  nsen,  ma  d  nekkni  truḥ  temẓẓi‑nneɣ.  Kker  fell‑ak yurǧa‑aɣ uxeddim, ma d tamurt yiwwas ahat ad tseggem.

‑ Amnay : Ahbuh...!

# Timenɣit taberkant

Ddunit‑a s yiԐejjajen‑nnes d usallas; ideg tettbedda Tifawin ur nexliḍ 14 n yiseggasen deg yila, tekker‑d deg yinuɣen n lwaldin, ass ur nԐeddi war imeṭṭawen; i as‑yeččin tiṭṭawin mndun tutawin‑nnes, leqrar‑nnes werԐad ur yefri ca, jar tɣimit id n tmeṭṭut n baba‑s d tarbibt, tay d tiggujla sa ddren lwaldin, u tarbibt adeg –nnes deg uxxam ulac… niɣ d aḍfar n yemma‑s u tezra matta had tt‑yettrajan ɣer tsednan n xwali‑s…leqrar yifen matta tetthenna d anjli.

Ass‑idin mfahmen, tekker‑d mani tafukt urԐad ur d‑tegri ca izenzaren‑nnes; ayen i d‑tlayem seg wureɣ n tmeṭṭut n baba‑s ur yedris, tekkes‑it‑id d tuffra…awal tegri‑t jar‑as d yiman‑nnes yemmed… d tarsast ma tekker‑d ur tettlawa ca ad twella timendeffert… yyin i teğğa urԐad deg wammas n tirja… tarjit tameqrant i d‑iwellan d tidet, d tarewla –idin i d‑terwel u tessattam ur trenni ca ad d‑tuɣal.

Qadda n yilel, tarbaԐt n yilemziyen ttrjan‑tt… win s usawal yettirar, way yeggar isurifen, taruḥit d twellit; win daya n yiceqfan i d‑yettwellan seg waman… ma d ccaf ileɣɣeḍ syun: « ur tennim ca had nḍal ammay, yyin had naf dun miss ma had rajan…», yiğ teɣni‑t tehyuyt –idin yellan ur as‑teḍsi ca tmeddurt deg wudem seg wasmi i tt‑yessen,… kuz n temmar (4H) ur d –tewwiḍ ca, aqeyyal deg ujenna yerza‑asen ixfawen… araji ɣer‑s tilisa, alli had d‑yerg…Ԑezmen ad kkren; taflukt tengug… yus‑d ugerzi qič yettlaɣa‑d daya n tmejjin n uhyuy‑idin i as‑yeslin yessiwel: « rajat rajat ddmam, tumert tban‑d ɣef wudem‑nnes, a‑tt‑an tus‑d…», ḥebsen annak qič n tqeyyart tuḍu zdat‑sen war tabeddit… tekker teflukt, win ineggez‑d ur hen‑yeḍfir ca, iruḥ yettazzal annak taneffut ulac; idammen ttcercren‑d… ziɣ d afaqi i as‑faqen ɣef tikkurda…tewwi‑as‑d tamettant blac.

Imir‑idin tehwa‑d tmeqqit n unẓar, yila ujenna, ɣef matta iḍran yid n baba‑s d yelli‑s,… truḥ Tifawin d asfel; am nettat am labas n tutawin‑nnes yettwanɣayen…ḥermen‑asen ussan n tmeddurt, d usirem i yessaram yal amezzyan ɣir ad yeggeԐmer…urԐad timenɣit n derri tegguma ad tberka deg tmurt‑nneɣ, ulac n usaḍuf( lqanun) had yinin win yenɣin ad yettwaneɣ, akma yella d lwaldin a ineqqen tsa‑nsen.

Zenni Manel

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Nanna xedduja

Win i tt‑yezrin ur d‑yeqqar ca tay seg udrar; tegma‑d deg uԐcuc n ucal, jar 4 n wayetma‑s; tekkes cci i sԐant tqeyyarin, tutawin‑idin‑nnes, akma d tamɣart deg 60 n yiseggasen, tif‑ihent deg legder d taɣisi.

Tḍerru sen –idin n tcendaḍ i d‑teggar ɣef waziwen‑nnes, yebberken uzaw –nnes am ujaref –idin iseg ttuččen lemtul, niɣ am yiḍan‑idin n tejrest ideg ur d‑tegri c tziri, Tiṭṭawin‑nnes zegzwent am yilel, u ttberurriqent seg lebԐidt … rrzanet d ssfayet; tiggilli teggil, ma tbedd zdat n temɣarin; teqqur seg tfednin ɣer yixef; ad tinid idammen ur gguren ca deg‑s, ahat daya iɣef tettban d tawraɣt u d tazdadt, imi‑nnes am ubrim‑idim amezzyan yennekmec; ma teqfel‑it yettban yegni, tiɣmas‑nnes urğin hennan‑hent ɣir ad tettutlay niɣ ad tetteffez; ɣer‑s ca n lhibeyyet win i tt‑ihennan ur yettrafad ca tiṭṭawin‑nnes; jamek ttḥebbaren‑tt, yerni tettwaggad; tezzeddeɣ‑d tsusmi ɣir ad tehmel; ad tinid d arr i d‑ inekkben.

Deg teqliԐt‑idin ur sellen ca ma truḥ axxam n yimuḍan, tettdawa iman‑nnes s yiman‑nnes, teṭṭef deg yisennila d yisufar n yimɣiyen i d‑txeddem s ufus‑nnes, akkma llan ttawilat yessishilen tameddurt imir‑a; tcehhel arebbi n yiguzaḍ n waԐraben; u ɣir ad ggԐemren tetteg‑ihen d aberbuc; win i t‑yemḍin wad yečč iḍuḍan‑nnes, teṭṭef aṭas n yinezgam deg wul‑nnes, macan ḥedd ma itthenna‑tt terfa, dima taḍsa, d tumert banen‑d ɣef wudem‑nnes .. teqfez yerni ruḥ deg tenfusin i d –tettales i ddrari imezzyanen a yeḥlant u a tceffa fell‑asent.

Asmi nesla temmut ḥedd ma yeqqim ur d‑yerzif ca aqewwar ideg tedder u tegguma ad tekker seg‑s ald i tuta ḍar, iɣber‑itt ucal.

# Turi-t Zenni Manel.

# Insi d uccen

Zik n zik ald i yettutlayen yiɣersiwen, yella cra n yinsi yeffud, yerga bac ad iruzzi ɣef tmeqqit n waman, deg ubrid‑nnes yufa cra n tanut d tamezzyant, ineggez ɣer daxel jamek fad yenɣi‑t, yeswa ald yerwa, mi i iruḥ ad d‑yerg ur yufi ca mammek, yeqim yettraja manni way had d‑iԐeddan, deg wammin annak iԐedda‑d wuccen, ula d netta yeffud, iqqel ɣer tanut ihenna insi, yeḍsa ɣer‑s wuccen yenna‑as: mukca tudfed din ay insi?

YuԐa‑as‑d win: daya isehlen, Ԑelleq‑d iman‑nnek ɣef yixef n usɣun, tehwid‑d ɣer‑i, netta iԐelleq iman‑nnes yebda ihugga, insi yeṭṭef deg yixef aneddi.

Uccen ihugga insi yettali, mlaqqan deg tlemmast n tanut, yenna‑as wuccen i yinsi: mani tiled??

Yenna‑as: d tay d dummet cra yettali cra ihugga.

# Turi-t: Zenni Amel seg tsekla n zik

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Taqliɛt n Buzina

Ur as‑ucin azal jar tmura ad tettwassen, ur tt‑ǧǧin ad tettwandel, yyiḍ ttjebban fell‑as, yyiḍ ruḥen beƐden‑as, yuca‑as Rebbi lbehwet d thuski sƔer‑s, d taqliƐt yemma‑s n teqliƐin, TaqliƐt n Buzina.

Tikli deg‑s ur tetteǧǧa ca imi ad yessusem, taqliƐt‑a d itri seg yitran yessifawen taƔiwant n Buzina, tuca‑as aruḍ d amaynut, zlin‑d fell‑as yidurar am tnewwart, deg talƔa Ɛunni d aqellal, tus‑d jar teqliƐt n Mezlin d wadeg seg teqliɛt n Sammer qqaren‑as « tibḥirin », tikli srid Ɣer teqliƐt‑a tettawi Ɣer telwiḥt tƐelleq, yettwari deg‑s « taqliƐt n Buzina » s yisekkilen n tlatinit d tifinaɣ.

Deg wadaf n teqliƐt ttqabalent‑id tiddar ttwaṣkant s uẓru d ucal, d tiqdimin, ttwabnant deg tallit n Fransa, cra d ixxamen ilin deg‑sent yudan, cra d tiḥuna, tiddar‑a mseddant ad tinid d tirekkabin, tikli Ɣef tama tafusit n tmasext n teqliƐt tettawi Ɣer cra ljameƐ qqaren‑as :

« LƐatiq », ma tikli Ɣef tama tazelmaḍt yettqabal‑itt‑id uḥellaq n usuf, s waman‑nnes izeddganen, d treƐqay ččurent d tiseḍwa d wurtiyen. Daxel yettaf umdan ukuẓ n teƐwini, ttnekkarent‑id seg yideflawen yefsin, niƔ s wanẓaren yutin s legder. aman‑nsent ḥlan ula i tsessi, taƐwint tamezwarut qqaren‑as : « tiṭ n tabƔa », aman‑nnes rragen‑d seg tmurt ttayzayen, snnej‑nnes yettqabal‑d qli n lkaf qqaren‑as : « lkaf n tsiwant », aman n teƐwint‑a gguren deg qli n terga, tteswayen yis‑sen yudan.

Ɣer nnej qič n teƐwint‑aya tella teƐwint n « sut ∑ebdella », aman‑nnes rrayen‑d seg ttiqan n ufsil n cra n tmeṭṭut i mumi qqaren : « Faṭima ut ∑ebdella ». seg tama tafusit n teƐwint‑a tella qli n teƐwint qqaren‑as : « ∑ebd ssadeq », aman n kraḍ n teƐwinin‑aya ttemlilen deg usuf. Ma d taƐwint taneggarut qqaren‑as tala ḥelluf Alay Ɣer ljameƐ, tettqabal‑it‑id txennaqt d taḥellaqt, qqaren‑as : « Xeẓrun », i d‑yettnekkaren Ɣir ad tili lgerret.

Taqliɛt d adeg n wakkas Ɣef wul d usgunfu, ttasen‑d Ɣer‑s seg yal tamnaḍt, awladi ma tireḍ aƐlaw amellal deg tejrest, niƔ twella d tazegzawt deg tefsut, niƔ deg wakud mani sfugilen s yennar d tfeswin tessenƐat‑d isennila‑neγ, akkedma ur as‑tuci ca ddulet‑nneγ azal d ameqqran, ad teqqim teqliƐt s wazal‑nnes.

Turi-t ZENNI Manal

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Udmawen : Dihya ; Amira, tamƔart, yemma‑s n Dihya

Ad truḥ Dihya ɣer tesnawit s tmelḥeft, u ad temlil yid n tmeddukkelt‑nnes Amira.

# AMIRA

azul ! hiiii i wa matta teggid deg yiman‑nnem ?!!!!

# DIHYA

maƔer ? matta yellan !!!!

# AMIRA

bleɛqel bleɛqel !! matta way i tirḍed ass‑a ?!!!!

# DIHYA

irḍeƔ ammin i ttraḍen yudan.

# AMIRA

hhhhhhh aruḍ‑aya yexḍa n uƔerbaz.

# DIHYA

maƔef ?? tay d timelḥeft am nettat am waruḍ yeǧǧ.

# AMIRA

semḥ‑ay a weltma, macan aruḍ‑aya n tmeɣriwin, yexḍa way quḥ d adeg‑nnes !

# DIHYA

maɣef ? , yerg‑d usaḍuf (lqanun) d amaynut, ur nesli ca yis‑s !, irḍeɣ timelḥeft d tajbibt n lejdud‑inu, way d lasel d uxenfuf‑nneɣ, ɣer‑s azal d ameqqran, yerni yesser.

# AMIRA

ih d tidet yesser, besseḥ maɣer ass‑a i tirḍed amma

# DIHYA

yaxxah mani tettilid !!!! ur teẓrid ca matta yellan ass‑a ??

# AMIRA

araḥa !

# DIHYA

ihi amensi ad cem‑ɛerḍeɣ, taseḍ‑d ad tetɛecciḍ ɣer‑neɣ, w ad teẓreḍ matta yellan ass‑a ?

Tṣuna udfent tnelmadin ad qrant … Ɣer umensi annak Amira tessṭebṭub ɣef uxxam n Dihya

# AMIRA

mselxir fell‑awen

# AYT TADDART

azul fell‑am ; ad nsuf yis‑m ɛedda‑d.

# DIHYA

i wa nanna mda had teẓred ! Amira ur teẓri ca matta yellan ass‑a ?!!!

Twejjed‑d yemma‑s n Dihya amensi ɣef lmayda ɛeddan ukkel ad ččen

# TAMƔART

bismillah bismillah ncallah ad yili d aseggas amerbuḥ, yeččur d talwit d tumert, wad d‑iwella fell‑aneɣ s lxir d lbaraket

# AMIRA

welleh a Dihya la fehmeɣ walu, ad tinid la tteddreƔ deg tmurt‑inuɣ

# TAMƔART

( teḍsa ) : a yell‑i ass‑a d amenzu n yennayer, d ixef n useggas ɣer yimaziƔen.

# AMIRA

yaa ziƔ yella useggas yeǧ bla lmiladi d lhiǧri ?!!!!!!!!!!

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
DIHYA : hiiiih a weltma, aseggas imaziɣen weḥd‑s sefhem‑as a nanna mukca yella leḥsab‑nneƔ ?

TAMƔART : necni a Amira a yell‑i, zik icawiyen ḥessben akud s leflaḥet, s leflaḥet i nẓerr melmi tettili tefsut, tajrest, anebdu d tmenzut…

AMIRA : hi yennar, matta yella, u maɣef i as‑semman amma, u melmi i d‑yettas ???

TAMƔART : yennayer deg‑s sen n wawalen : yen = amezwaru, ayer= yur; d yur amezwaru ɣer yimaziƔen, yettili iḍ n 13 janfi irumyyen, jamek deg wass‑a i yerna Cicnaq agellid‑nneɣ, agellid n yiferɛunen Ramsis; seg syidin bdun ḥessben‑t d ixef useggas u netta a yezwaren amezruy n lmiladi d win lhijri jamek newweḍ‑d 2969.

AMIRA : tanemmirt‑nwen, ass‑a i fehmeɣ amezruy‑nneɣ aḥeqqani, u syamma daymen yuma ad nesfugil yis‑s wad t‑nuɛa d tafaska taɣelnawt.

Zenni Manal.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Jar n Yimi d Usekkil

Amezruy n wemdan yeqqen id n tmurt mani ilul‑d u yegmi, seg ucal ani‑s ay yetwexleq di tikti tamezwarut. D taqṣiṭṭ yeṭṭuẓeṭṭen; falu ɣer uma‑s, aldira ad yemmir usili n ifeǧǧajen ayes ad iqam uẓeṭṭa n yal timetti deg umaḍal. Qqaren amdan d mmi‑s n twennaṭ‑nnes, amkan ani yerxa iẓuṛan s wegtay.

Maziɣ mani yella, jar‑annes d ucal n tmurt‑nnes iseɣwan ay yellan ur yezmir ad d‑tuqablen s wagel n Qaṛun d Ferɛun! Al ass‑a, ad yezmer ad yesmeḥ deg aṛuḍ‑nnes ur isemmeḥ ca di terdast nniɣ ahemmiṣ si treɛqay‑nnes. Ccan d nnif iṭṭawwad lḥedd aneggaru aldira argaz bab n tmurt ad yerfed tgersa u ibetta ikkerrez i tɣemmayt n tfeswin, nniɣ tin sdat n uwessu. D amdan netta d amezwaru d uneggaru ay itteččarayen tamzirt s wa ay yiqedden i lemmali d tarwa‑nnes.

Texḍa tamurt ay yettučen lexyurat ammin wehdes ma welli ca n ufus t‑yettabbaɛen qič s qič. Amezruy n umaziɣ amezwaru d aqbuṛ, d tuta n tmurt d iẓerwa, iẓerwa ay yikettan matta ay yeḍran zik. S usekkil “Alibi”, nniɣ “Tifinaɣ”, yetwaǧǧ weltum s mayes nečnin nefdek tiṭṭawin‑nneɣ ɣef matta aɣen‑nnan u weṣṣan ayet n imir‑a. D tict n teqṣiṭṭ s sen n wudmawen, Tamurt d wemdan, amezruy d “Tfinaɣ”.

Amsal di teẓrut d awalen tusekken d izamulen ččuṛen d rremgat d tenfas, yes‑sen ɛebban wulawen u jemmen allen aldira faḍen u felqen ma hennid d tḥemmamt n lefrdus di tlemmast n temsunt. Isekkilen twaḥejmen, ḥerqṣen s labas n thusi d inumak, qqaren aherrar ay yeffer yiles daxel n yimi ay yegguman ad yeqqen aked ma yella ussan iberkanen xsent ad izemm u ad iɛuggen. Tewweḍ‑aneɣ “Tfinaɣ”, ddren isekkilen mamek ay yedder maziɣ d umezruy‑nnes.

Mamek nella ad nnili ma welli ca n isekkilen?! “Tira” nettat d isugal n tmusniwin s mayes yezmer ad yebbi yebriden s tikli ɣer dat u ad yeṣṣiɣer igmiren lkul amek i llan bla awelli ɣer deffer. Amdan yetmetta beṣṣeḥ awal‑nnes ad yedder u ad ikemmel tmudri, imal d yiwal u ugar n yisuggasen d leqṛun ... S tira n yiles d wawal yexḍa s timawit.

Yal aseggas yetmetta wemɣaṛ nniɣ d temɣaṛt u xeččan yid‑sen aqenṭar n wawalen d wannayen ay yifessin u truḥan ammin berk mamek a truḥan waman s‑ddu n tfukt n yulyez. Jar n tmudri n baba d yemma d tmudri inu tetwaɛṛeq Tcawit. Yal aseggas tetmetta tamkerḍit, tasekla yewwi‑t usuf, qli d attaw, qli d astehzi, u qli d utay n nneḥ.

Di tsirt n wussan yettemmeḍran weflu, wa d‑yegguren yif wa ay yiɛeddan. Tella “Tmaziɣt” d leḥram, lḥebs d ddwa n wa t‑yennan, ass‑a, yuli‑d ufuk n lḥeqq, tetna Tcawit tetwarqam di zmam. Imir‑a yezmer yict ad yini u ad yemru matta ad as‑d‑yusin deg ixef, deg iḍ, deg ass, deg uselkim, deg umsiwel, uqqan sebbat i wa yettafen sbayeb. Tcawit d yiles n tutlayt, n wemru, n tezrigt, n zmamat d yeɣmisen, wa ay yexsen ad yerni di‑s; d tarennayt deg iman‑nnes netta, xaṭer tayemmat d ẓar ssi‑s a twalqamen tnuqlin ad yeǧǧen teẓgi n timmuzɣa akkas d tazizawt.

Yunes Aɣugali.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Tawrirt-nneɣ d idurar

Tella cṛa n tidet ur yezmir i yict ad t‑iberber; Tgama nettat d yemma‑tneɣ, ssi‑s a nekker u ɣer‑s a d‑netwella nexs nniɣ nemmexs. Tizzuzut n idurar d turawin ay yeṣṣuḍayen taneffut n tmudri.

Yal taṣeṭṭa d amaḍal ay yessuktuyen deg iḍ u deg ass bla ayaḥbas, d luzin ur yetberka amsiwi, di tsusmi d tezdeg ḥed ur as‑yetfaq.

Taṣeṭṭa d adrar u wedrar d taṣeṭṭa, wa d azgen n wa bac ad ssergen taẓeṛbit n Uḥellaq i yifesren d iɛessasen ɣef ijenwan, iṣeffaḥen d iɣeẓṛan.

Deg Awras ad d‑naf Celyet, Furar, Bezzaz, Icc n Yedgel, Bellezma, Sidi Rɣis, d ismawen yetwasnen di yal tama n tɣemmaṛ: Xencla, Batent, Um Lebwagi. Yal adrar ɣer‑s tɣawsa t‑yetteǧǧan ixalef adrar iṭṭ s labas n lemmayer; lqedd‑nnes, tiɣmmay yettilin din, leqdic n uturez ma yella, ... ɣrt.

Ma nejbed‑d awal ɣef wedrar n Celyet xaṭer netta d ameqṛan u yis‑s a tetwassen teɣmeṛt n Wawras. Adrar‑aya di tɣiwant n Buḥmama (Afraqsu), yus‑d d agmir jar n sent n lwilayat, Xencla d Batent. Lqedd‑nnes azal n 2828 m (yexf n Keltum), yetwaḥsab d wis sen di leɛla di tmurt n Dzayer wern n wedrar Tahṭatakur di tmurt n Imuhaɣ (itergiyyen). Celyet tif adrar n Jerjer s wazal n 8 n lmitrar daya.

Celyet tɛerrem lhul, neqqad n yebriden yeṣṣawwaḍen ɣer‑s; tɣawsa‑aya t‑yeǧǧin d lqibelt n ḥewwasen si lwilayat yyiḍ u s uɛerrem iseggasen‑aya tineggura. Seg imukan yetwasnen di‑s mliḥ: tizuggaɣin, yexfawen n waman, aman iberkanen, yexf n hella, Taɣit, Tḥemmamin, yelmaten, Tmectawin, Inuɣisen, Icc n wul (Lemdint), ... ɣrt.

Si tɣemmayin yellan di Celyet ad d‑naf taṣeṭṭa n yedgel; s mayes itwassen udrar‑aya neqqad. Yedgel yedrus deg umaḍal jemla, d taṣeṭṭa yebhan nezzeh, labas a di‑s n wanawen itwasnen s ulawi n teṣmeḍ (yeggam deg ujris), u iṭɛeṭṭal di tgemmayt‑nnes, yezmer ad d‑yawi ɛecrin n iseggasen bacana ad tali luheṛ n lmitra ɣef lḥedd n ucal. Ɣer‑s izunbayen, u ssi‑s nezmer ad d‑nekkes aselɣaɣ, akeccuḍ‑nnes yeqquṛ u yegsa, ɣef wayyi‑t labas n yimakaren t‑itebbin s tukeṛḍa u znuzuyen‑t s leɣla. Yella ssi‑sen daɣ wa t‑ittakren u ssi‑s xedmen tiṛba d tẓiwa.

Iseggisa‑aya tineggura yendur yedgel labas si ca n tkeččawt t‑isercayen seg yixef ald abuḍ u itteǧǧa taṣeṭṭa tbedd d aɣidud d awṛaɣ. Tɣaṛuṛt d lḥemman rninr fella‑s, yexḍa am zik segga yetɛerrim wedfel.

Celyet d idurar ukk d leɛmaṛt n tmurt‑nneɣ, afeyyi‑nsen d lexṣaṛt d taḥellaqt i yudan d dduban; times d useṛɣi n tẓegwa meḥsub yal anebdu d twaɣitt yellan ḥed ur d‑inejjem ad t‑iḥebbes kkes ma ukin‑d ayet bab n tmurt d inijiwen yettasen d iḥewwasen. Teṣeṭṭa ma teṛɣa yezemer laɛɛad ad tteɣmi, u ma teɣmi‑d ilaq‑as kem n iseggasen bac ad ttetna mamek a tella.

Aḥadi ɣef tezdeg n twennaṭ daɣ d temsalt irennin di thusi n tmurt. Amdaṛ n zebbalin deg ul n wedrar yetwaḥsab d anɣay n teẓgi d wa yettedren di‑s. Iɛeggalen n tdukliwin ilaq‑asen ad sseḥrcen leqdic n usezdeg d usemres deg imukan ani tɣiman yudan labas. Ad ssersen tiblakin n uwelleh, u ad xedmen tumliwin i leɛbad ad fehmen mamek ad ḥadan ɣef tgama d twennaṭṭ.

Aẓay n tṣeṭwin di yal tama d nfeɛ yeḥlan nezzeh bac timdinin d iqewwira ad bhan u ad qqimen d annar azdgan i ayet bab‑nnes. Azraɛ n tict n tṣeṭṭa ma hennid d tlalitt n ldufan ɣer dimmet, taɣemmayt‑nnes d tafeggunt i yal yict ssi‑neɣ.

Yunes Aɣugali.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021

# Ẓaṛ n Tirrugza

Ad ileɣ fell‑ak a yass

Wellahi ma iliɣ fell‑ak a yass

Ameṭṭi, azal‑nnes d imer

Imeṭṭi azal‑nnes d imer

Ad ileɣ aked ma …

Izellin, yeṭṭenḍen s tizzla

Imeṭṭi ɣer tirrugza

Yexf‑inu seg xemmem ɛeṛqint‑as

Ur yeɣzi tiregwa

Ɣer zzat nniɣ ɣer deffer ad yelfa

D tizellayin bla yagmir

Yecceqqeɣ walli, kfin‑t‑as

Ma bdant … ur ẓriɣ

Ɣer wulac ugellil ha‑t yersa

Ma kfant

Ḥlil i yiɣsan ay yizedɣen tafekka

D ticeqfin ɣer wemrir

Asirem a sessen ma yeqqur … yuqqa

Ḍelṣent d abuliɣ

Ḥlil i leɛmer‑inu bla ssas

Cukkeɣ ur tmirant

Yexs ad yermeg tumert deg ujenna

Ad ileɣ fell‑ak a yass

Ḥlil i temẓi‑inu ay yiqemḍen ccan

Imeṭṭi azal‑nnes d imer

Ma d imir‑a d iɣed, xsin urjan

Leɛmer yettuẓeṭṭ s ifulan

Aḥeq Rebbi, ad ileɣ fell‑ak a yass

Ẓdin s tezdeg n waman

Imeṭṭi azal‑nnes d imer

Tikwal s uqerriḥ ẓwan

Gemneɣ tesdukkuled yiḍ

Ẓlen abrid n wasennaṭ

Kullec iṛẓem‑awen ifassen ula d itran

Yers d ttimsiɣeṛt ɣer yimal

Ɣef lqern n ugur asɛif d tziri

Gara n teqṣiḍin n yiḍ msaman

Tebḍa‑m aɛekkaz

Igin tiwa ɣer tiwa … ḍeṣṣen

Tamettant …

Fella neč yennirfen

Islan …

Fella neč yeqṛuṛḥen

Taẓedya ɣer‑wen d asufir maci d alili

Fella neč yeṛwan

Ma nečč kerfeɣ, iṭṭaw kan thennan

Taḍṣa iwelmen s imeṭṭawen

S tbeɣjijt tṛajiɣ abeɣjij n lefjer ad d‑yali

Am was‑inu, am yiḍ‑inu … d iberkanen

Ad rewleɣ i tallast n inezgam

Ad ileɣ fella‑k a yass

Awelli ad ndacen deg ass ma yuli

Imeṭṭi azal‑nnes d imer

Ah! Neč matta ay‑tṛajan!

Ma necna twarẓmen‑aneɣ imejjan

Ah! Iẓag umedwal …

Sal ɣef ulawen ma sɛan iman

Seg umulli ɣer umulli

S tufra suffuɣen iḥulfan

Ah! Werɛad tala teteffi‑d d iɣeẓṛan

Ma nessuktu, ula d ajenna yetmeḍṛan

Fell‑ak ad ileɣ a yass

Kan abrirret ad ttesled sɣer wemdan

Aberrug azal‑nnes d imer

S tɣeṛḍin fell‑ak ad uɛan

Ay yetɛeddan cek a leɛmer … d asfel.

Yunes AƔUGALI.

# inkizfi ? MAIVCVO

Deg taggayt-agi ad tafem iḍrisen, d temsirin d umawal s tutlayt n tmacaqt “tatergit” sɣur uselmad AISSI Meḥfuḍ

# Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
tamT d awaqas

tamT iiat tamihaR, alwyan-tt iHanGa. trwal-asn abaraqa. tgraw awqas, idbal-tt ar tt-d-isiwaD Ror amzaR-nit. Adwin donat-nit, sastanan-tt, nan-as: ma kam d-iwin? tana-hasn: iwi-hi-d awaqas iian, iga–hi tolok anir orgiR imi-nit irkan.

Klad ibakt awqas, isla awa tna, iGla, okayan ihaDan wiiaD, ar ahl iian taka tamT isRaran tamhay d awaqas, ina-s: etkat asRar iian, awat-i, tana-s: kala, or kay GatR. Iga-hi awaqas iian n lxir, or sinaR kay miR iian haDan. Ina-s awaqas: nako. tana-has: or dobiR a kay wtaR, ina-s awaqas: awat-i miR akm kHaR, tatkal tamT asRar tawat-t, tasboyas-t, ina-has awaqas: dimardaR aGal.

Snatat talil miR kraDat dafir awin, imhay awaqas d tamT, ina-has awaqas: anhi edaG wa dR hi-tasboysad, iji miR kala? tana-has: iji. Ina-has awaqas: aboyis itaji tafirt n imi taHaDat or taji, sofaR tiwit n takoba i ils n tamT.

Risi maxfoD

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# dasin

dasin oalt hama, oaltma-s n axamok,

tadiw d als iian ism-nit afelan.

daR ahaGar war tali tamT iofan dasin.

tamT hagart, ti malat, RaGalat anDaran, odm-nit ihosay; tiTawin-nit tihosaynit, daZnit. Isinan-nit malolanin asaRnin, tawila-nit tahosayat.

tasan imZad holan, tla tayte taGit, drosnin midan wi lanin tayte hod dasin daR ahaGar miR war tali fo.

# tasoRalt s Ror Risi maxfoD

# tihosay n tamT

tihosay n tamT: ti RaGalat, tla eri hagarin, tla angor ihosayn ibdadn, tla anarn sTafnin sdidnin, tla tiTawin tihosaynin, sTafnin, maqornin. IDlay-nit war hohran war sdidn, tla isinan malolanin asaRnin, tla temaZayt. Isan n tayniwin-nit RaGalan, tegehe–nit sadid, tamT n geregere war hagarat war gazol, tla tawila tahosayt, iDaDwan sadidnin, tla tasna saloft, lamidat hond lahrir.

# tasoRalt s Ror Risi maxfoD

# Ismawan n imnas

- abhaw: chameau marron rougeatre.
- abroG: chameau grisonnat.
- abzaw: chameau blanchatre.
- adGnas, ebaidaG: chameau blanc.
- adyaw, talmt: un grand troupeau de chameau.
- aGosrar: chameau avec un dos et un cou blanc.
- ahaGar, ezGar: chameau avec poil rouge.
- ahamal: un troupeau de chameau mâles.
- Ajmilal: sorte de chameau ( ?)
- Akamhor: un bon chameau.
- alaway, amkalo, abaxol: chameau de charge.
- alGas: un chameau de deux a trois ans.
- alm n akabor: chameau qui court vits.
- alm, amis: chameau mâle.
- Almlar: chameau gris.
- amoGay: chameau de faible constitution.
- Arnanas: un chameau qui blatére souvent.
- Asfakas: chameau qui avance a longs pas.
- Aslraf: chameau noir et blanc.
- atGamtGm: chameau qui avance a petit pas.
- Atlar: un chameau de couleur acajou.
- Awinak: chameau avec un dos gris, flanc blancs autour de la bosse, les pattes et la queue.
- Awrar: chameau entre gris clair et marron clair.
- Azorzom: chameau avec des pattes arrières blanches.

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021

chameau moucheté.

# ebrhay

chameau entre le gris et le blanc.

# ebrim

chameau jaunâtre.

# edamdan

chameau couleur foncé au rouge avec un museau blanc.

# eGaDe

chameau brun clair.

# ekawl

chameau noir.

# emanGal,inGal

chameau gris foncé.

# enil

chameau gris foncé avec du blanc sur le ventre et les hautes des pattes.

# ezrif

chameau gris metallique.

# iiGan

chameau avec des pattes blanches.

# Imolsan

chameau avec museau blanc.

# Iwinarn

chameau avec des yeux bleuâtre.

# tarajawi

un chameau qui blatére au chargement.

# tarik, argan, targant

chameau de couleur.

# tazGa

un petit troupeau de chameau.

# Izem YUΓALEN D AΓYUL

Sγur : D.Messaoudi

Izem d agellid n yimudren,

Netta d win yeqwan, d win muhaben.

Aγyul d ungif gar yebhimen,

Fell‑as εebban, yes‑s kerzen.

Izem d ilelli deg udrar.

Aγyul d akli deg uzaγar.

Izem iγaḍ‑it meskin uγyul,

Deg‑s yezga yettweṣṣi seg wul:

Zeεbeḍ ! Neggez ! Ṣukk !

M’ulac ur ssaram ddel fell‑ak ifuk.

Aγyul yebra i yimejjugen‑is yeqqim,

Deg‑s bab‑is la ineğğeε, la yettdeqqim.

Ugar n 40 iseggasen d yizem yetteg ineẓman

Γef uγyul yeddren s tsusmi deg yir ussan.

Izem d bu yiseγ ur iqebblen ddel,

Maca ul‑is yettilqiq ma γer umedlul yemmuqel.

Akken ad iwanes aγyul umi meččen yizerfan,

Yedda γer win yeskaren iḥeddfan.

Deg teglimt n uγyul, izem yekcem s adaynin.

Aγyul yefreḥ: taεkemt ad tt‑ddmen deg sin.

D.Messaoudi

Amawal

imudren = animaux; ilelli = libre; ineẓman = soucis ; amedlul = soumis ; adaynin = étable ; iseγ = dignité

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# At yigenni

Deg wasmi tzedɣem igenni

Tekksem amḍiq i yitran

Asigna yuɣal d taduli

Yis‑s teɣbam iṭij n yirrezgan

Yid‑wen tewwim‑d cctawi

D asawen refden‑aɣ waman

Leεwanṣer ččuṛen d ahni

Ɣef wakal meqqin yiẓekwan.

Ccwal ɣur‑wen d icedhi

Tinufa deg‑s i tent‑tettaǧwem

Nnig‑nneɣ mi teṭṭfem kulci

I lmektub tbeddlem udem

Ẓẓur teǧǧam‑t i udari

Di leεnaya‑s tettidirem

Ternam azref d inigi

Win yekkren yis‑s ad t‑tɣeḍlem.

Tesgugmem ccna n tefsut

Yexsi usirem i d‑ilulen

D tasusamt teqqel tsekkurt

Tunef i yibẓiẓen cewwqen

# Yid‑wen tthuzzun tamurt

Deg unebdu uḍan ɣezzifen

Aɣmim yeɣli‑d am tagut

I icebbeḥ taweṣṣaft‑nwen !

Ul ma reglen‑t wurfan

S yimi ara frunt tilla

Ma tiɣri‑s tennebran

Ur tt‑teǧǧim ad tusu kra

Ḥṣut ihi d ayen kan

Ɣer ufus ad taweḍ tuḍna

Ur yewεiṛ uɣilas yeṛwan

I yewεeṛ umcic di tuqqna.

Ayen akk i deg tesrewtem

Yis‑s ara tεemrem aseksut

Deg wayen tessendayem

Deg‑s ara tseqqim taṛbut

Ama d tiẓeṭ, ama d tesmem

Qeblet‑tt tura d lqut

Ar melmi ara tfaqem

Asmi ara tenhez tmurt.

# Mi ak‑d‑iban ubrid

Teddu kan d uẓawali

Ḍleq‑as i yal lqid

Ḍfer abrid n tlelli

Iziḍ am zzbib

Meεna ur sqizzib

Ili‑k kan d lǧid

I win yellan d lxali

Ferren deg ujdid

Ddem kan deg‑s lεali

Tamussni‑k ad tzid

Ma telliḍ d usdid

Ur ttamen At‑lǧib

Tqudreḍ lejdud‑ik d tirni

D win ur k‑neεǧib

Yazid Werdi

Tasɣunt ASELMAD uṭṭun wis 8. Yennayer 2021
# Agumi

Aqli‑n am ṭṭir yufgen

Arṣaṣ yeddeqdiq,

Ur nesɛi afriwen

Sibil meskin yemḥa

D ɛamayen deg ttexmim,

Ixdeɛ Ɛmer u Yusef

Ccib i yilef

Asmi d‑nensa deg Menṣuren

Caḍen imucaṛen,

Yenna‑as: bibb Fransa,

Ɣef rrabɛa i sirklin,

Yessenz tamurt‑is

D agumi mi teṭṭfen i taddart‑nsen,

Yerna adewwar‑is

Isteɛmil ḥedd ur t‑yessin.

Ɣef tgamilt n ṣupa,

Ɣef tgamilt n ṣupa

Ayen! ay agumi

Mi txedmeḍ tigi

A yelli igujjlen

Ini‑aɣ‑id anwi i k‑isumḥen

Hder a gma s nniya‑k

Asmi i d‑iṣubb ar lbiru

Lmijal yeḍba‑k

Ihedder, ittru, ičča.

Ifuk ukessar d usawen,

Ifuk ukessar d usawen

Aṛublan, tuli‑d iɣẓer

Slimi ṢABRINA

# Amuḍin

Aqli am yinijel aquran

Aqli am yinijel aquran

Yekfa wafud iresres,

Ikfa wafud‑iw yeɛya,

Lehlak yezzi ɣef yixef‑inu

Lehlak izzi‑d ixef‑inu

Ur sɛiɣ ḥedd d amwanes

Ur sɛiɣ ḥedd ɣer tama

A Rebbi xdem‑iyi ttawil,

A Rebbi ili‑k d amwanes

Arfed tasumta, nuyes.

Efk‑aɣ‑id ddwa neɛya.

# Aẓekka

Wellah ur ugadeɣ leflas

Ma luẓeɣ, ad d‑aǧweɣ irden

Wellah ur ugadeɣ tirẓi

Ma rẓeɣ ad yi‑cudden,

I yugadeɣ d aẓekka

Imi ad ruḥen, ad yi‑ǧǧen.

Wellah ur ugadeɣ leflas

Ma luẓeɣ ad d‑aǧweɣ timẓin,

Wellah ur ugadeɣ tirẓi

Ma rẓeɣ ad yi‑cudden s tuflin,

A yugadeɣ d aẓekka

Mi ara d‑qqlent tmedlin.

Ay ixef‑iw, ixef n uzger

Ma ḥkiɣ‑ak leɣbayen, ad truḍ

Ufiɣ ɣazen aẓekka s ugelzim

Swan leḥyuḍ,

Ur sqizzib ur ḥeqqer

Ur ttawi seg wa ɣer wa

Awal, ixeddem lmenkeṛ

Ineǧǧer abrid i tlufa

Xas zzman tura yewεer

Ili‑k d imɣi n ṣṣaba

Di laṣel‑ik mger εemmer

D winna kan ay d lɣella

Win iran ad ak‑ixaṭer

Eǧǧ‑it, sefḍ lǧerra

Taqbaylit ay tesεa zzher

Ay ixef‑iw aɛzizen ad temteḍ

Ad k‑yečč wakal, ad terkuḍ.

Mi d‑uliɣ di tmeqbart,

Ar ttweḥḥideɣ Rebbi

Ufiɣ ɣazen aẓekka

Ur as‑ǧǧan iɣisi

Tarwiḥt ad tt‑refdent lmuluk

Ssura aɛzizen, tɣelli.

Mi d‑uliɣ di tmeqbert

La ttweḥḥideɣ axellaq

Ufiɣ ɣazen aẓekka

Ur as‑ǧǧan lfiraq

Tarwiḥt ad tt‑refdent lmuluk,

Izdeɣ‑it wul ur ixaq

ṢABRINA Slimi,

SARRIINA Sliui;,

Asefru n yemma.

Aselru 1 yewnua

Mi tt‑refden wat lḥerma

Tajmilt i tarwa n lḥar

Yerẓan asalu s tira

Idles‑nneɣ, yezger lebḥer

Tefka‑t taεwint i tala

D awezɣi! tura awexxer

Win yusmen yeṭṭef tama!

ɣas akka ɣezzif umecwar

Azekka‑s d tafrara

Ilaq ad nkemmel ad nezwaṛ

Ad neddu d yimezwura

# D tasuqilt n tezlit “chedda wetzoul n Yaḥya Tebbic d Sufiya Aya”

# A yemma ɛzizen

# ‑A yemma ɛzizen yemma

# I yelhan fell‑as yettwexxir

# Txussed‑iyi ass‑a

# ‑A yemma isem‑im d acebḥan

# Imi dayen ur d‑tettuɣaleḍ

# Di yal tamurt d azeddgan

# Anwa deg‑neɣ ur t‑id‑nebdir

# Di tumert neɣ di lmeḥna

# ‑Bedde

Tahuski i wumi ur ngi isem !

«Mi ɣriɣ walaɣ !»

Sɣur Ramdane ABDENBI

La ferrnen yimeskaren tiwsatin akked talɣiwin yemgaraden deg unnar n tsekla iwakken ad ssiwḍen i yimeɣriyen tidmi-nsen, tiktiwin-nsen, iḥulfan-nsen, tamuɣli-nsen akked yiwellihen-nsen. D wa i d iswi amezwaru, iswi agejdan n yal amaru.

Ma yebɣa usdawan ad yezrew aḍris aseklan, ma yebɣa uneɣmas ad yaru ɣef wayen i d-iẓergen d amaynut deg tsekla, ma yebɣa uselmad ad yesleḍ ungal, tullist neɣ asefru, anda ara afen wigi merra allalen d yisulal iwulmen i ccɣel-agi-nsen i bɣan ad t-id-heggin stmaziɣt ? D acu i ilaqen ad nadin fell-as deg uḍris aseklan iwakken ad d-inin «yelha» neɣ «diri-t» ? Amek ara t-id-inin ? D acu-ten wawalen i ilaq ad ten-sqedcen i waya ?

D taɣuri taḥerfit, d tasleḍt neɣ d tazrawt, d tutlayt i ilaqen ad tesɛu tizemmar ara sqedcen «yimeɣriyen-a» merra iwakken ad d-snesren seg yiḍrisen ayen akken bɣan ad t-id-inin yimura, ad t-id-arun, ad d-sfeṛzen ccbaḥa n tugniwin yuzzaren deg tefyirin, afiren akked wawalen iɣef bnan yimeskaren-a iḍrisen-nsen… mulac ttawilat deg tutlayt, d taḥkayt akked usentel iɣef ara yili wawal -yernu s tewzel- war ma rran lwelha-nsen ɣer uḥric ameqqran aseklan n yiḍrisen imi ur yelli wamek ara d-hedren fell-as… ulac awalen akked tenfaliyin… ulac win(wid) i ten-id-yesnulfan.

Ugur n yismawen deg tmaziɣt yuǧew-d asnulfu n wawalen imaynuten ur nelli ara deg tutlayt. Ma yugi neɣ ikukra umeskar ad ten-yesseqdec, yezmer ad ibeddel amyag, arbib… neɣ isem s taggayt n wawalen n yal ass ara fehmen yimeɣriyen, akken yezmer daɣen ad yeglem amdan, tigawt… neɣ taɣawsa ma ur as-yufi ara isem neɣ ahat yugi ad t(t)-id-yebder. Teḍḥa-d tarrayt-a n tira d yiwen seg wallalen yeggten i ucebbeḥ n tira deg tutlayin-nniḍen yecban tafransit.

Sin imedyaten-a mmalen-d azal akked unamek n wawalen iɣef yebna uḍris, tafyirt neɣ afir.

1. Yenna Cheikh Mohand Oulhoucine :
- Simmal nettaweḍ / Simmal mazal ad naweḍ / Imi aggaḍ / Ur t-yettaweḍ ḥedd.
2. Yenna Cheikh Mohand Ouali i Cheikh Mohand Oulhoucine :
- Ruḥ ay aderwic n at Yeḥya / Rriɣ-k d lmeṣbaḥ n tmura / D tasarut n tewwura.

Deg umedya amezwaru, allus n wawal «simmal» deg tazwara n wafir qqaren-as «amsales deg tazwara» s tmaziɣt neɣ «anaphore» s tefransit.

Deg umedya win sin, yuɣal «uderwic» d «lmeṣbaḥ», d «tasarut» ; amdan yuɣal d taɣawsa akken yezmer ad yuɣal d aɣersiw, qqaren-as s tefransit «réification», ma s tmaziɣt...

Amek ara nsemmi i tefyar (tinfaliyin) yecban tigi : «Yennɣel-d ṭṭlam fell-as seg tafat yedlen wiyaḍ» (=yusem). «Yeǧǧa-d ilem deg uxxam» (=yemmut). «Teṭṭef-it tannumi n ɛawaz» (=yuki). «Tɛedda-d tnafa tewwi-t» (=yeṭṭes). «Tesberber fell-as tatut» (=yettu). «Iɣeẓẓa iles-is» (=yemmut). «Yeɣli-d ṭṭlam deg uzal», «Yenɣa-yi laẓ», «Tiɣri n tsusmi», «Yuli d
asawen»,  «La yettseyyix wul-iw»,  «Iɣil n lkettan / Iɣil Ufella / Iɣil n jeddi»,  «a tiẓedt tamezrẓagut» !...

Ɣef waya i ilaq ad ad yers yisem ɣef tekti, ɣef tɣawsa, ɣef uneḍruy… ɣef thuski, mulac ad yuɣal uḍris aseklan d amgrad aɣamsan. Ilaq ad d‑yini umeɣri di taggara : «mi ɣriɣ walaɣ» ayen i yebɣa ad t‑id‑yini umeskar. Iban‑d gar wallen‑iw amzun din i lliɣ.

# Tiɣbula :

- Abdesselam Abdennour, Categories du vocabulaire de langue berbère, avril 1999.
- Abdesselam Abdennour, Cheikh Mohand Oulhoucine Amoussnaw ou la renaissance de la pensée kabyle, avril 2005.
- Bouamara Kamal, Amawal n tunuɣin n tesnukyest, HCA, 2007.
- Bouamara Kamal, Issin, asegzawal n teqbaylit s teqbaylit, Editions l’Odysée, 2010.
- Mammeri Mouloud, Poèmes Kabyles anciens, Editions Mehdi, Algérie, 2009.
- Mammeri Mouloud, Inna-yas Ccix Muhend (Cheikh Mohand a dit), 1990.
- Meksem Zahir, Tisekkiwin n yiḍrisen, HCA, 2010.
- Salhi Mohand Akli, Asegzawal ameẓẓyan n tsekla, Editions l’Odysée, 2012.
- Salhi Mohand Akli, Kra n tsura i tɣuri n tsekla, Editions Tira, aḥric 1, 2015.
- Salhi Mohand Akli, Kra n tsura i tɣuri n tsekla, Editions Tira, aḥric 2, 2015.
# Kra n tefyirin n tmaziγt tatrart yegdazalen tiden n tefṛansist

Sγer: D.Messaoudi

Ur yezmir yiwen ad yenkeṛ dakken tamaziγt xuṣṣent-tt kra n tefyar swayes imatlayen imaziγen zemren ad d-ssenfalin kra n tektiwin. Γef waya ad ten-tafeḍ sseqdacen srid tifyirin taεrabin neγ tifṛansisin, ayen yeğğan tamaziγt ur iban d acu-tt tikkwal.

Amagrad-a ur yemmid ara; nekk reẓmeγ yes-s tiwwura n unadi deg taγult-a; a win yafen ad ilin wiyaḍ ara t-yekemmlen s telqayt, neγ xerṣum ara t-yesneqden i tfayda-nneγ akkit.

# 1. « Quelque soit »

Agdazal n tefyirt-a deg tmaziγt d “bγu (urmir)+ili (urmir)”.

Imedyaten:

- Ayen tebγuḍ tiniḍ-as-t, ur ak yesmusgut ara. (quelque soit ce que tu lui dis, il ne t’écoutera pas)
- Akk-n tebγu tili tezmert-is, ur k-yrennu ara. (quelque soit sa puissance, il ne te vaincra pas)

# 2. « à chaque fois que »

Llan sin n yigdazalen i tefyirt-a : “yal mi ara” ed “yal tikkelt ara”.

Imedyaten:

- Yal m’ara tečč aksum, ad d-terr. (à chaque fois qu’elle mange de la viande, elle vomit)
- Yal tikkelt ara yessew, ad yennaγ yid-neγ. (à chaque fois qu’il boit, il se dispute avec nous)

# 3. « en tous les cas »

Tafyirt-a ur tt-ufiγ deg tentaliwin deg nudaγ, maca ufiγ awalen “tajṛut” ed “awan” (cas) deg yimawalen ay d-bedreγ swadda deg wedriraw.

Amedya :

- Deg tijṛa akk, ur qebleγ asumer-ik. (en tous les cas, je n’accepte pas ta proposition)

# 4. « au cas où »

Deg teqbaylit, tella yiwet n tefyirt yegdazalen ta n tefṛansist ; d “madegyella i”.

Amedya :

- Madegyella teḥwağeḍ tallalt, aql-i da. (au cas où tu auras besoin d’aide, je suis là)

# 5. « en cas de besoin »

Tafyirt-a ad tt-kkalkiγ γef tefyirt taεrabt ay tt-yqublen ii.

Amedya:

- Deg wakud n wassar, siwel-iyi-d. (en cas de besoin, appelle-moi)

# 6. « contrairement à »

Tafyirt-a yba wegdazal-is deg tentaliwin timaziγin ay ssneγ; ta swadda ihi d asumer.

Amedya:

- Mgali γef wayen yettwannan, … (contrairement à ce qui se dit, …)

# 7. « de plus en plus »
Deg tillawt, tikti-a tettwasenfali-d s tmaziγt s useqdec n wawal “simmal” ed wurmir ussid. I lmend n wawal, ad tiniḍ “simmal gemmun isekla-a” (ces arbres poussent de plus en plus). Maca, nezmer ad nesnulfu tafyirt niḍen s ukkalki γef tutlayin tibeṛṛaniyin am tneglizit, tafṛansist neγ taεrabt.

Amedya:

- Gemmun isekla-a ugar d wugar.

# « par contre »</h8>
Agdazal n tefyirt-a deg tmaziγt n Yiqbayliyen d “wamma”.

Amedya:

- Asenduq-a meẓẓi, wamma win-a meqqer. (Ce coffre est petit, par contre celui-là est grand)

# « plus … que »</h9>
Llant snat n tefyirin timaziγin yegdazalen ta n tefṛansist; ḥṣut dakken tanfalit-a tqebbel kan arbib ed umyag n waddud.

Imedyaten:

- Yidir ẓẓay γef Muḥend s sin n yiḥricen. (Yidir est deux fois plus lourd que Mohand)
- Nekk qwiγ fell-ak s waṭas. (je suis beaucoup plus fort que toi)

# « plus de … que »</h10>
Tella deg tmaziγt tefyirt yegdazalen ta n tefṛansist.

Amedya:

- Llan ugar n medden γer-i γef γer-k. (il y a plus de gens chez moi que chez toi)

# « moins de … que »</h11>
Nezmer ad nesseqdec awal amaynu “nkiẓ iii” i usenfali n tefyirt-a tafṛansist.

Amedya:

- Llant nkiẓ n tlawin γer-neγ γef γer-wen. (il y a moins de femmes chez nous que chez vous)

# « ne pas encore »</h12>
Deg teqbaylit, nesseqdac urḍil “mazal”. Maca deg tumẓabt tella tefyirt “zeddiγ wer”, ma deg tmaziγt n Murakuc alemmas tella “sul ur”.

Imedyaten:

- Mazal d-tusi yemma seg tala. (ma mère n’est pas encore arrivée de la fontaine)
- Yell-is zeddiγ wer tebliγ. (sa fille n’est pas encore mûre)
- Isul ur d-yewwiḍ. (il n’est pas encore arrivé)

# « avant que »</h13>
Deg teqbaylit, yella wegdazal n tefyirt-a; netta d awal uddis.

Amedya:

- Werεad yessuli taẓallit, yemmut. (avant qu’il finisse sa prière, il meurt)

# « à propos de / en ce qui concerne / en ce qui a rapport à»</h14>
Llant kra n tefyirin tiqburin s wawalen urḍilen; llant tiyaḍ d tatrarin.

Imedyaten:

- Γef temsalt n Yidir, nezmer … (à propos de Yidir, on peut …)
- Γef wayen yeqqnen γer wemxillef gar … (en ce qui a rapport au différent entre …)

# « depuis que »</h15>
Llant snat n tefyirin yemgarrden acemma kan deg unamek.
# Imedyaten:

- Segmi d-tuweḍ nettat ur tessusem. (elle n’arrête pas de parler depuis qu’elle est arrivée)
- Segwasmi d-tlul, nettat d tamuḍint. (elle est malade depuis le jour où elle est née)

# 16. « au moins / tout au moins »

Llan kraḍ n yirman swayes nezmer ad d-nessenfali tifyirin-a n tefṛansist.

# Imedyaten:

- Ssew axxi yiwen wakus n uyefki. (bois au moins un verre de lait)
- Ečč xerṣum iniγem uqbel ad tiniqeḍ. (mange au moins une figue avant de partir)
- Siwel-as meqqar s utilifun ma ur rezzfeḍ γer-s. (téléphone-lui tout au moins, si tu ne le visiteras pas)

Deg tillawt, awal-a yettwanṭaq akk-a : /madagella/, maca iban dakken yekka-d seg “ma+deg+yella”.

# 1 S taεrabt qqaren « في وقت الحاجة »

# 1 Awal “nkiẓ” ssuddmeγ-t-id seg urbib “unkiẓ” (amoindri) d-yekkan seg umyag “nkeẓ” (diminuer) ; am deg “deffir / ḍfer”.

# Amsadaɣ, d anaw gar wanawen n Tesnukyest.

D tugna i d-yettbanen deg talɣa n wawal akked tefyirt.

D amagrad sɣur Belɛidi Lyes

S lmenddad n uselmad n tesdawit : Muḥend Akli SALḤI

# Aɣawas

# Asenked.

# 1- Amsadaɣ alɣawan di talɣa n wawalen.

# 1-1-Amsadaɣ ummid.

# 1-2-Amsadaɣ aɣezfan.

# 1-3-Amsadaɣ awezlan.

# 2‑ Amsadaɣ aseddasan.

# 3‑ Amsadaɣ n usalaɣ (tussnalɣa).

Amawal.

Tiɣbula.

# Asenked :

Lekyasa n usekcem n tugniwin akked tunuɣin neɣ awalen akked tenfaliyin ara yernun ccbaḥa i uɣanib n uḍris aseklan. Ay agi yekcem gar yiferdis n tesnukyist³², d nutenti i yettakken azuɣer i yimeɣri neɣ win isellen ticki ara tili d timawit. Ddeqs i yellan, gar-asent ad naf amsadaɣ.

Amsadaɣ, d tugna n uɣanib i yeɛnan talɣa n wawalen. Deg tefyar n uḍris n tesrit neɣ deg yiwen n wafir n usefru nettaf awalen mgadan neɣ ttemcabin di tira akked ususru meɛna mgaraden deg unamek. Yezmer ad yili di talɣa n wawalen, taseddast n tefyar, taɣessa n tseddart, taɣessa n wafir… Ittusemma d iferdisen imqaraben aṭas di talɣa akked lmenṭeq. Llan ddeqs n wanawen igejdanen n umsadaɣ alɣawan, gar-asen :

# 1- Amsadaɣ di talɣa n wawalen :

Dagi amgada yettban-d deg wamek uran wawalen. Awalen ttemcabin deg yisekkilen. Yesɛa krad n tewsatin.

# 1-1- Amsadaɣ ummid.

Dagi ad naf tuɣal-d akk talɣa n wawal-nni ur ixus ula d asekkil.

- Imi di tili i telliḍ, tili fiḥel ma ccqiɣ-d iman-iw.
- Tili (amalu, ur yekcim yiṭij) / tili (limer)
- Issens inebgi, issens fell-as tafat !
- Issens (yeṭṭes) / issens (isexsi)
- Yak tḥemmleḍ ddreɛ, aha ihi err-as ddreɛ i tewwurt.
- ddreɛ (taɣennant, zzkara) / ddreɛ (azekkṛun)
- Iɣil yesεa iɣil, netta ṭṭfen-as-d tiɣilt
- iɣil (yeǧɛel) / iɣil (lǧehd)
- yewweḍ d wass ideg ara teddu d tislit yeffeɣ-as-d ṣṣer, bɛek ṣṣer-aɣ ay agsim.

32 Tasnukyest deg-s 05 yiḥricen : l’inventio (invention), dispositio (disposition), elocution (élocution), action (diction) et memoria (procédés pour mémorisation de discours.
# ṣṣer (d lehlak n yicenfiren) / ṣṣer (ffer taluft)

# Laɛmer i t‑yeǧǧa laɛmer³³

Yeɛmer di ccib‑is iban

# Laɛmer (lmuḥal) / laɛmer (acḥal n yiseggasen di tudert)

1. Amsadaɣ aɣezfan. Deg tewsit‑agi xuṣen kra n yisekkilen.
2. D ilemẓi yeksa timura, yettnadi ɣef tsura ara yeldin tiwwura. (Timura tiwwura)
3. Mazal ad aruɣ fell‑am³⁴
4. Mazal ad ruɣ fell‑am (ad aruɣ / ad ruɣ)
5. Ur as‑d‑ittserriḥ uzekka, ma d aẓekka i t‑ijemɛen tawwurt‑is tsekcam ur tessuffuɣ. (Azekka / aẓekka)
6. Tin yebɣan ad tawi amur, seksu deg uxxam‑is ad ifur. (Amur ifur)
7. Siwleɣ i uɣrib yenfan, ad iyi‑d‑tsel tmurt i t‑yeḍfan, ad t‑id‑terr. (Yenfan / yeḍfan)
8. Netta inumen tudert n yigelliden, ur yelli di lbal‑is belli tamurt i tt‑izedɣen d igellilen. (yigelliden / igellilen)
9. Degger ɣer tejmal yekfan³⁵ neɣ ḍegger tijmal di ccehwat neggar (degger / ḍegger / neggar)
10. Rrmel aqejmur deg uẓekka³⁶ Rruḥ d uzekka ad iruḥ Iman ad d‑yeggri aka (Azekka / aẓekka) (Rruḥ / iruḥ)
11. Kemm d azekka n tefsut³⁷ Nekka d aẓekka d lmut (Azekka / aẓekka)
12. Ttxemmimeɣ asma ara mmteɣ³⁸ Rruḥ anda ara iruḥ? (iruḥ / Rruḥ)
