# Amsadaɣ awezlan

Dagi ad naf kan tuɣalin n kra n yisekkilen. Alama yekcem ccek ahat mačči d awalen imgadan.

- Iruḥ ad isexsi times, terwel‑as tixsi i umeksa! (isexsi / tixsi)
- Bururu yekkat tajewwaqt ɣef yiɣerban iɣeḍlen. (yiɣerban / iɣeḍlen)
- Bu ugennur atabani annect n ugaɛmir. (ugennur / ugaɛmir)‑(Ugennur / uqenddur)
- D tabaḥant, d tamelḥant, d tacebḥant (tacebḥant / tamelḥant / tabaḥant)
- Ad am‑yekkes ṭṭiq ɣef wul‑im ³⁹
- ɣef wul‑iw ad yekkes lxiq
- ṭṭiq‑iw akked lxiq‑im (ṭṭiq / lxiq)
- Gguniɣ tasusmi ad as‑sleɣ⁴⁰
- susmeɣ iḍ, segneɣ iḍes (susmeɣ iḍ / segneɣ iḍes)
- Ma d uẓum⁴¹
- ɣef uksum
- ɣunzeɣ tufẓa n umdan (uẓum / uksum)

Deg umedya-agi ad naf akk tugniwin n umsadaɣ alɣawan n wawal.

« Nfaq⁴² mi zrin wussan, nfaq ur yelhi, d lebɣi‑nneɣ ur yelḥi, qublen‑aɣ‑d wuḍan ideg yeksdeb lemri‑nneɣ »

|Amsadaɣ ummid|Amsadaɣ aɣezfan|Amsadaɣ awezlan|
|---|---|---|
|Nfaq / nfaq|ur yelḥi / ur yelhi|lebɣi‑nneɣ / lemri‑nneɣ|
|wussan / wuḍan| | |

# Amsadaɣ aseddasan

Dagi d amgada ara naf deg talɣa n tefyar akked tenfaliyin. Yeɛna amseḍfer n wawalen.

- Biḥuc ad ak‑yečč, /Akluzal ad ak‑yawi. (Isem + ad n wurmir + amqim awṣil+ amyag)/ (Isem + ad n wurmir + amqim awṣil+ amyag)
- Ad ččen tagella yeḥman,/
- ad taccar tɛebbuḍt yexwan (Amyag + Isem+ amyag amaɣun / (Amyag + Isem+ amyag amaɣun)
- Yekkes ayla,/ yeddem afḍis,/ yerẓa ikufan d yicbula, /yekkes sser ɣef tuddar ... (Amyag + asemmad usrid) / (Amyag + asemmad usrid) / (Amyag + asemmad usrid …)
- Yexnunes lbext‑iw,/ yenfeḍ ssqef‑iw, / teɣli tgemmi‑iw, /texsi tafat‑iw… A nnaɣ !

42 Nfaq : d tanekkra n Ccix Aheddad akked Lmeqqrani (tanekkra n leqwabyel)
(Amyag + asemmad imsegzi + amqim awṣil) / (Amyag + asemmad imsegzi attwaɣ + amqim awṣil)

‑ Axxam yettṣeffir, tasilt ur tuli,/ seksu ur yerdim.

(Isem asentel + tazelɣa n tibawt+ amyag ar yizri) / (Isem asentel+ tazelɣa n tibawt+ amyag ar yizri)

‑ Nedda d waman ⁴³

neffeɣ iberdan

neggan ussan

nɛawez uḍan

amyag +asemmad usrid isem asget

# 3- Amsadaɣ n usalaɣ (tussnalɣa) :

‑ Igrawliwen ttaẓẓen ur ttwexxiren, teddun ur ttuɣalen. Ur beqqun ad neḥcamen.

(teddun / beqqun) C₁EC₂C₂UC₃ / C₁EC₂C₂UC₃

‑ Ad ččen tagella yeḥman, taɛebbuḍt yexwan ad taccar

(yeḥman / yexwan) yEC₁C₂An / yEC₁C₂An

‑ Ula d nettat ur tt‑yezgil. Teknef, tegdez.

Teknef / tegdez. TEC₁C₂EC₃ / TEC₁C₂EC₃

‑ Ḍefren tiqeddacin, yewwin ticekkarin yeččuren.

(Tiqeddacin / ticekkarin). tIC₁EC₂C₂AC₃In / tIC₁EC₂C₂AC₃In

‑ Ma yella d uḥdiq neffer‑it

Abrid wayeḍ ad iqatel

Ma yella d ungif nemmel‑it

ad fell‑as ṣewwbeɣ lmaqel (yusef uqasi) .   (uḥdiq / ungif).  UC₁C₂IC3

* ungif /uhdiq: si tama n talɣa d amsadaɣ, sεan di sin yiwet n talɣa  UC1C2IC3 , si tama n unamek d inemgalen.

# TWSSNA:

Sɣur: Azzedine Abdous

Tansaẓwant d tazrawt tussnant n uẓawan, tessiliɣ‑d taɣult n tussniwin talsanin.

Anegmay i iderwen neɣ yekkin deg tezrawt‑a d asnaẓwan (Musicologue), tanekta n wawal‑a "Tasnaẓwant /Musicologie) tefruri‑d ɣer Yigrikiyen, i Iran ad d‑ yinin d akken d awal uddis (composé).

[Mousikē}(« Musique / Aẓawan) akked [Logos}(«tazrawt, tamussni/Tussna/ Étude, connaissance). Awal‑a ad d‑yesbadu: Tussna n uẓawan.

Seg tasut tis 19, Tasnaẓwant tella tebḍa ɣef snat n taɣulin Tigejdanin, (Tasnaẓwant tanmezrayt (musicologie historique) akked d tesnaẓwant tanagrawt (musicologie systématique). Ihi aseylel ‑a (subdivision) neɣ beṭṭu ‑a yella‑d usenseb‑ines deg yiwen umagrad n Usnaẓwan (Musicologue), aprufisur, anemsawi (Autrichien) ”#Guido_Adler " «Etendue, méthode et buts de la musicologie), anda i d‑yessumer ahil amedran (fondateur) n tesnaẓwant deg useggas 1885.

Deg tasut tis 20, asnaẓwan G.Adler yefka‑d umuɣ n tegriwin timaruzin (Disciplines annexes) neɣ tussniwin timallalin (sciences auxiliaires) gar‑asent:

1‑Tasnaẓwant tanmezrayt: d tin i izerwen ilmend:1‑1‑Amezruy amatu1‑2‑Tasemɣezt tanaẓwant (Paléographie musicale)1‑3‑Tazrakud (Chronologie)1‑4‑Tagerdast (Diplômatique)1‑5‑Adlismuɣ (Bibliographie)1‑6‑Adlisdemsan (Bibliothéconomie)1‑7‑tella daɣen:Tasukit(Archivistique):deg‑s ad naf:a‑Amezruy aseklan, amutlay (Histoire littéraire et linguistique)b‑Amezruy n unezwu n tesreḍt (histoire de la liturgie)c‑Amezruy n umezgun asusam d ccḍeḥ (Le mime et la danse)d‑Timeddurin n yimaẓwanen (biographies des musiciens), imezgiyen (Stastiques), tidukkliwin (Associations), tisinagin/ tisudawin (institutions) d tnabazin timaẓwanin (Exécutions musicales).
2‑ Tasnaẓwant Tanagrawt; tzerrew ayen akk yellan d inagrawen n tsutant (acoustique)

2‑1‑ Tussnakt (Mathématique)2‑2‑Tasnimant (Psychologie)2‑3‑Armas n leṣwat (Perception du son)2‑4‑Tasengama (Physiologie); d tin i yeskanayen neɣ yesbaduyen ssut2‑5‑ Iferdisen n leṣwat (éléments du son)2‑6‑Tidmi Tanaẓwant (pensée musicale): d tin i yesɛan; ‑ Tajerrumt, tamedyezt, tasengmit d ccbaḥa (Grammaire. Poésie, pédagogique et esthétique...).
Deg tasut tis 21, Tanaẓwant tekkes‑d beṭṭu n kraḍ n tguriwin Tigejdanin;

‑Tasnaẓwant tanmezrayt.

‑Tiẓri d tesleḍt tanaẓwant (théorie et l'analyse musicales), akked d teslaẓwant 7 (ethnomusicologie)
# Asentel w ukayad akked useyti-imes

# Sɣur Zuhra Laɣa

# Ameḥbus

Ḥekkun‑d di Junim neɣ Tapalque, taqṣit n yiwen n uqcic, iruḥ mi d‑ẓedmen Ihendiyen. Qqaren‑d d ihendiyen ay t‑yukren. Imawlan‑is, nudan fell‑as acḥal ur t‑ufin ara. Ɛeddan iseggasen, ha‑t‑an yusa‑d yiwen n uɛsekri, iḥka‑asen‑d ɣef yiwen n uhendi, allen‑is d tizegzawin am yigenni. Yezmer ad yili d netta i d mmi‑tsen. Uɣalen mlalent (...) Ɣilen ɛeqqlen‑t. Argaz, yuɣ tanummi d Sseḥra d lexla, yettu ula d tameslayt n yimawlan‑is, d acu kan yeqbel yeddad s axxam.

Yewweḍ‑d kan ɣer umnar n tewwurt n berra, ibedd; yezmer lḥal imi bedden wid‑nni nniḍen. Imuqel tawwurt amzun akken ur tt‑yeɛqil ara. Tallit kan akka, isers aqerru‑is yuẓẓaf, iberrez s axxam, ur yeẓri amek yegga ubrid. Yekcem s axxam, yerra srid ɣer tḍellaɛt‑nni iɛelqen di lḥiḍ. Imekken afus‑is, yekkes‑d tajenwit‑nni bu tfettust n yiqci i yeffer asmi yella d agrud. Allen‑is tberriqent si lferḥ. Imawlan‑is ttrun imi d‑ufan mmi‑tsen.

Izmer lḥal macci ala ay‑a ay d‑imekta. D acu kan ahendi amcum, yegguma ad yidir gar rebɛa 04 n leḥyuḍ. Yiwen n wass yekker ad inadi ɣef tmurt‑is...

Jorge Luis Borges, 1960, El Hacedor.

# Tasuqilt ɣer teqbaylit sɣur Boukherrouf Remdhan

# I - Tigzi n uḍris : ( 6/6)

1. D anwa yukren aqcic‑agi?
2. D acu i ixdem uqcic mi yekcem s axxam?
3. Af‑d deg uḍris anemgal n wawal “ittu ”.
4. Anallas deg uḍris‑agi, d agensay neɣ d azɣaray?
5. Suffeɣ‑d seg uḍris sin n yimedyaten i t‑id‑yemmalen.

# II- Iferdisen n tutlayt : ( 6/6)

1. Ini‑d d acu‑tt twuri n wawal yettuderren deg uḍris
2. Suffeɣ‑d deg uḍris :

# III- Asenfali s tira :

Sugen‑d tudert n uqcic‑a i yukren Ihenddiyen, mi d‑yuɣal s axxam‑nsen.
# Aseɣt n usental wis krad : (03)

# Isestanen

# Aseɣti

# Tazmilt

I tigzi n uḍris 06/06

1. D ihendiyen, ay t-yukren.
2. Mi yekcem uqcic s axxam, yerra srid ɣer tḍellaɛt-nni iɛelqen di lḥiḍ. Imekken afus-is, yekkes-d tajenwit-nni bu tfettust n yiqci i yeffer asmi yella d agrud.
3. Anemgal n wawal : yettu : imekta-d. Anallas deg uḍris-agi : D azɣaray Sin n yimedyaten i t-id-yemmalen :
- Imyagen fetin ɣer kraḍ: yeẓra, yusa, iruḥ...
- Amatar udmawan, ad yili d( i, y): ibedd, yettu...
- Imqimen iwsilen : gar-as, baba-s, yenna-as...

# Iferdisen n tutlayt

06/06

1. Talɣa d twuri n wawal-a “argaz” deg tefyirt : “Argaz, yuɣ tanummi d Sseḥra d lexla” Talɣa : d isem asuf, amalay deg waddad ilelli. Tawuri : d anemmal n usentel.
2. Asuffeɣ-d deg uḍris : Aseɣru umyig : Yekcem s axxam. Aseɣru arumyig : Argaz, yuɣ tanummi d Sseḥra d lexla.

# Tira

08/08

# Talɣa n uḍris:

- Azwel
- Aḍris yebḍa d tisddarin.
- Asexdem n yimezdiyen.
- Ilem gar tseddarin.
- Askil ameqqran.
- Asigez iwatan.
- Imyagen ftin ɣer tmezrit ilaqen.
- Ma ur iffiɣ ara i wesntal.
- Ugulen (tucḍiwin) n tira, asmres n wawalen n tmaziɣt.
adagella/, maca iban dakken yekka-d seg “ma+deg+yella”.
